# Readwise | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_656b06cb7d)

[](#h_3ace794400)

[](#h_b561779316)

[](#h_c61185b405)

[All Collections](/en/)

[Plugins](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820559-plugins)

Readwise

Get the most out of what you read.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 8 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_656b06cb7d)

[](#h_3ace794400)

[](#h_b561779316)

[](#h_c61185b405)

Connecting Readwise to TRMNL takes just a few seconds and does not require any coding.

**Step 1 - Visit the Readwise plugin**
--------------------------------------

Inside TRMNL, navigate to Plugins > Readwise.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1158645682/692f380f978db8db458d93ad/trmnl-readwise-plugin.png?expires=1743477300&signature=d886ab0d9a96bf60802bbe403bd2c670e652a5441098e3ef1e2b8eb02fe620f4&req=dSEiHs96mIdXW%2FMW1HO4zTRd2ynFh%2Flj1Vm065RRaPxXCi624Wx3oaRTZpI7%0AkBDU5pNQxKo1Xx6W3dw%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1158645682/692f380f978db8db458d93ad/trmnl-readwise-plugin.png?expires=1743477300&signature=d886ab0d9a96bf60802bbe403bd2c670e652a5441098e3ef1e2b8eb02fe620f4&req=dSEiHs96mIdXW%2FMW1HO4zTRd2ynFh%2Flj1Vm065RRaPxXCi624Wx3oaRTZpI7%0AkBDU5pNQxKo1Xx6W3dw%3D%0A)

**Step 2 - Connect Readwise**
-----------------------------

Inside Readwise, navigate to [Access Tokens](https://readwise.io/access_token)
.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1158647344/d664af508a91e08ee5b20f4a/readwise-create-access-token.png?expires=1743477300&signature=0d4ba9abb1b4edf897304865294ca29c019047bf6968ae0ea8c18332f598f37e&req=dSEiHs96moJbXfMW1HO4zUkOH1QihIxteUt0SoT02H%2BKJNdXxMRuK261905E%0AI%2Bi2e6Nsup4DBUWGbac%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1158647344/d664af508a91e08ee5b20f4a/readwise-create-access-token.png?expires=1743477300&signature=0d4ba9abb1b4edf897304865294ca29c019047bf6968ae0ea8c18332f598f37e&req=dSEiHs96moJbXfMW1HO4zUkOH1QihIxteUt0SoT02H%2BKJNdXxMRuK261905E%0AI%2Bi2e6Nsup4DBUWGbac%3D%0A)

Click "Get Access Token" (or copy an existing one, if available) and you'll be presented a long string of characters.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1158648328/3f52970c522ddf141915125e/readwise-api-access-token-example.png?expires=1743477300&signature=4ac9be38be207064583829acecf2583c210aed64086280f086a25364ef55ab25&req=dSEiHs96lYJdUfMW1HO4zVljTec%2B0m%2FIeJ5P9%2FlpNKPonpiTJYgOQGGUeHZZ%0AniWsqCx1lHPbGLyBtEk%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1158648328/3f52970c522ddf141915125e/readwise-api-access-token-example.png?expires=1743477300&signature=4ac9be38be207064583829acecf2583c210aed64086280f086a25364ef55ab25&req=dSEiHs96lYJdUfMW1HO4zVljTec%2B0m%2FIeJ5P9%2FlpNKPonpiTJYgOQGGUeHZZ%0AniWsqCx1lHPbGLyBtEk%3D%0A)

Copy this to your clipboard.

Step 3 - Configure Plugin
-------------------------

Back inside TRMNL, paste this value in the configuration form and (optionally) give this plugin a name. Click Save.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1158651876/6bb6def2cb08c26bf7414e8b/trmnl-readwise-configuration.png?expires=1743477300&signature=7bf2f440a74604802a60891de147fe8e446870b892fc911b7fee97894729d959&req=dSEiHs97nIlYX%2FMW1HO4zY9zDZ%2BbkGI72UNlruvg4ZaZ%2FrFQBYWj0LDJbBj4%0AgZfaOoVooIQDtg4QVWk%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1158651876/6bb6def2cb08c26bf7414e8b/trmnl-readwise-configuration.png?expires=1743477300&signature=7bf2f440a74604802a60891de147fe8e446870b892fc911b7fee97894729d959&req=dSEiHs97nIlYX%2FMW1HO4zY9zDZ%2BbkGI72UNlruvg4ZaZ%2FrFQBYWj0LDJbBj4%0AgZfaOoVooIQDtg4QVWk%3D%0A)

**Step 4 - You're Done!**
-------------------------

Based on your desired refresh settings, TRMNL will begin showcasing useful highlights from your Readwise account very soon.

Stay focused.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

# Robinhood | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_02619a5f21)

[](#h_b864ef919d)

[](#h_e520220fa0)

[](#h_16d75d0d9a)

[](#h_77b0fd611d)

[All Collections](/en/)

[Plugins](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820559-plugins)

Robinhood

Monitor your portfolio performance over time.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 10 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_02619a5f21)

[](#h_b864ef919d)

[](#h_e520220fa0)

[](#h_16d75d0d9a)

[](#h_77b0fd611d)

Connecting your Robinhood account to TRMNL takes just a few seconds and is done securely via our OAuth2 integration with Plaid, a leading financial institution connector.

**Step 1 - Visit the Robinhood Plugin**
---------------------------------------

Inside TRMNL, navigate to Plugins > Robinhood.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1098149177/c5cb0bdc074ad66c43114940/trmnl-robinhood-plugin.png?expires=1743477300&signature=2a4fe8a62f2060e73c2b131ca685de7c4dde3cdec52e784b53e497e938af780b&req=dSAuHsh6lIBYXvMW1HO4zaFYg810ENpgiKIGevT869mxczQi8wvERQp4PXdG%0Ag67hq6Hs1jQZMP7eNf0%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1098149177/c5cb0bdc074ad66c43114940/trmnl-robinhood-plugin.png?expires=1743477300&signature=2a4fe8a62f2060e73c2b131ca685de7c4dde3cdec52e784b53e497e938af780b&req=dSAuHsh6lIBYXvMW1HO4zaFYg810ENpgiKIGevT869mxczQi8wvERQp4PXdG%0Ag67hq6Hs1jQZMP7eNf0%3D%0A)

**Step 2 - Connect Robinhood**
------------------------------

Click to "Connect with Robinhood" on the right side of the screen, then click the Robinhood logo and follow the prompts to approve access to TRMNL.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1098134522/9a4f4a898cc2d01a07828564/robinhood-allow-access.png?expires=1743477300&signature=a5a05f5b190d5d251d88ad06a8265b7743e42bf8c85af027666ed2cd483bf059&req=dSAuHsh9mYRdW%2FMW1HO4zduaSZD04v0CLtrON8tv9S126nZKUAJrBGYf99R9%0Aquyp3a9XEhTVd%2FYAPxE%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1098134522/9a4f4a898cc2d01a07828564/robinhood-allow-access.png?expires=1743477300&signature=a5a05f5b190d5d251d88ad06a8265b7743e42bf8c85af027666ed2cd483bf059&req=dSAuHsh9mYRdW%2FMW1HO4zduaSZD04v0CLtrON8tv9S126nZKUAJrBGYf99R9%0Aquyp3a9XEhTVd%2FYAPxE%3D%0A)

You'll be asked to choose a particular account within Robinhood, for example your stock portfolio or Crypto portfolio.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1098134739/a04a54733387baae668865fd/robinhood-choose-account.png?expires=1743477300&signature=e965b5611cce13be72d57a2abf9be608d12d237f03a9e288c1ca93d26db7d3ff&req=dSAuHsh9mYZcUPMW1HO4zSaCoUg0nc4N%2BgVXxhjUBMXZNraIVHQ75hzrqZkX%0Az1cT6hAEHhbFfyU0vic%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1098134739/a04a54733387baae668865fd/robinhood-choose-account.png?expires=1743477300&signature=e965b5611cce13be72d57a2abf9be608d12d237f03a9e288c1ca93d26db7d3ff&req=dSAuHsh9mYZcUPMW1HO4zSaCoUg0nc4N%2BgVXxhjUBMXZNraIVHQ75hzrqZkX%0Az1cT6hAEHhbFfyU0vic%3D%0A)

After selecting an account (just 1 please), the Plaid modal will confirm the permissions TRMNL is requesting. They are the `investments` and `assets` products, which you can learn more about [here](https://plaid.com/docs/api/products/investments/)
 and [here](https://plaid.com/docs/api/products/assets/)
.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1098135160/8782bc8245de7b9e971c5f20/robinhood-plaid-modal-permissions.png?expires=1743477300&signature=04639171cf8d30c74fc12d75f43328ef3cff487d9307a26d0a25c312a8669f1c&req=dSAuHsh9mIBZWfMW1HO4zfNbCKThvqXUlWmDcuGuniVDRws9007%2B05ZCryIM%0ApccZoynzAYVFW3dtz8k%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1098135160/8782bc8245de7b9e971c5f20/robinhood-plaid-modal-permissions.png?expires=1743477300&signature=04639171cf8d30c74fc12d75f43328ef3cff487d9307a26d0a25c312a8669f1c&req=dSAuHsh9mIBZWfMW1HO4zfNbCKThvqXUlWmDcuGuniVDRws9007%2B05ZCryIM%0ApccZoynzAYVFW3dtz8k%3D%0A)

**Step 3 - Configure Plugin**
-----------------------------

After selecting the final "Allow" option in Step 2, you'll need to finish setting up your plugin inside TRMNL. Start by giving it a name and refresh rate.

![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1098136110/eedb050a418ab3e852370a4b/robinhood-plugin-configuration.png?expires=1743606000&signature=9940a7acb0add05a6ede6a25c002bfbe5168054495794eead62adba0cfa7a770&req=dSAuHsh9m4BeWfMW3Hu4gYdRNlFOVANFnUmlzfl9UeEmECatJUST6KVNLTDO%0Aqw%3D%3D%0A)

Next, determine if you want to see a chart of your portfolio value over time, or simply a large number with your current portfolio value.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1098136416/30efe67b212c3e13ca7879a9/robinhood-configuration-visual-type.png?expires=1743477300&signature=12c7852a4802ff962fb0a7df8eba4439bf610500e9b89170533ab6677f6ea25e&req=dSAuHsh9m4VeX%2FMW1HO4zYXfXL81EFD3iLXAiiogiNiBxnD2Librjr5E6jel%0Ag%2FWIJKX8tf9ssCgi2sk%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1098136416/30efe67b212c3e13ca7879a9/robinhood-configuration-visual-type.png?expires=1743477300&signature=12c7852a4802ff962fb0a7df8eba4439bf610500e9b89170533ab6677f6ea25e&req=dSAuHsh9m4VeX%2FMW1HO4zYXfXL81EFD3iLXAiiogiNiBxnD2Librjr5E6jel%0Ag%2FWIJKX8tf9ssCgi2sk%3D%0A)

The "Portfolio Value" type is a number, and the "Value Chart" type is a line graph, similar to [this](https://usetrmnl.com/plugins/robinhood_portfolio)
 example.

**Step 4 - You're Done!**
-------------------------

Based on your device's refresh settings, you'll begin seeing Google Calendar very soon.

Stay focused.

**Troubleshooting**
-------------------

If you'd like to disconnect Robinhood from TRMNL, first delete the plugin via the top right trash can icon when viewing the plugin configuration.

Next, we suggest making a free Plaid.com account with your email or phone number. This will automatically look up and link all of your Plaid-driven financial connections, such as TRMNL.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1098137363/be2189dcfa670f6958c61037/Robinhood+-+sharing+data.png?expires=1743477300&signature=72c3551d501d73df9400c0e94543e6c124595a2561fad9030626149c8e21aab9&req=dSAuHsh9moJZWvMW1HO4zapcAWpqHalrQJFW3Svx3DAMtl2VaqEpG1Rjb3w0%0AVmhzzVlH45mxUHWHZFQ%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1098137363/be2189dcfa670f6958c61037/Robinhood+-+sharing+data.png?expires=1743477300&signature=72c3551d501d73df9400c0e94543e6c124595a2561fad9030626149c8e21aab9&req=dSAuHsh9moJZWvMW1HO4zapcAWpqHalrQJFW3Svx3DAMtl2VaqEpG1Rjb3w0%0AVmhzzVlH45mxUHWHZFQ%3D%0A)

Simply click the TRMNL connection from the list in your Plaid dashboard, then select that you want to stop sharing information and click Continue.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1098137582/1ec7adb5a201d3a0638bdd31/Robinhood+-+stop+sharing+confirm.png?expires=1743477300&signature=d6ecb3affaf63d8fae648dde62f41e0abbe639c6325e28653009a6ffa8bdf8bb&req=dSAuHsh9moRXW%2FMW1HO4zck31Luukat%2BCml%2Bnrpi5phZW0q%2BNr4CPkA2HW4r%0AOr44zr%2FIRCJsAKpZLm8%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1098137582/1ec7adb5a201d3a0638bdd31/Robinhood+-+stop+sharing+confirm.png?expires=1743477300&signature=d6ecb3affaf63d8fae648dde62f41e0abbe639c6325e28653009a6ffa8bdf8bb&req=dSAuHsh9moRXW%2FMW1HO4zck31Luukat%2BCml%2Bnrpi5phZW0q%2BNr4CPkA2HW4r%0AOr44zr%2FIRCJsAKpZLm8%3D%0A)

TRMNL will no longer have any access to your Robinhood account (via Plaid), but you can reconnect anytime by following Steps 1-2 above.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

# Google Analytics | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_f9025aa61c)

[](#h_e6fe85cfae)

[All Collections](/en/)

[Plugins](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820559-plugins)

Google Analytics

Web traffic and visitor analytics.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 5 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_f9025aa61c)

[](#h_e6fe85cfae)

Connecting Google Analytics to TRMNL just takes a few seconds and doesn’t require any coding.

Step 1 - Visit the Google Analytics plugin
------------------------------------------

Inside TRMNL, navigate to Plugins > Google Analytics. There you need to:

*   Link your Google Analytics account
    
*   Name your plugin (usually the name of your website)
    
*   Choose a [Google Property ID](https://developers.google.com/analytics/devguides/reporting/data/v1/property-id)
    
*   Select a lookback period (Type) of 7, 30, or 90 days
    

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1193267011/bedda96e01cacec3537c185b/AD_4nXegiuesUVrBuDavryelLswnEZ7l7TEDdCUXlIkOE3O8YM3qViUHA6VLiYjOz59QpWUwplKM-aQU4dAhWrAwAgNv04JKuKyu_xigdfoYLahmCpmVNsIkquPWBZCN0-QPZWnX0v8FiRsKLtTCBEfiDmW_AVx4?expires=1743477300&signature=ed76e4580c3d070e0794ae46094f61ea3b0adda5d09abed92cdbe3df007214c3&req=dSEuFct4moFeWPMW1HO4zSf5gyM%2F43ieGDPsVkd6LKNb93RUPb%2FrFygSHM4n%0AJ9XsQ35a%2FwZayG6C8mc%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1193267011/bedda96e01cacec3537c185b/AD_4nXegiuesUVrBuDavryelLswnEZ7l7TEDdCUXlIkOE3O8YM3qViUHA6VLiYjOz59QpWUwplKM-aQU4dAhWrAwAgNv04JKuKyu_xigdfoYLahmCpmVNsIkquPWBZCN0-QPZWnX0v8FiRsKLtTCBEfiDmW_AVx4?expires=1743477300&signature=ed76e4580c3d070e0794ae46094f61ea3b0adda5d09abed92cdbe3df007214c3&req=dSEuFct4moFeWPMW1HO4zSf5gyM%2F43ieGDPsVkd6LKNb93RUPb%2FrFygSHM4n%0AJ9XsQ35a%2FwZayG6C8mc%3D%0A)

Step 2 - You're Done!
---------------------

Based on your desired refresh settings, TRMNL will begin showcasing analytics data from account very soon.

Stay focused.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1193267005/ad093642bd86ec69d8e404d6/AD_4nXfOs9rYhK4GzA8nybTN8q2HoTGn8QqhyOF77fsKY9m9pjkSKvscWthgCGl_7sl1cDOUiAh3u1AHDrIVJB_vfQ1eZXrygink0HC7_3qvD1IhJi6hKR0sciT4NvTb8oleWY1ZvnhEcM_bdQpnR6ieiLyoyXgx?expires=1743477300&signature=958470d075173a17d20e93e1e7e8315b7fe48de36a542b953c7724c9945b903a&req=dSEuFct4moFfXPMW1HO4zdzPHOs6d1Z6GJEok%2FJK2O44I%2B%2Fz5rZvD%2FeFW%2BKf%0AkUk3pguERSrLKCg%2BWOE%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1193267005/ad093642bd86ec69d8e404d6/AD_4nXfOs9rYhK4GzA8nybTN8q2HoTGn8QqhyOF77fsKY9m9pjkSKvscWthgCGl_7sl1cDOUiAh3u1AHDrIVJB_vfQ1eZXrygink0HC7_3qvD1IhJi6hKR0sciT4NvTb8oleWY1ZvnhEcM_bdQpnR6ieiLyoyXgx?expires=1743477300&signature=958470d075173a17d20e93e1e7e8315b7fe48de36a542b953c7724c9945b903a&req=dSEuFct4moFfXPMW1HO4zdzPHOs6d1Z6GJEok%2FJK2O44I%2B%2Fz5rZvD%2FeFW%2BKf%0AkUk3pguERSrLKCg%2BWOE%3D%0A)

# Upcoming Movies | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_db4ac9e48c)

[](#h_8f091be47f)

[](#h_ce1e97f5b9)

[All Collections](/en/)

[Plugins](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820559-plugins)

Upcoming Movies

What's playing in theaters, now or in the near future.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 6 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_db4ac9e48c)

[](#h_8f091be47f)

[](#h_ce1e97f5b9)

A casual feed of upcoming movies is just a couple clicks away. Credit to TMDB ([The Movie Database](https://www.themoviedb.org/)
) for providing this data.

Step 1 - Visit the Upcoming Movies Plugin
-----------------------------------------

Inside TRMNL, navigate to Plugins > Upcoming Movies.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1210905827/bb588c374845ec37d8cda8c6f91f/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=d28240273e4c1e5dab9e5433f17c616edfc74bfcfebc46ca20805b732b3236ce&req=dSImFsB%2BmIldXvMW1HO4zStC%2B9IFtI9H8ScEHEkBukKV4sFOMuWfKjLU4pq4%0AHkiUjT91Morh93VsEk8%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1210905827/bb588c374845ec37d8cda8c6f91f/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=d28240273e4c1e5dab9e5433f17c616edfc74bfcfebc46ca20805b732b3236ce&req=dSImFsB%2BmIldXvMW1HO4zStC%2B9IFtI9H8ScEHEkBukKV4sFOMuWfKjLU4pq4%0AHkiUjT91Morh93VsEk8%3D%0A)

**Step 2 - Configure Plugin**
-----------------------------

First set your region / country on the right hand side to filter movies that are coming out in your area.

Next set a "Filter By" preference. If you choose "Now Playing," movies that come out as recently as yesterday will be returned on your device. If you choose "Upcoming," movies that come out today or later will be shown.

Step 3 - You're Done!
---------------------

Based on your device's refresh settings, you'll begin seeing new movies soon.

Stay focused.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

# beehiiv | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_158b16527e)

[](#h_fca68b1ace)

[](#h_d107f608c3)

[](#h_0f1c0b85a2)

[](#h_82bacca4f0)

[All Collections](/en/)

[Plugins](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820559-plugins)

beehiiv

The newsletter platform built for growth

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 7 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_158b16527e)

[](#h_fca68b1ace)

[](#h_d107f608c3)

[](#h_0f1c0b85a2)

[](#h_82bacca4f0)

Connecting beehiiv to TRMNL just takes a few seconds and doesn’t require any coding.

Step 1 - Visit the beehiiv plugin
---------------------------------

Inside TRMNL, navigate to Plugins > beehiiv. There you need to

*   Name your plugin (for example the name of your newsletter)
    
*   Add beehiiv API key
    
*   Add beehiiv Publication Id
    

[![](https://trmnl.intercom-attachments-7.com/i/o/1181902826/74ffc1707b791c18c7f77ba8/AD_4nXc8n8cayAMrqEXUf1lBYmw_AJJXKeiWxo8okq1WvVjIba_kNbZZal4_wmcvOSrsWOcfcUcxdJ2nhCRuW9DyEk5xKwc5jzl5ZzwOAe7PN91TMWq2KiR44bjxN6lyR6QzRj8djVx_B08aWZSlmVa-3h_Hckbo?expires=1743477300&signature=1977bbd605f720f42f715d91f46fe8ac6c73f8d78586a887637876fb48541d42&req=dSEvF8B%2Bn4ldX%2FMW1HO4zcapLvaZaVnikbwbNSCyOam2gNHeDcxGo%2FXAorFP%0A0iKqR0j56ivsYDSeyqo%3D%0A)](https://trmnl.intercom-attachments-7.com/i/o/1181902826/74ffc1707b791c18c7f77ba8/AD_4nXc8n8cayAMrqEXUf1lBYmw_AJJXKeiWxo8okq1WvVjIba_kNbZZal4_wmcvOSrsWOcfcUcxdJ2nhCRuW9DyEk5xKwc5jzl5ZzwOAe7PN91TMWq2KiR44bjxN6lyR6QzRj8djVx_B08aWZSlmVa-3h_Hckbo?expires=1743477300&signature=1977bbd605f720f42f715d91f46fe8ac6c73f8d78586a887637876fb48541d42&req=dSEvF8B%2Bn4ldX%2FMW1HO4zcapLvaZaVnikbwbNSCyOam2gNHeDcxGo%2FXAorFP%0A0iKqR0j56ivsYDSeyqo%3D%0A)

Step 2 - Connect beehiiv
------------------------

Inside beehiiv, navigate to Settings > Integrations > API. There you will see Publication ID and API Keys

[![](https://trmnl.intercom-attachments-7.com/i/o/1181902839/642ccb2386a5e914e63d0467/AD_4nXfIp1CzpUyAMxfQ64J0yjaFFNoxdBtmhKz8klSzI1HWuuTLmvakyjMzHXf8eBtmyws4RhqmrzqfSKiHKaBJt6caa1kUpc0wDHTpsNDrcGPEDJPKFyRuB9mwp2DCGU2J-llX0gaJ4_Nt_RrgbWyDfLwHbUE?expires=1743477300&signature=623b9a367a9529d2c82a455696fef52d34b3cad7b2ecc5d69eb8fc46e44f8077&req=dSEvF8B%2Bn4lcUPMW1HO4zSoQK%2Fuxt2t3lJCTOsQxGiapKb70JAECVylNJ9pi%0A1CltD3pFWAoDK1KWm1Y%3D%0A)](https://trmnl.intercom-attachments-7.com/i/o/1181902839/642ccb2386a5e914e63d0467/AD_4nXfIp1CzpUyAMxfQ64J0yjaFFNoxdBtmhKz8klSzI1HWuuTLmvakyjMzHXf8eBtmyws4RhqmrzqfSKiHKaBJt6caa1kUpc0wDHTpsNDrcGPEDJPKFyRuB9mwp2DCGU2J-llX0gaJ4_Nt_RrgbWyDfLwHbUE?expires=1743477300&signature=623b9a367a9529d2c82a455696fef52d34b3cad7b2ecc5d69eb8fc46e44f8077&req=dSEvF8B%2Bn4lcUPMW1HO4zSoQK%2Fuxt2t3lJCTOsQxGiapKb70JAECVylNJ9pi%0A1CltD3pFWAoDK1KWm1Y%3D%0A)

Step 3 - Create new API Key
---------------------------

To create a new API just select New API key then Copy the New API Key

Step 4 - Configure Plugin
-------------------------

Back inside TRMNL, paste this API key in the configuration form then paste your API V2 key give this plugin a name. Click Save.

[![](https://trmnl.intercom-attachments-7.com/i/o/1181902860/c6e2bb7be5477ae8cf705c4b/AD_4nXdLWZC-utsNAB_4FHdhYFBuFyQCl_nwIjv39MKX3kP93C0qJCnO0e50zRi8rDFCcy0yP3EQk4Z4PjVfOSy1afOEObuHKIAffSNaRLfVaBBm_5xAhg8oLD_nW-ibAWcASumK_AVZdX7_HzIo7JZvD43LBg?expires=1743477300&signature=ff342e809572bb5f199c3e6707ee43ce46b42d874a8e8223d3f306f3e1505438&req=dSEvF8B%2Bn4lZWfMW1HO4za2yAu9Bx70wPF27OdA4%2BVytBZtITKMMNS%2FQTJHy%0AetGFJWsp4BDMzVT1z58%3D%0A)](https://trmnl.intercom-attachments-7.com/i/o/1181902860/c6e2bb7be5477ae8cf705c4b/AD_4nXdLWZC-utsNAB_4FHdhYFBuFyQCl_nwIjv39MKX3kP93C0qJCnO0e50zRi8rDFCcy0yP3EQk4Z4PjVfOSy1afOEObuHKIAffSNaRLfVaBBm_5xAhg8oLD_nW-ibAWcASumK_AVZdX7_HzIo7JZvD43LBg?expires=1743477300&signature=ff342e809572bb5f199c3e6707ee43ce46b42d874a8e8223d3f306f3e1505438&req=dSEvF8B%2Bn4lZWfMW1HO4za2yAu9Bx70wPF27OdA4%2BVytBZtITKMMNS%2FQTJHy%0AetGFJWsp4BDMzVT1z58%3D%0A)

Step 5 - You're Done!
---------------------

Based on your desired refresh settings, TRMNL will begin showcasing useful highlights from your beehiiv account very soon.

Stay focused.

Did this answer your question?

Shopping List

Simple tracker for upcoming purchases.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 6 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_26832c2cdc)

[](#h_d8bdaeca9b)

[](#h_5dd575cc05)

Don't forget a single thing (especially toothpaste) on your next grocery run with our native Shopping List plugin.

Step 1 - Visit the Shopping List Plugin
---------------------------------------

Inside TRMNL, navigate to Plugins > Shopping List.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1210909656/44d539680274e8ccedb58a87008d/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=a1991e8303e1c5cc13fa3c074aa362ca7e25252cc43adb07201428d488898228&req=dSImFsB%2BlIdaX%2FMW1HO4zdymL3wlb58ZSvoLXln2JthFVFuGHTP1GPIk6KKT%0AHr4EV812HTSV9MSmJK0%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1210909656/44d539680274e8ccedb58a87008d/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=a1991e8303e1c5cc13fa3c074aa362ca7e25252cc43adb07201428d488898228&req=dSImFsB%2BlIdaX%2FMW1HO4zdymL3wlb58ZSvoLXln2JthFVFuGHTP1GPIk6KKT%0AHr4EV812HTSV9MSmJK0%3D%0A)

Step 2 - Configure Plugin
-------------------------

Add as many items as you'd like. We actually encrypt these by the way.

\[**Coming Soon** - TRMNL CLI with command `trmnl go shopping_list add milk` (to add milk to your Shopping List, from your machine's native terminal!\]

Step 3 - You're Done!
---------------------

Based on your device's refresh settings, you'll see changes to your Shopping List very soon.

Stay focused.

Did this answer your question?

# Stock Price | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_937c5b5c31)

[](#h_35dde9fe19)

[All Collections](/en/)

[Plugins](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820559-plugins)

Stock Price

Public securities valuation by ticker

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 3 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_937c5b5c31)

[](#h_35dde9fe19)

Picking the stocks you want to keep up with takes a few seconds and doesn’t require any coding.

**Step 1 - Visit the Stock Price plugin**
-----------------------------------------

Inside TRMNL, navigate to Plugins > Stock Price.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1249285169/94b4d6cbe5c3d429d5e798f0ab75/trmnl-stock-price-plugin.png?expires=1743477300&signature=1f633efbadb7f33e016244aa2b9a8d253e221ebc13150f442355da1d3dcb30b9&req=dSIjH8t2mIBZUPMW1HO4zYn4QvPO9UKc%2B9KoR4KY3Z6Boo28klhkpwyn18GF%0AFnnFRjVhmvZhAcpvdYo%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1249285169/94b4d6cbe5c3d429d5e798f0ab75/trmnl-stock-price-plugin.png?expires=1743477300&signature=1f633efbadb7f33e016244aa2b9a8d253e221ebc13150f442355da1d3dcb30b9&req=dSIjH8t2mIBZUPMW1HO4zYn4QvPO9UKc%2B9KoR4KY3Z6Boo28klhkpwyn18GF%0AFnnFRjVhmvZhAcpvdYo%3D%0A)

Here you can:

*   Name your Plugin
    
*   Provide tickers (**USA markets only**) you would like to track (separated by a comma)
    
*   Choose a currency (email [\[email protected\]](/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#a0d4c5c1cde0d5d3c5d4d2cdcecc8ec3cfcd)
     if yours is not listed)
    

We currently support the following indexes, in addition to tickers:

VIX, MXACW, XWLD, MXUSA, MXEF, MXEA, DJI, RUI, RUT, OEX, OEX, SPX, XSP, XSP, SPESG, XND

To track crypto prices, use the CoinMarketCap plugin.

**Step 2 - You're Done!**
-------------------------

Based on your desired refresh settings, TRMNL will begin showcasing the most recent price and daily change very soon.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1225576176/41472d17733e52c985f4d6e30647/p69a6gh9mm3czx6gk0g69x7z8opr?expires=1743477300&signature=60cfc40e816ab39c1ef44e52eca83c71659b0599adf775e075cc3e61cae1b009&req=dSIlE8x5m4BYX%2FMW1HO4zY%2Fjps5CODWSP8tt%2FTWjru%2BPuAXY7fdqjZQqw5kO%0Akr6paeqtyom2VzscsQI%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1225576176/41472d17733e52c985f4d6e30647/p69a6gh9mm3czx6gk0g69x7z8opr?expires=1743477300&signature=60cfc40e816ab39c1ef44e52eca83c71659b0599adf775e075cc3e61cae1b009&req=dSIlE8x5m4BYX%2FMW1HO4zY%2Fjps5CODWSP8tt%2FTWjru%2BPuAXY7fdqjZQqw5kO%0Akr6paeqtyom2VzscsQI%3D%0A)

**Troubleshooting**

*   You can show up to 12 tickers at a time. We suggest creating multiple instances of the Stock Price plugin, then building a Mashup layout from your Playlists tab, if you want to see more on the same screen.
    
*   To edit a ticker, create a new plugin instance with the correct symbol and delete the incorrect plugin instance.
    
*   Some currencies like EUR will use a "," separator versus "." for decimals
    
*   If you submit a ticker that is invalid, it will show the code you entered with no price
    
    [![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1225573807/9215375dd6583f01ce6f213a28a5/Screen+Shot+2024-10-22+at+11_55_56+PM.png?expires=1743477300&signature=452d7264f8c4dcd376eefab843ef827ce996d2d3cbb47d8ebadb477a7a020fea&req=dSIlE8x5nolfXvMW1HO4zXYR29w90Tfk2wW41xoKXE%2B7foQ0lnp2TK792MBc%0APGmF%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1225573807/9215375dd6583f01ce6f213a28a5/Screen+Shot+2024-10-22+at+11_55_56+PM.png?expires=1743477300&signature=452d7264f8c4dcd376eefab843ef827ce996d2d3cbb47d8ebadb477a7a020fea&req=dSIlE8x5nolfXvMW1HO4zXYR29w90Tfk2wW41xoKXE%2B7foQ0lnp2TK792MBc%0APGmF%0A)
    
*   Some tickers require a different format than their trading syntax. [Read this post](https://www.marketdata.app/education/stocks/how-to-look-up-preferred-stock-symbols/)
     to learn more, for example NASDAQ should be input as "LFMDP". Another resource for figuring out tickers is [here](https://www.marketdata.app/education/options/complete-list-of-index-tickers/)
    .
    

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

# Weather | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_8cee686e19)

[](#h_4c339dff61)

[](#h_1bd21f82f5)

[All Collections](/en/)

[Plugins](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820559-plugins)

Weather

Your local forecast.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 3 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_8cee686e19)

[](#h_4c339dff61)

[](#h_1bd21f82f5)

Adding a weather tracker takes just a few seconds with data generously provided by [WeatherAPI.com](https://www.weatherapi.com)
.

Step 1 - Visit the Weather Plugin
---------------------------------

Inside TRMNL, navigate to Plugins > Weather.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1226285614/2c11a6d9e9ae0fea027fc8b03899/TRMNL+weather+plugin.png?expires=1743477300&signature=463a2a05e52a58be391b1819afac9a25bb7e71403895a67417bfb22ddf03a90c&req=dSIlEMt2mIdeXfMW1HO4zRSE6FSeAEpcojvcIsaArOY9Z6%2B6025Dycu16kPM%0Agd8RQhtp65ZFK0wWQe0%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1226285614/2c11a6d9e9ae0fea027fc8b03899/TRMNL+weather+plugin.png?expires=1743477300&signature=463a2a05e52a58be391b1819afac9a25bb7e71403895a67417bfb22ddf03a90c&req=dSIlEMt2mIdeXfMW1HO4zRSE6FSeAEpcojvcIsaArOY9Z6%2B6025Dycu16kPM%0Agd8RQhtp65ZFK0wWQe0%3D%0A)

Step 2 - Configure Plugin
-------------------------

Give your plugin a **name**, in case you want to track forecasts in multiple locations. This name is shown in the bottom right corner of your device screen.

Next input a **location**. You may have to try a couple different combinations, for example "Atlanta, GA" (city, 2-digit province) works, but for ambiguous locations it's better to be verbose. So "LA" could mean Los Angeles, but also Louisiana, or some other country we don't even know about.

Finally choose a **temperature unit**, either Fahrenheit or Celsius.

Step 3 - You're Done!
---------------------

Based on your device's refresh settings, you'll begin seeing weather reports very soon.

Note: while we fetch data according to your refresh interval, TRMNL only generates new screen renders if the data fetched has changes. So if you set the weather to refresh every 15 mins, but the forecast is the same for 4 hours, the 'refreshed at' timestamp will remain the same.

Stay focused.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

---

# Gumroad | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[All Collections](/en/)

[Plugins](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820559-plugins)

Gumroad

See how much stuff you're selling.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 5 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_ac161921cf)

[](#h_9164f8f9b8)

[](#h_152d897ea1)

[](#h_6699993621)

Connecting your Gumroad to TRMNL takes just a few seconds.

Step 1 - Visit the Gumroad Plugin
---------------------------------

Inside TRMNL, navigate to Plugins > Gumroad.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1237722764/241639ccdf2b4d8568d701fc5668/Screen+Shot+2024-11-02+at+3_14_48+PM.png?expires=1743477300&signature=4c6070ea8c4fe1f4bbbb33c0df50704ae0bf8bb7153762799cce891821f24cc9&req=dSIkEc58n4ZZXfMW1HO4zdDRtulJfO8XC4435kTluxZgRgHIduyGM8dkevKN%0Asu%2BKK7qv5veXO%2FbBKHY%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1237722764/241639ccdf2b4d8568d701fc5668/Screen+Shot+2024-11-02+at+3_14_48+PM.png?expires=1743477300&signature=4c6070ea8c4fe1f4bbbb33c0df50704ae0bf8bb7153762799cce891821f24cc9&req=dSIkEc58n4ZZXfMW1HO4zdDRtulJfO8XC4435kTluxZgRgHIduyGM8dkevKN%0Asu%2BKK7qv5veXO%2FbBKHY%3D%0A)

**Step 2 - Connect Gumroad**
----------------------------

Click to "Connect with Gumroad" on the right side of the screen, review TRMNL applications then select "Authorize"

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1237723678/7545e4baf6b1b953e589db46c424/Screen+Shot+2024-11-02+at+3_15_55+PM.png?expires=1743477300&signature=871e5b3566badd8d800b0918ab7fdad4140c7eedf98bc39bebbbd941a6e34f86&req=dSIkEc58nodYUfMW1HO4zYZxML%2BAXV4Qn%2FIT2ZPypsxvskkwrOYwt81BlJA1%0AQ89E1aU%2FxsxLJsQiAxc%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1237723678/7545e4baf6b1b953e589db46c424/Screen+Shot+2024-11-02+at+3_15_55+PM.png?expires=1743477300&signature=871e5b3566badd8d800b0918ab7fdad4140c7eedf98bc39bebbbd941a6e34f86&req=dSIkEc58nodYUfMW1HO4zYZxML%2BAXV4Qn%2FIT2ZPypsxvskkwrOYwt81BlJA1%0AQ89E1aU%2FxsxLJsQiAxc%3D%0A)

**Step 3 - Configure Plugin**
-----------------------------

Give your channel plugin a name then select a "Lookback Period." This is simply the number of days you prefer TRMNL to tally sales count and sales value.

**Step 4 - You're Done!**
-------------------------

Based on your device's refresh settings, you'll begin seeing Gumroad data very soon.

Stay focused.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

# RSS Feed | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

RSS Feed

Get updates from your favorite website, blog and online publications

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 5 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_9ae76b8b46)

[](#h_ad00ede8e2)

[](#h_50a03f6786)

[](#h_0635db1d4d)

Setting up your favorite RSS Feed is easy with TRMNL.

Step 1 - Visit the RSS Feed Plugin
----------------------------------

Inside TRMNL, navigate to Plugins > RSS and create a plugin Name.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1262720413/21cc474797172a309573314d3ce5/Screen+Shot+2024-11-22+at+5_26_13+PM.png?expires=1743477300&signature=10e3508850221ea66e0e8661b074819a227dce945530d9e39e186cc68ffbd9e2&req=dSIhFM58nYVeWvMW1HO4zXBG9XHpwSU2dxbWQpJIF96gJBvXQC%2BTLPjPpxBR%0Adt%2By%2BNdrnFX0hIdiv9Y%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1262720413/21cc474797172a309573314d3ce5/Screen+Shot+2024-11-22+at+5_26_13+PM.png?expires=1743477300&signature=10e3508850221ea66e0e8661b074819a227dce945530d9e39e186cc68ffbd9e2&req=dSIhFM58nYVeWvMW1HO4zXBG9XHpwSU2dxbWQpJIF96gJBvXQC%2BTLPjPpxBR%0Adt%2By%2BNdrnFX0hIdiv9Y%3D%0A)

**Step 2 - Add RSS Feed URL**
-----------------------------

Drop in the URL of the RSS Feed you'd like to point to. XML files [like this one](https://search.cnbc.com/rs/search/combinedcms/view.xml?partnerId=wrss01&id=100003114)
 will work best.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1262721874/7bcd6cfb4351884fe4562cd05340/Screen+Shot+2024-11-22+at+5_28_39+PM.png?expires=1743477300&signature=18b2f0b4023dcdb87517dcea0322ae6ca3756648c78080f228ae95913cca68b1&req=dSIhFM58nIlYXfMW1HO4zZbTfr%2BLVeSxpP0jg%2BJgj09BAvSnELkl1TT1Dco3%0AC9TFpNRqa2l5kzu7qdI%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1262721874/7bcd6cfb4351884fe4562cd05340/Screen+Shot+2024-11-22+at+5_28_39+PM.png?expires=1743477300&signature=18b2f0b4023dcdb87517dcea0322ae6ca3756648c78080f228ae95913cca68b1&req=dSIhFM58nIlYXfMW1HO4zZbTfr%2BLVeSxpP0jg%2BJgj09BAvSnELkl1TT1Dco3%0AC9TFpNRqa2l5kzu7qdI%3D%0A)

**Step 3 - Press Save and You're Done!**
----------------------------------------

Based on your device's refresh settings, you'll begin seeing RSS feed data very soon.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1262723434/5634a9b53aca3ca234593ff80d6a/Screen+Shot+2024-11-22+at+5_31_05+PM.png?expires=1743477300&signature=d5ec9336f343807cfb324185b6ff4ec77172385f63fccfa2e6ba0124d16af9b1&req=dSIhFM58noVcXfMW1HO4zSo%2FvM7zswxKOYPnMcN4wDeZh9Gs3ys8SSUMmuFL%0AyyyTT8nCAKpGxbrz0YI%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1262723434/5634a9b53aca3ca234593ff80d6a/Screen+Shot+2024-11-22+at+5_31_05+PM.png?expires=1743477300&signature=d5ec9336f343807cfb324185b6ff4ec77172385f63fccfa2e6ba0124d16af9b1&req=dSIhFM58noVcXfMW1HO4zSo%2FvM7zswxKOYPnMcN4wDeZh9Gs3ys8SSUMmuFL%0AyyyTT8nCAKpGxbrz0YI%3D%0A)

**Popular RSS Feeds**
---------------------

We curated a list of some of the most popular RSS feeds on the internet, [check it out here](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1EyQdmrFG9DHTK1VcGPV3BHi2jM4rtSjde95OR_shDHk/edit?gid=0#gid=0)
.

Stay focused.

Did this answer your question?

# Language Learning | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_d9153a497d)

[](#h_ab5ff1806c)

[All Collections](/en/)

[Plugins](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820559-plugins)

Language Learning

Discover new words in your target language.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 4 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_d9153a497d)

[](#h_ab5ff1806c)

The TRMNL language learning plugin is simple -- 1 new word, every 12 hours, with an example sentence. Setting it up takes just a few seconds.

**Step 1 - Visit the Language Learning Plugin**
-----------------------------------------------

Inside TRMNL, navigate to Plugins > Language Learning.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1303324607/7ee20edb5edde494577b5670ef4b/trmnl-language-learning-plugin.png?expires=1743477300&signature=714be1c6018a12218cd323659a7925a04a208429843b5b965487ea720240ef8a&req=dSMnFcp8mYdfXvMW1HO4zYAeDtQ9BsvBHauVoAezh88Kd%2Bg3YZaJuFIdC4gg%0AaiJA%2B12Px%2BXMtuRfjN0%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1303324607/7ee20edb5edde494577b5670ef4b/trmnl-language-learning-plugin.png?expires=1743477300&signature=714be1c6018a12218cd323659a7925a04a208429843b5b965487ea720240ef8a&req=dSMnFcp8mYdfXvMW1HO4zYAeDtQ9BsvBHauVoAezh88Kd%2Bg3YZaJuFIdC4gg%0AaiJA%2B12Px%2BXMtuRfjN0%3D%0A)

Choose a target language from the dropdown, then click Save.

**Step 2 - You're Done!**
-------------------------

Based on your device's refresh settings, you'll begin seeing new words and sentences very soon.

Stay focused.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1303310107/82509658bacfcc41509f9230505d/trmnl-screensaver-plugin.jpeg?expires=1743477300&signature=e697f44cb7217d96b4688ac7c267a87bd65b95b9c33692cee7c3d49db40c0765&req=dSMnFcp%2FnYBfXvMW1HO4zW1KyTzjCbnQQqotAxb25PsVneGH3VpGV4bLt%2FRs%0A85Wbi53wKN%2FrZlGgxIs%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1303310107/82509658bacfcc41509f9230505d/trmnl-screensaver-plugin.jpeg?expires=1743477300&signature=e697f44cb7217d96b4688ac7c267a87bd65b95b9c33692cee7c3d49db40c0765&req=dSMnFcp%2FnYBfXvMW1HO4zW1KyTzjCbnQQqotAxb25PsVneGH3VpGV4bLt%2FRs%0A85Wbi53wKN%2FrZlGgxIs%3D%0A)

# Email Meter | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_1756ce6bd2)

[](#h_22be7b5a33)

[](#h_135c87c4f8)

[](#h_a3ec83aade)

[All Collections](/en/)

[Plugins](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820559-plugins)

Email Meter

Benchmark stats from your Gmail or Microsoft inbox.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 5 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_1756ce6bd2)

[](#h_22be7b5a33)

[](#h_135c87c4f8)

[](#h_a3ec83aade)

Measuring how you leverage email requires 2 things: a free or paid Email Meter account, and a little bit of (safe, ethical) web browser hacking.

To make a free Email Meter account, visit [emailmeter.com](https://emailmeter.com/)
. Then follow along below.

**Step 1 - Visit the Email Meter Plugin**
-----------------------------------------

Inside TRMNL, navigate to Plugins > Email Meter.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1247934195/e3a96f74999ce07bcd48a410ef1c/email-meter-plugin-example.png?expires=1743477300&signature=6c1f13afbf2d198a42cc05295c66c489fed178cbd30c1e2e46545f923bdaab99&req=dSIjEcB9mYBWXPMW1HO4zeqOwpahwuPhTHRIXS2u19QAbt2jVEbM7dqYcZkZ%0Adg4zN2fP2QnL%2FwBFqkE%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1247934195/e3a96f74999ce07bcd48a410ef1c/email-meter-plugin-example.png?expires=1743477300&signature=6c1f13afbf2d198a42cc05295c66c489fed178cbd30c1e2e46545f923bdaab99&req=dSIjEcB9mYBWXPMW1HO4zeqOwpahwuPhTHRIXS2u19QAbt2jVEbM7dqYcZkZ%0Adg4zN2fP2QnL%2FwBFqkE%3D%0A)

**Step 2 - Find your Email Meter API Token**
--------------------------------------------

Now for some web hacking. Don't worry, no coding experience is required.

Using either Chrome or Firefox (web browser), log into Email Meter and visit your dashboard. It will look something like this:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1247937188/7362f0a76e8252d2585367e1c816/email-meter-dashboard-example.png?expires=1743477300&signature=584d0c5056f3aea731e148b7b17f3fbeadaa6857602dbb9fa3e4f47519524a9a&req=dSIjEcB9moBXUfMW1HO4zdcNPt2VHB30sk%2FBuN8kHd2HW8mGZ3%2Bw5iLHUoPw%0Auc7UeJJJclNTIcHIcbc%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1247937188/7362f0a76e8252d2585367e1c816/email-meter-dashboard-example.png?expires=1743477300&signature=584d0c5056f3aea731e148b7b17f3fbeadaa6857602dbb9fa3e4f47519524a9a&req=dSIjEcB9moBXUfMW1HO4zdcNPt2VHB30sk%2FBuN8kHd2HW8mGZ3%2Bw5iLHUoPw%0Auc7UeJJJclNTIcHIcbc%3D%0A)

Next, open your browser's Developer Tools via the browser's toolbar, navigating to View > Developer > Developer tools like so:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1247937972/028b39f4f20802b7f22511fbdfb2/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=0fa0d6d8af8a2bed33b5fa0965224b28105584a334bcf5a0cdca9115ac91ca0c&req=dSIjEcB9mohYW%2FMW1HO4zUrDoBqiZmckbJAnEuljMvIB2sPgu%2F30zUjEdQsp%0AadTkAHdjMagVEOtjq8s%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1247937972/028b39f4f20802b7f22511fbdfb2/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=0fa0d6d8af8a2bed33b5fa0965224b28105584a334bcf5a0cdca9115ac91ca0c&req=dSIjEcB9mohYW%2FMW1HO4zUrDoBqiZmckbJAnEuljMvIB2sPgu%2F30zUjEdQsp%0AadTkAHdjMagVEOtjq8s%3D%0A)

A new section should appear in your browser. It may be along the bottom, the right side, or even popped out as a new tab. Click on the "Network" tab of this new pane.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1247939040/2c570783013244bd5fd379243cde/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=9de578389089f7408b4346287b44cd26a025f86926a717a1f7f596f3723a1a63&req=dSIjEcB9lIFbWfMW1HO4zSKPpgY%2B0WWL2G1TuekXDGhM%2FmLpa04kty1%2BnCrQ%0Axxhry%2BPfwBzamTPavls%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1247939040/2c570783013244bd5fd379243cde/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=9de578389089f7408b4346287b44cd26a025f86926a717a1f7f596f3723a1a63&req=dSIjEcB9lIFbWfMW1HO4zSKPpgY%2B0WWL2G1TuekXDGhM%2FmLpa04kty1%2BnCrQ%0Axxhry%2BPfwBzamTPavls%3D%0A)

Now, reload the web page. You should see a lot of text populate this Network tab. After the page loads, type "team-labels" in the Filter field:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1247940337/5e93a2894d7a2e35d4335d7e6a02/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=1573a79bf4c84b70d4edf9b51f2520cc174e76435b15ebc8f5bb8b4aceb5c089&req=dSIjEcB6nYJcXvMW1HO4zWz9jiCxxFuP3RgHotwzp01Tad%2Bzh7p3Yw51Lkzn%0AgKfxG5flJeytF%2BwF6bQ%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1247940337/5e93a2894d7a2e35d4335d7e6a02/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=1573a79bf4c84b70d4edf9b51f2520cc174e76435b15ebc8f5bb8b4aceb5c089&req=dSIjEcB6nYJcXvMW1HO4zWz9jiCxxFuP3RgHotwzp01Tad%2Bzh7p3Yw51Lkzn%0AgKfxG5flJeytF%2BwF6bQ%3D%0A)

Click on the result with the <i> (orange) graphic, which will also have a Method value of "GET + Preflight" in one of the table columns to the right. On the new 'Headers' tab, scroll down to the Request Headers section and find the "Authorization" row.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1247942433/9226e9bad1a12c0ce744f87c3fa1/email-meter-api-token.png?expires=1743477300&signature=62478c33379faf999925c5cc6eb2365cb55d3cb9a3f83b5f1a86e2da82b9da63&req=dSIjEcB6n4VcWvMW1HO4zUiBTmOSK8DEpIc1RZHKai8FGJkcy9r%2FTsALD9H5%0AhUSq1d0TyV%2FyP54yggo%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1247942433/9226e9bad1a12c0ce744f87c3fa1/email-meter-api-token.png?expires=1743477300&signature=62478c33379faf999925c5cc6eb2365cb55d3cb9a3f83b5f1a86e2da82b9da63&req=dSIjEcB6n4VcWvMW1HO4zUiBTmOSK8DEpIc1RZHKai8FGJkcy9r%2FTsALD9H5%0AhUSq1d0TyV%2FyP54yggo%3D%0A)

Copy the long string of characters after the word "Token" from this row. Note that you may need to click open to expand the Request Headers section if you don't see these rows of content.

**Step 3 - Configure Plugin**
-----------------------------

Back inside TRMNL, paste your API token into the API Token field:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1247944172/70251f2460f273b76de13acce04d/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=f6d677470fd83ab70bfe944287563d89a51dbdfa9181b07bd1a009ce6439179e&req=dSIjEcB6mYBYW%2FMW1HO4zbfu%2BZwuEhUS5cV%2BjYYlmxaLBNUMge90sIl%2BcJMt%0AAvwmY943egjBAQ8Axjw%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1247944172/70251f2460f273b76de13acce04d/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=f6d677470fd83ab70bfe944287563d89a51dbdfa9181b07bd1a009ce6439179e&req=dSIjEcB6mYBYW%2FMW1HO4zbfu%2BZwuEhUS5cV%2BjYYlmxaLBNUMge90sIl%2BcJMt%0AAvwmY943egjBAQ8Axjw%3D%0A)

  
Optionally give your Email Meter plugin a name, then click Save.

**Step 4 - You're Done!**
-------------------------

Based on your device's refresh settings, you'll begin seeing Email Meter analytics very soon.

**Note**: the Email Meter team is aware of our integration and they are considering a simpler solution to connecting your account. Also, your API token may expire automatically for security purposes. If you notice incorrect stats, repeat Steps 2-3 above.

Stay focused.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

# ChatGPT | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_c5a68a47a2)

[](#h_ce37389cf8)

[](#h_b3d2229bba)

[All Collections](/en/)

[Plugins](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820559-plugins)

ChatGPT

What can ChatGPT help you with?

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 5 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_c5a68a47a2)

[](#h_ce37389cf8)

[](#h_6a22222442)

[](#h_b3d2229bba)

Add a dash of artificial intelligence to your TRMNL e-ink display with ChatGPT.

Step 1 - Visit the ChatGPT Plugin
---------------------------------

Inside TRMNL, navigate to Plugins > ChatGPT and create a plugin Name.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1253810445/54b6ce2dcdb5f7e44f55421bf0da/Screen+Shot+2024-11-15+at+5_45_41+PM.png?expires=1743477300&signature=04d940dafb860b12d58c4606b9c4f829656e3d1933802ab4238c85a382d0b1b8&req=dSIiFcF%2FnYVbXPMW1HO4zdeBPRT85qVeTQmkH4nSMgF20MIBgyq68DAQVzWX%0AL9rGWMX25h9pV5cmoc4%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1253810445/54b6ce2dcdb5f7e44f55421bf0da/Screen+Shot+2024-11-15+at+5_45_41+PM.png?expires=1743477300&signature=04d940dafb860b12d58c4606b9c4f829656e3d1933802ab4238c85a382d0b1b8&req=dSIiFcF%2FnYVbXPMW1HO4zdeBPRT85qVeTQmkH4nSMgF20MIBgyq68DAQVzWX%0AL9rGWMX25h9pV5cmoc4%3D%0A)

**Step 2 - Create ChatGPT API Key**
-----------------------------------

Go to [this link](https://platform.openai.com/settings/organization/api-keys)
 and create a new secret API.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1253812246/88596fb0e8e5d9c64700b0dc8751/Screen+Shot+2024-11-15+at+5_48_27+PM.png?expires=1743477300&signature=b18ec564b3487645ff3f9da6115a4a3070c005eb8dff453ecbb6940db32f2f88&req=dSIiFcF%2Fn4NbX%2FMW1HO4zZtxVleZ7Sib5KHWZeG4iBNZivt1NaWp2vHafaIt%0A7fhdzSmtpTCMTqhjhEg%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1253812246/88596fb0e8e5d9c64700b0dc8751/Screen+Shot+2024-11-15+at+5_48_27+PM.png?expires=1743477300&signature=b18ec564b3487645ff3f9da6115a4a3070c005eb8dff453ecbb6940db32f2f88&req=dSIiFcF%2Fn4NbX%2FMW1HO4zZtxVleZ7Sib5KHWZeG4iBNZivt1NaWp2vHafaIt%0A7fhdzSmtpTCMTqhjhEg%3D%0A)

Give your key a name, add to a project and select All Permissions, then select create key.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1253812624/5266e342ed9a0f499d13ae2c368b/Screen+Shot+2024-11-15+at+5_48_57+PM.png?expires=1743477300&signature=c398ceabf047e4aa74501ef429c1484c7f0517c786cc356bba75ac84b406f3b4&req=dSIiFcF%2Fn4ddXfMW1HO4zVSn811UIoFGxAErlJLegIE4LaJNtKNO4BOr3Wxv%0AADg%2FysaKzDg2mvJa4gY%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1253812624/5266e342ed9a0f499d13ae2c368b/Screen+Shot+2024-11-15+at+5_48_57+PM.png?expires=1743477300&signature=c398ceabf047e4aa74501ef429c1484c7f0517c786cc356bba75ac84b406f3b4&req=dSIiFcF%2Fn4ddXfMW1HO4zVSn811UIoFGxAErlJLegIE4LaJNtKNO4BOr3Wxv%0AADg%2FysaKzDg2mvJa4gY%3D%0A)

Copy your API Key.

**Step 3 - Configure Plugin**
-----------------------------

Paste your Account API Key and create a prompt you want pulled repeatedly and press save.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1253815703/0cdbeb9c111e0197ece8bdd3f682/Screen+Shot+2024-11-15+at+5_53_53+PM.png?expires=1743477300&signature=fed6b30eecd495a7969fc0f1aca6a90ef27f0f1eb602cb38f09e569394a32665&req=dSIiFcF%2FmIZfWvMW1HO4zYQvvTv%2FqhwoWmmpiwjzeaKJeTHhfjJBEzBVS0%2F%2B%0Akpvm%2BcYmZ4CncH9Bbbs%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1253815703/0cdbeb9c111e0197ece8bdd3f682/Screen+Shot+2024-11-15+at+5_53_53+PM.png?expires=1743477300&signature=fed6b30eecd495a7969fc0f1aca6a90ef27f0f1eb602cb38f09e569394a32665&req=dSIiFcF%2FmIZfWvMW1HO4zYQvvTv%2FqhwoWmmpiwjzeaKJeTHhfjJBEzBVS0%2F%2B%0Akpvm%2BcYmZ4CncH9Bbbs%3D%0A)

**Step 4 - You're Done!**
-------------------------

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1253817025/af6ce6fac52e46dbcc145537018a/Screen+Shot+2024-11-15+at+5_55_52+PM.png?expires=1743477300&signature=690d7a8f91f0eab99df97f349f04ddfcf5239163208bf5b4ea0295514da84f25&req=dSIiFcF%2FmoFdXPMW1HO4zdLx0pchrb0cWAEg%2FNlah5VXydrZw9ra0ywtdWaZ%0AN4TmOtk0kgDzyPp2ico%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1253817025/af6ce6fac52e46dbcc145537018a/Screen+Shot+2024-11-15+at+5_55_52+PM.png?expires=1743477300&signature=690d7a8f91f0eab99df97f349f04ddfcf5239163208bf5b4ea0295514da84f25&req=dSIiFcF%2FmoFdXPMW1HO4zdLx0pchrb0cWAEg%2FNlah5VXydrZw9ra0ywtdWaZ%0AN4TmOtk0kgDzyPp2ico%3D%0A)

Based on your device's refresh settings, you'll begin seeing ChatGPT data very soon.

You will need to make sure you are below your rate limits or else TRMNL may show an error from ChatGPT. Details on rate limits [here](https://platform.openai.com/docs/guides/rate-limits?context=tier-one#usage-tiers)
 and error codes [here](https://platform.openai.com/docs/guides/error-codes/api-errors)
.

Stay focused.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

# Outlook Calendar | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_5c027e2a5a)

[](#h_85c15ca329)

[](#h_8cb205ac9c)

[](#h_8e2de4e8f5)

[All Collections](/en/)

[Plugins](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820559-plugins)

Outlook Calendar

View your upcoming schedule, apointments, and tasks.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated this week

Table of contents

[](#h_5c027e2a5a)

[](#h_85c15ca329)

[](#h_8cb205ac9c)

[](#h_8e2de4e8f5)

Connecting your Outlook 365 Calendar to TRMNL takes just a few seconds.

**Step 1 - Visit the Outlook Calendar Plugin**
----------------------------------------------

Inside TRMNL, navigate to Plugins > Outlook Calendar.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1268653992/291f94424686cc9349718dda8646/trmnl-outlook-calendar-plugin.png?expires=1743477300&signature=519acfc6d3ead73c02d69e3c83c7b9d12d8778def466d3c80df5ac29a64ebf71&req=dSIhHs97nohWW%2FMW1HO4zU0x7DrQZHyk4C62wOdJ1CvwHQOQjYYutAFor7VD%0AlCWRCEG%2FdlIIK28%2BH8A%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1268653992/291f94424686cc9349718dda8646/trmnl-outlook-calendar-plugin.png?expires=1743477300&signature=519acfc6d3ead73c02d69e3c83c7b9d12d8778def466d3c80df5ac29a64ebf71&req=dSIhHs97nohWW%2FMW1HO4zU0x7DrQZHyk4C62wOdJ1CvwHQOQjYYutAFor7VD%0AlCWRCEG%2FdlIIK28%2BH8A%3D%0A)

**Step 2 - Connect Outlook Calendar**
-------------------------------------

**Note**: _Enabling this plugin requires publishing your Outlook calendar to an anonymized "ICS" style format. This is similar to publishing an unlisted YouTube video or "view with link" permission Google Docs file. If your calendar has sensitive data you may limit the published permissions to only expose timestamps, not event details._

First log in to your Outlook email at [outlook.office365.com](https://outlook.office365.com)
. Visit your calendar on the left side navigation, then click the settings gear cog in the top right corner.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1268644107/3d6c1b4e471501b168d6b7a61aaf/outlook-calendar-view.png?expires=1743477300&signature=bfda4be251155a41443321c9201d3520e930893b468561378f160fc6e82dbf14&req=dSIhHs96mYBfXvMW1HO4zbOR6tfCwErGtrNwrcetoqDakpq4qNSpgWpUsoGX%0AvOnr%2FldkFjbb4hIEtbk%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1268644107/3d6c1b4e471501b168d6b7a61aaf/outlook-calendar-view.png?expires=1743477300&signature=bfda4be251155a41443321c9201d3520e930893b468561378f160fc6e82dbf14&req=dSIhHs96mYBfXvMW1HO4zbOR6tfCwErGtrNwrcetoqDakpq4qNSpgWpUsoGX%0AvOnr%2FldkFjbb4hIEtbk%3D%0A)

Click the "Shared calendars" link, then underneath the "Publish a calendar" heading you can select a calendar + set permissions.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1268644689/1546a677f4f832a57e894f04b345/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=ed49ce3e1d7d858e65455602564e1f27e11e8c0bc39eb2bfcccdb987b3f96dd2&req=dSIhHs96mYdXUPMW1HO4zfkQuR84cIOutAq%2BQM2teSC3sC6MoaVOa%2BUq7Y9P%0AnHl%2BUj23K04Zp9oogY4%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1268644689/1546a677f4f832a57e894f04b345/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=ed49ce3e1d7d858e65455602564e1f27e11e8c0bc39eb2bfcccdb987b3f96dd2&req=dSIhHs96mYdXUPMW1HO4zfkQuR84cIOutAq%2BQM2teSC3sC6MoaVOa%2BUq7Y9P%0AnHl%2BUj23K04Zp9oogY4%3D%0A)

Click Publish, then click to copy the 2nd link labeled ICS.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1268647467/2f614244b0e6eb8a6ed36330ab78/outlook-calendar-published-ics-link.png?expires=1743477300&signature=090b2eec3bb3f99338a7a3b739d388ac8c56ef0b52c9a3572b29f9c4a7268374&req=dSIhHs96moVZXvMW1HO4za57PBlL%2F2gI%2Bk2hiyyN6LbqwcmQ286rhsEWuAfE%0AXW9RRlui4j%2FjMFDEK4M%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1268647467/2f614244b0e6eb8a6ed36330ab78/outlook-calendar-published-ics-link.png?expires=1743477300&signature=090b2eec3bb3f99338a7a3b739d388ac8c56ef0b52c9a3572b29f9c4a7268374&req=dSIhHs96moVZXvMW1HO4za57PBlL%2F2gI%2Bk2hiyyN6LbqwcmQ286rhsEWuAfE%0AXW9RRlui4j%2FjMFDEK4M%3D%0A)

**Troubleshooting**

If you don't see the ability to Share or Publish a calendar, first make sure that calendar sharing is enabled at the administrator level. The following view is accessible from your Office 356 admin area:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1274966999/ce6848a648120379361b6ae0e95a/office-365-admin-sharing-settings.png?expires=1743477300&signature=ff123e976247878dabd47b4c46ced345e957b9bcb4c25f40ba6b422fef984b6a&req=dSIgEsB4m4hWUPMW1HO4zYbXxgVRUFlyZsZRkP7aGvGhOyyhSa82hMJFCHr8%0AwlbwKv6inER8JcTxnKc%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1274966999/ce6848a648120379361b6ae0e95a/office-365-admin-sharing-settings.png?expires=1743477300&signature=ff123e976247878dabd47b4c46ced345e957b9bcb4c25f40ba6b422fef984b6a&req=dSIgEsB4m4hWUPMW1HO4zYbXxgVRUFlyZsZRkP7aGvGhOyyhSa82hMJFCHr8%0AwlbwKv6inER8JcTxnKc%3D%0A)

After confirming that users may share their calendars, retry the beginning of Step 2 above.

**Step 3 - Configure Plugin**
-----------------------------

Back inside TRMNL, paste your published calendar link into the ICS input field.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1274965109/98d3cbff2dc82797032bd507e551/outlook-calendar-ics.png?expires=1743477300&signature=49202ad35a474abc3bc75129049d14ba8a7becc7d9ff45347d69f2e5088dbfcf&req=dSIgEsB4mIBfUPMW1HO4zeerngq16Q7gFdJD5zBr00Tsmm2aBF9TyLGOR7iZ%0AHMZniFR%2BY292FlhvO90%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1274965109/98d3cbff2dc82797032bd507e551/outlook-calendar-ics.png?expires=1743477300&signature=49202ad35a474abc3bc75129049d14ba8a7becc7d9ff45347d69f2e5088dbfcf&req=dSIgEsB4mIBfUPMW1HO4zeerngq16Q7gFdJD5zBr00Tsmm2aBF9TyLGOR7iZ%0AHMZniFR%2BY292FlhvO90%3D%0A)

Next you may set a few preferences.

**Time Format**

24 hours vs 12 hour (AM/PM) style.

**Include Description**

If "Yes," a truncated preview of the event's description field will be shown beneath the event title. Note that on the "default" Layout (explained below), setting this option to "No" will ~double the number of events shown thanks to saved space.

**First Day of Week**

Applies only to the "month" view. Similar to native Outlook Calendar (month view), this allows you to set which day of the week is represented by the first column, furthest to the left. Defaults to Sunday.

**Ignored Phrases**

Supports a list of words that will be used to ignore events based on title or description content.

**Layout**

*   Default (upcoming events for today, tomorrow, next day)
    
*   Week (5-7 days upcoming)
    
*   Month (this calendar month)
    

Note that only "Week" and "Month" layouts support multi-day events, but every layout supports all-day events.

**Example** - Week layout with multi-day event ("Michael OOO")

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1268641947/975784ce19c21471b61c23b53fe3/trmnl-google-calendar-week-mode.png?expires=1743477300&signature=1adc02de9a6586c728662cb380d75dcca246405e58b21c6770850a45b473ca8d&req=dSIhHs96nIhbXvMW1HO4za4Z2lUj%2BJWNLyn4J%2FcdpoO8RKMiEAFMyMrJUBe0%0AJfrNQ%2FPtuve7KJpyEDk%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1268641947/975784ce19c21471b61c23b53fe3/trmnl-google-calendar-week-mode.png?expires=1743477300&signature=1adc02de9a6586c728662cb380d75dcca246405e58b21c6770850a45b473ca8d&req=dSIhHs96nIhbXvMW1HO4za4Z2lUj%2BJWNLyn4J%2FcdpoO8RKMiEAFMyMrJUBe0%0AJfrNQ%2FPtuve7KJpyEDk%3D%0A)

**Example** - Default layout with all-day event ("Michael OOO")

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1268641949/9ff6ebc26b61de3ebf3315364ec5/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=c39380e7ff7ffe4e5fc28c8d8843602b6ae4782714b3f25bf35223deea1ccde1&req=dSIhHs96nIhbUPMW1HO4zW7SFfc9T2AJnaH9YEp%2FVsVFXgD5jsrKWPSg39dY%0A3k4BGNkBHD5DhYVAzgo%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1268641949/9ff6ebc26b61de3ebf3315364ec5/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=c39380e7ff7ffe4e5fc28c8d8843602b6ae4782714b3f25bf35223deea1ccde1&req=dSIhHs96nIhbUPMW1HO4zW7SFfc9T2AJnaH9YEp%2FVsVFXgD5jsrKWPSg39dY%0A3k4BGNkBHD5DhYVAzgo%3D%0A)

**Example** - Month layout with multi-day event:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1268641948/4e26e6aa3efbcf6f298b23afaaf4/trmnl-google-calendar-month-example.png?expires=1743477300&signature=c0cc702325265dc17245eabdaf5ef9cc19b44913918f8424b92fc70ad7f58b64&req=dSIhHs96nIhbUfMW1HO4zfU4qi8IuCqK5ldPeuR%2Brf8b0ANfj4ZTRlOwB%2BL3%0AUX%2BKJXv4KbcpKZhedeE%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1268641948/4e26e6aa3efbcf6f298b23afaaf4/trmnl-google-calendar-month-example.png?expires=1743477300&signature=c0cc702325265dc17245eabdaf5ef9cc19b44913918f8424b92fc70ad7f58b64&req=dSIhHs96nIhbUfMW1HO4zfU4qi8IuCqK5ldPeuR%2Brf8b0ANfj4ZTRlOwB%2BL3%0AUX%2BKJXv4KbcpKZhedeE%3D%0A)

**Step 4 - You're Done!**
-------------------------

Based on your device's refresh settings, you'll begin seeing Outlook Calendar events very soon.

Note: while we fetch data according to your refresh interval, TRMNL only generates new screen renders if the data fetched contains changes. Thus setting your layout to "Default" (which shows 2-3 days) but updating an event 4+ days in the future will not trigger a screen refresh.

Stay focused.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

# Screenshot | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_500c135310)

[](#h_c6336d48ce)

[All Collections](/en/)

[Plugins](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820559-plugins)

Screenshot

Capture any web page.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 2 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_500c135310)

[](#h_c6336d48ce)

With the Screenshot plugin you can take a snapshot of any public web page, with any type of content. This could be a CCTV video feed, sports scores, or your child's lunch menu.

Step 1 - Visit the Screenshot plugin
------------------------------------

Inside TRMNL, navigate to Plugins > Screenshot.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1303298107/41496724566070fedde711e0907a/trmnl-screenshot-plugin.png?expires=1743477300&signature=5ec0f97bcb9c54103cd7440bba4ff314d24a65a9bf9ee15526d0d6739ba0ea2f&req=dSMnFct3lYBfXvMW1HO4zWYRKotRlJVeMrudOJ0gAjVGv0W1vXj0hTQ6miEn%0A0oN6cCLhzH9AcBcDPUg%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1303298107/41496724566070fedde711e0907a/trmnl-screenshot-plugin.png?expires=1743477300&signature=5ec0f97bcb9c54103cd7440bba4ff314d24a65a9bf9ee15526d0d6739ba0ea2f&req=dSMnFct3lYBfXvMW1HO4zWYRKotRlJVeMrudOJ0gAjVGv0W1vXj0hTQ6miEn%0A0oN6cCLhzH9AcBcDPUg%3D%0A)

First provide a website URL:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1303298293/3d62e38bed8fd60b7863266c68da/screenshot-plugin-url.png?expires=1743477300&signature=3f6f3df66b4b8d52f97c4341bccd0be4c1dd34238931413eb13a1d88c595d27b&req=dSMnFct3lYNWWvMW1HO4zRCDrMVY7CloubIkiPblxp3XQmwIaA07nshjuJMn%0A9NqFlBAAEmZ0jDHhVCQ%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1303298293/3d62e38bed8fd60b7863266c68da/screenshot-plugin-url.png?expires=1743477300&signature=3f6f3df66b4b8d52f97c4341bccd0be4c1dd34238931413eb13a1d88c595d27b&req=dSMnFct3lYNWWvMW1HO4zRCDrMVY7CloubIkiPblxp3XQmwIaA07nshjuJMn%0A9NqFlBAAEmZ0jDHhVCQ%3D%0A)

Next, optionally add Header values in case the website needs to be authenticated.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1354106208/e4fb13881640fc02a86aa17b2a18/trmnl-screenshot-plugin-http-headers.png?expires=1743477300&signature=856daafeb52635806c50f3c9e8094ea3ecec328e1a9422f48c55dcc995d86baa&req=dSMiEsh%2Bm4NfUfMW1HO4zW461IKm%2BwSHn%2FovC2qzO4mTFSA6rgyJCg3mWwZh%0Ai2zCdVkCxjK7mnAkYTg%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1354106208/e4fb13881640fc02a86aa17b2a18/trmnl-screenshot-plugin-http-headers.png?expires=1743477300&signature=856daafeb52635806c50f3c9e8094ea3ecec328e1a9422f48c55dcc995d86baa&req=dSMiEsh%2Bm4NfUfMW1HO4zW461IKm%2BwSHn%2FovC2qzO4mTFSA6rgyJCg3mWwZh%0Ai2zCdVkCxjK7mnAkYTg%3D%0A)

Assign header key/values with = and separate them with `&`. So `authorization=bearer xxx&content-type=application/json` becomes:  
​

{  
  "authorization":"bearer xxx",  
  "content-type":"application/json"  
}

If a key/value requires an `=` sign in the value, for example `bearer jwt==`, simply encode it as `%3D`, so `bearer%20jwt%3D%3D`.

Finally, give your Screenshot plugin instance a name and click save.

Step 2 - You're Done!
---------------------

Based on your desired refresh settings, TRMNL will begin generating screenshots with this URL.

**Troubleshooting**

_The website doesn't look the same as in my browser._

*   The TRMNL display resolution is 800x480. In your browser (Chrome/Firefox) hold down shift+ctrl+c (Windows) or shift+cmd+c (Mac) to enter the Inspector mode. Here you can change the viewport to 800x480 to simulate how TRMNL will see the contents.
    

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1303298459/304ed0604c823e82ed122e738476/trmnl-screenshot-page-size-inspector.png?expires=1743477300&signature=1a005bd40a7be8f3eb3c0bc642b0c61b1080745c6d1374c407643445ba93861b&req=dSMnFct3lYVaUPMW1HO4zYcrGJ%2B3IpBVbViyGyNH4jjvmwiA1%2BGhNC41a6M8%0AyBCLTu9RcaH0aD54luU%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1303298459/304ed0604c823e82ed122e738476/trmnl-screenshot-page-size-inspector.png?expires=1743477300&signature=1a005bd40a7be8f3eb3c0bc642b0c61b1080745c6d1374c407643445ba93861b&req=dSMnFct3lYVaUPMW1HO4zYcrGJ%2B3IpBVbViyGyNH4jjvmwiA1%2BGhNC41a6M8%0AyBCLTu9RcaH0aD54luU%3D%0A)

_The website styling is broken_.

*   TRMNL does not visit this website directly and take a screenshot. Instead, we copy/paste the page's HTML contents into a new browser, then screenshot that result. This HTML will include references to CSS and JavaScript, which in most cases allows the page to be recreated anywhere.
    
*   In some cases, however, the web page may references CSS (styling) via relative links such as `"/styles.css"` instead of absolute links like `"https://some-website.com/styles.css"` .
    
*   For this situation, TRMNL attempts to convert all relative URLs for CSS + JavaScript to a full URL, granting our generated browser the context it needs to find your styling and interactive elements. This is not a perfect solution however.
    
*   If you have control over the web page you are screenshotting, we suggest ensuring that styles and other externally included libraries are available with absolute URLs instead of relative paths.
    

_Images don't load._

*   Similar to our note above on relative vs absolute content paths, TRMNL needs embedded images to point to a full URL. So if your web page has an "<img>" tag with a source attribute such as "photo.jpg", TRMNL cannot determine which URL this photo should be loaded from.
    
*   While TRMNL attempts to find the image on your website URLs server, this is not a perfect solution.
    
*   Image "src" attributes need to contain absolute paths to ensure accuracy during screenshot generation.
    

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

# GitHub Contributors | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

GitHub Contributors

Summarized committer progress.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 4 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_b1aaa4db1c)

[](#h_b56f42d829)

[](#h_268e1840b5)

For a quick snapshot of your team's interactions with a given repository, the GitHub Contributors plugin can be set up in just a couple minutes.

**Step 1 - Visit the GitHub Contributors plugin**
-------------------------------------------------

Inside TRMNL, navigate to Plugins > GitHub Contributors.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1303317277/84f49f32672d3fc584c10ce1eeaa/trmnl-github-contributors-plugin.png?expires=1743477300&signature=e75ae9c4f97b3aba9e1ad78f2c5ecd6aa2571b7563e9d7eb460e3de65b394074&req=dSMnFcp%2FmoNYXvMW1HO4zUNnLHx0IXAiBGSQQS%2BJBHrXN10pV0x43%2FjPv0qh%0AmHKd4h8W4wSqnh5y9dw%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1303317277/84f49f32672d3fc584c10ce1eeaa/trmnl-github-contributors-plugin.png?expires=1743477300&signature=e75ae9c4f97b3aba9e1ad78f2c5ecd6aa2571b7563e9d7eb460e3de65b394074&req=dSMnFcp%2FmoNYXvMW1HO4zUNnLHx0IXAiBGSQQS%2BJBHrXN10pV0x43%2FjPv0qh%0AmHKd4h8W4wSqnh5y9dw%3D%0A)

**Step 2 - Configure Plugin**
-----------------------------

First provide the repository you'd like to monitor, along with a "Fine Grained Access Token" from your GitHub account.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1303318645/bc0a6c505ecf93fa154a3fc65467/trmnl-github-contributor-fields.png?expires=1743477300&signature=3a3ca7e87a590b00e5ace8b0be3cc2b6122e3b34d4029916a7e027bc30391cd3&req=dSMnFcp%2FlYdbXPMW1HO4zeUdffhfMXw7wuXwySmS5VYIoBqgrjHNQUAfpeeq%0AF0HoNtHaPQWd3mi3sQM%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1303318645/bc0a6c505ecf93fa154a3fc65467/trmnl-github-contributor-fields.png?expires=1743477300&signature=3a3ca7e87a590b00e5ace8b0be3cc2b6122e3b34d4029916a7e027bc30391cd3&req=dSMnFcp%2FlYdbXPMW1HO4zeUdffhfMXw7wuXwySmS5VYIoBqgrjHNQUAfpeeq%0AF0HoNtHaPQWd3mi3sQM%3D%0A)

This access token only needs the "Read Repository Metadata" scope and can be created here:

[https://github.com/settings/tokens?type=beta](https://github.com/settings/tokens?type=beta)

After generation your GitHub should look like this:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1303319304/9b2d8003df6e30a320661ad86dc8/github-fine-token-creation.png?expires=1743477300&signature=68db2e098c86a26481d953cf24805b81d36441f969ad49a25b0c9ca34f718ccf&req=dSMnFcp%2FlIJfXfMW1HO4zbnI5FX3swN8zSrS7Av7wES6jLfRfrrbOpfxpxuB%0ARwR8LXIm1lU9FCipy7o%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1303319304/9b2d8003df6e30a320661ad86dc8/github-fine-token-creation.png?expires=1743477300&signature=68db2e098c86a26481d953cf24805b81d36441f969ad49a25b0c9ca34f718ccf&req=dSMnFcp%2FlIJfXfMW1HO4zbnI5FX3swN8zSrS7Av7wES6jLfRfrrbOpfxpxuB%0ARwR8LXIm1lU9FCipy7o%3D%0A)

The access token will be visible only once, at the top of this screen. Provide it inside TRMNL and click Save.

**Step 3 - You're Done!**
-------------------------

Based on your device's refresh settings, you'll begin seeing contributor stats very soon.

Stay focused.  
​

# Importing and exporting private plugins | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_4112dcb4f0)

[](#h_beb59a12f0)

[](#h_8082721aed)

[](#h_581fb988f0)

[All Collections](/en/)

[Plugins](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820559-plugins)

Importing and exporting private plugins

You worked hard developing your plugin - now share it!

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 2 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_4112dcb4f0)

[](#h_beb59a12f0)

[](#h_8082721aed)

[](#h_581fb988f0)

There's a rich ecosystem of user-developed plugins outside of our [official integrations](https://usetrmnl.com/integrations)
, and it's very simple to share and utilize these handcrafted private plugins.

We've developed a standard ZIP file format that plugin developers (dare we say, artisans) can follow. It conveniently combines plugin settings, custom fields, and markup into one archive.

Exporting a private plugin
--------------------------

Exporting is as simple as clicking **Export** on the settings page for the specific plugin. A ZIP file will be downloaded with the entire contents of your plugin, including its settings, custom fields, and markup.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1377194969/89b08c4d39a1014ad64edf1f9fd7/CleanShot+2025-02-12+at+09_26_20%402x.png?expires=1743477300&signature=9513126730f0a59af54f3c4e3069c56009a32e6008819d3d2f34185a8e4e9611&req=dSMgEch3mYhZUPMW1HO4zUUmIaEY15ZDg1PAG6xJOOY0HdrOS2aI06WXaakj%0AM2EZAxRrhE4vhS%2FYL3k%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1377194969/89b08c4d39a1014ad64edf1f9fd7/CleanShot+2025-02-12+at+09_26_20%402x.png?expires=1743477300&signature=9513126730f0a59af54f3c4e3069c56009a32e6008819d3d2f34185a8e4e9611&req=dSMgEch3mYhZUPMW1HO4zUUmIaEY15ZDg1PAG6xJOOY0HdrOS2aI06WXaakj%0AM2EZAxRrhE4vhS%2FYL3k%3D%0A)

Importing a private plugin
--------------------------

On the [Private Plugin settings page](https://usetrmnl.com/plugin_settings?keyname=private_plugin)
, simply click **Import new** and select the ZIP file to import. A new plugin will automatically be created and added to your playlist.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1377198793/970119152304656587d6f3eb8646/CleanShot+2025-02-12+at+09_28_31%402x.png?expires=1743477300&signature=18cdb498fd3e1d55b4e4cf281b6b7a648d4cdee665bce12f260724ab51c87f10&req=dSMgEch3lYZWWvMW1HO4zSF992onISPtYV8ksikdQtNgDZQ3773bmEW9X3gC%0A19z%2F%2Fe2KFjbf%2FRM4Yj8%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1377198793/970119152304656587d6f3eb8646/CleanShot+2025-02-12+at+09_28_31%402x.png?expires=1743477300&signature=18cdb498fd3e1d55b4e4cf281b6b7a648d4cdee665bce12f260724ab51c87f10&req=dSMgEch3lYZWWvMW1HO4zSF992onISPtYV8ksikdQtNgDZQ3773bmEW9X3gC%0A19z%2F%2Fe2KFjbf%2FRM4Yj8%3D%0A)

Plugin ZIP file contents
------------------------

The ZIP archive of a private plugin contains the following flat list of files (no subdirectories):

settings.yml  
full.liquid               
half\_horizontal.liquid  
half\_vertical.liquid  
quadrant.liquid 

`settings.yml` is required.

The `.liquid` files correspond to the individual [Liquid HTML templates](https://docs.usetrmnl.com/go/private-plugins/templates)
 for each viewport. The maximum template file size is 1 MB.

settings.yml
------------

See [this article](https://intercom.help/trmnl/en/articles/10513740-custom-plugin-form-builder)
 for details on configuring `custom_fields`.

\---  
\# required:  
name: My Awesome Plugin  
strategy: polling         # polling | webhook | static  
refresh\_interval: 60      # minutes; 15 | 60 | 360 | 720 | 1440  
  
\# polling strategy only:  
polling\_url: https://example.com  
polling\_headers: ''  
polling\_verb: GET               # GET | POST  
  
\# static strategy only:  
static\_data: '{"foo": "bar"}'   # JSON string  
  
\# generic options:  
no\_screen\_padding: 'no'         # 'no' | 'yes' (quotes are necessary!)  
dark\_mode: 'no'                 # 'no' | 'yes' (quotes are necessary!)  
  
\# custom plugin form fields (optional, see docs):  
custom\_fields:  
\- keyname: units  
  name: Units  
  field\_type: select  
  options:  
  - Metric  
  - Imperial  

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

# Compare custom plugin types | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_f0839e6230)

[](#h_408c8fe817)

[](#h_864a583072)

[](#h_5fd8956c0d)

[](#h_531f88b37b)

[All Collections](/en/)

[Plugins](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820559-plugins)

Compare custom plugin types

There are several ways to write a custom plugin - which is right for your application?

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 2 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_f0839e6230)

[](#h_408c8fe817)

[](#h_864a583072)

[](#h_5fd8956c0d)

[](#h_531f88b37b)

From easiest to hardest:

|     |     |     |     |     |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|     | **Public** | **Server required?** | **OAuth required?** | **Language** |
| **Private Plugin** | no  | no  | no  | [Liquid](https://docs.usetrmnl.com/go/private-plugins/templates) |
| **Recipe** | yes | no  | no  | [Liquid](https://docs.usetrmnl.com/go/private-plugins/templates) |
| **Screenshot** | no  | yes | no  | any |
| **Public Plugin** | yes | yes | yes | any |
| **BYOS** | no  | yes | no  | any |

Private Plugin
--------------

The simplest way to write a custom plugin is as a [Private Plugin](https://intercom.help/trmnl/en/articles/9510536-private-plugins)
. Feed it data via HTTP polling or a webhook, design a beautiful dashboard with our [UI framework](https://usetrmnl.com/framework/)
, and we handle the rest.

While private plugins are not publicly listed in the TRMNL directory, they can be conveniently shared with others by [exporting](https://intercom.help/trmnl/en/articles/10542599-importing-and-exporting-private-plugins)
.

For inspiration, check out the list of [awesome community plugins](https://github.com/usetrmnl/plugins)
.

Recipe
------

Recipes are simply private plugins that have been approved by the TRMNL team to be listed publicly. As recipe master, any changes you make will be automatically propagated to others who have installed your recipe.

Learn more about [building and submitting recipes](https://intercom.help/trmnl/en/articles/10122094-plugin-recipes)
.

Screenshot
----------

Another way to get custom content to a TRMNL is to leverage the [Screenshot plugin](https://intercom.help/trmnl/en/articles/10302121-screenshot)
. Write and host your own web app that serves up a TRMNL-friendly web page, and the Screenshot plugin will periodically poll your app to generate screen images.

Public Plugin
-------------

A public plugin is the most capable - and the most complex - custom plugin type. You provide a web application with an OAuth2 authentication flow, per-user setting management, and generated markup. TRMNL servers will periodically poll the application to generate images for the device.

Learn how to [build and submit a public plugin](https://docs.usetrmnl.com/go/plugin-marketplace/introduction)
.

BYOS
----

For complete control over your TRMNL hardware, you can [Bring Your Own Server](https://docs.usetrmnl.com/go/diy/byos)
. This capability bypasses all plugin functionality provided above.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

---
