# Fastmail Calendar | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_5dcc42048e)

[](#h_2a21c29c63)

[](#h_a62e236032)

[](#h_6b10229053)

[All Collections](/en/)

[Plugins](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820559-plugins)

Fastmail Calendar

Know what's on your schedule.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated this week

Table of contents

[](#h_5dcc42048e)

[](#h_2a21c29c63)

[](#h_a62e236032)

[](#h_6b10229053)

Connecting your Fastmail Calendar to TRMNL takes just a few seconds.

**Step 1 - Visit the Fastmail Calendar Plugin**
-----------------------------------------------

Inside TRMNL, navigate to Plugins > Fastmail Calendar.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1309302016/7071d89009920f92ddc3e45cb6b9/trmnl-fastmail-calendar-plugin.png?expires=1743477300&signature=5444ae52339f65ed8ebc1ff2e87945dfe8724ca0bb219af371de71847bd29bd7&req=dSMnH8p%2Bn4FeX%2FMW1HO4zR6BXqasNMNh%2F0Ndrk%2B5gI9rDz6rmLRmIK317UYi%0AYingcPZ6GL2Fzskdz2E%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1309302016/7071d89009920f92ddc3e45cb6b9/trmnl-fastmail-calendar-plugin.png?expires=1743477300&signature=5444ae52339f65ed8ebc1ff2e87945dfe8724ca0bb219af371de71847bd29bd7&req=dSMnH8p%2Bn4FeX%2FMW1HO4zR6BXqasNMNh%2F0Ndrk%2B5gI9rDz6rmLRmIK317UYi%0AYingcPZ6GL2Fzskdz2E%3D%0A)

**Step 2 - Connect Fastmail Calendar**
--------------------------------------

**Note**: _Enabling this plugin requires publishing your Fastmail calendar to an anonymized "ICS" style format. This is similar to publishing an unlisted YouTube video or "view with link" permission Google Docs file. If your calendar has sensitive data you may limit the published permissions to only expose timestamps, not event details._

Inside Fastmail, navigate to Settings > Calendar. Beside the calendar you wish to integrate with TRMNL, click the Edit & Share button.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1309298292/b5333575c9acd9bf6b156be24ac4/fastmail-calendar-sharing-example.png?expires=1743477300&signature=3f7c70cf959560d989d62c7b919924fa37cfcbb648f1f5cbd2959fcd7d8f05d2&req=dSMnH8t3lYNWW%2FMW1HO4zexTpmSFk2tOEJ4Ij1dKy4p0EMKq6zaL%2B07kp2Cl%0AX8ZBwqlLds10LLyyLjY%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1309298292/b5333575c9acd9bf6b156be24ac4/fastmail-calendar-sharing-example.png?expires=1743477300&signature=3f7c70cf959560d989d62c7b919924fa37cfcbb648f1f5cbd2959fcd7d8f05d2&req=dSMnH8t3lYNWW%2FMW1HO4zexTpmSFk2tOEJ4Ij1dKy4p0EMKq6zaL%2B07kp2Cl%0AX8ZBwqlLds10LLyyLjY%3D%0A)

In the **Publish** section and click the toggle button next to Full event details or Free/busy information, depending on what information you wish to share. ([source](https://www.fastmail.help/hc/en-us/articles/360060590793-Calendar-sharing)
)

Click "Copy to clipboard" below this long URL.

**Step 3 - Configure Plugin**
-----------------------------

Back inside TRMNL, paste your published calendar link into the ICS input field. Important: replace the "webcal" text with "https" so your full URL looks like `https://user.fm/calendar/v1-....`.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1309254989/12ed03b21313c38bad3b8b612033/outlook-calendar-ics.png?expires=1743477300&signature=e952f0eeb79b40da506e364be3213e1645e88838b614fb0d929fb58350afdb3e&req=dSMnH8t7mYhXUPMW1HO4zRRil5K4H2YEpK8V8mYyppdBdRkywyqg2nZW%2Fna%2F%0ACL2dTEJ6FlkLKCTYl8w%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1309254989/12ed03b21313c38bad3b8b612033/outlook-calendar-ics.png?expires=1743477300&signature=e952f0eeb79b40da506e364be3213e1645e88838b614fb0d929fb58350afdb3e&req=dSMnH8t7mYhXUPMW1HO4zRRil5K4H2YEpK8V8mYyppdBdRkywyqg2nZW%2Fna%2F%0ACL2dTEJ6FlkLKCTYl8w%3D%0A)

Next you may set a few preferences.

**Time Format**

24 hours vs 12 hour (AM/PM) style.

**Include Description**

If "Yes," a truncated preview of the event's description field will be shown beneath the event title. Note that on the "default" Layout (explained below), setting this option to "No" will ~double the number of events shown thanks to saved space.

**First Day of Week**

Applies only to the "month" view. Tis allows you to set which day of the week is represented by the first column, furthest to the left. Defaults to Sunday.

**Ignored Phrases**

Supports a list of words that will be used to ignore events based on title or description content.

**Layout**

*   Default (upcoming events for today, tomorrow, next day)
    
*   Week (5-7 days upcoming)
    
*   Month (this calendar month)
    

Note that only "Week" and "Month" layouts support multi-day events, but every layout supports all-day events.

**Example** - Week layout with multi-day event ("Michael OOO")

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1309254986/ba9f12a8d7f59af871d70f9fa6fd/trmnl-google-calendar-week-mode.png?expires=1743477300&signature=5796af8201ae26586db4b829ab3ebc165dbb7c65368beb83298b88b74a7d68a2&req=dSMnH8t7mYhXX%2FMW1HO4zYOwo2%2Fgu10sFtxwEAWkiHE5sQP07HZQjANZAij4%0ATeexDctq6dP24r%2BtoRs%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1309254986/ba9f12a8d7f59af871d70f9fa6fd/trmnl-google-calendar-week-mode.png?expires=1743477300&signature=5796af8201ae26586db4b829ab3ebc165dbb7c65368beb83298b88b74a7d68a2&req=dSMnH8t7mYhXX%2FMW1HO4zYOwo2%2Fgu10sFtxwEAWkiHE5sQP07HZQjANZAij4%0ATeexDctq6dP24r%2BtoRs%3D%0A)

**Example** - Default layout with all-day event ("Michael OOO")

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1309254985/ad37544e88a0bf8d47f8ae4187bb/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=f5268b4241ce0628c916769aa1d7bf2302606c8506fcb293319015c62975d94a&req=dSMnH8t7mYhXXPMW1HO4zdkQH1%2BYSy0Y6bGUSgLaYFTOAhRYyxyuH%2BZOpCPK%0ASq1QvzSEneBUtd6VRq4%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1309254985/ad37544e88a0bf8d47f8ae4187bb/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=f5268b4241ce0628c916769aa1d7bf2302606c8506fcb293319015c62975d94a&req=dSMnH8t7mYhXXPMW1HO4zdkQH1%2BYSy0Y6bGUSgLaYFTOAhRYyxyuH%2BZOpCPK%0ASq1QvzSEneBUtd6VRq4%3D%0A)

**Example** - Month layout with multi-day event:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1309254988/ada78f4dba493527a556e203e7db/trmnl-google-calendar-month-example.png?expires=1743477300&signature=186f5e4effa07e6407258f5d15f402f128dea6106cbe1b24dd6114fdcfdb1f36&req=dSMnH8t7mYhXUfMW1HO4zUr6fT4MLkspSkDVqs4eiVmXvl7ZJq8s4mNErqjC%0AfaWUYSsJmvUuKzxA9tU%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1309254988/ada78f4dba493527a556e203e7db/trmnl-google-calendar-month-example.png?expires=1743477300&signature=186f5e4effa07e6407258f5d15f402f128dea6106cbe1b24dd6114fdcfdb1f36&req=dSMnH8t7mYhXUfMW1HO4zUr6fT4MLkspSkDVqs4eiVmXvl7ZJq8s4mNErqjC%0AfaWUYSsJmvUuKzxA9tU%3D%0A)

**Step 4 - You're Done!**
-------------------------

Based on your device's refresh settings, you'll begin seeing Fastmail Calendar events very soon.

Note: while we fetch data according to your refresh interval, TRMNL only generates new screen renders if the data fetched contains changes. Thus setting your layout to "Default" (which shows 2-3 days) but updating an event 4+ days in the future will not trigger a screen refresh.

Stay focused.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

# Alias Plugin | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_3c78692475)

[](#h_e087776f9e)

[](#h_2a312aef61)

[All Collections](/en/)

[Plugins](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820559-plugins)

Alias Plugin

Fetch encrypted content from any origin server.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over a week ago

Table of contents

[](#h_3c78692475)

[](#h_e087776f9e)

[](#h_2a312aef61)

Advanced TRMNL users who can generate screens themselves, can make use of our Alias plugin.

As the name indicates, this plugin simply passes along your own (hosted) image to your TRMNL device. This may sound similar to our Image Display plugin, but with one key difference: Alias lets you encrypt + decrypt the content, making it impossible for TRMNL to know what's being displayed.

**How it works**
----------------

TRMNL expects image content to be accessible over the internet / home-network. This image content may then be plugged into the TRMNL web application in either plain text or encrypted format.

The diagram below explains how each of the Alias plugin strategies differ.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1405932721/466e4b48f1b6a64677806197d324/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=611f44627156d572207ae9f696035f4a5c8654c7218b6f09967bea112633ae7c&req=dSQnE8B9n4ZdWPMW1HO4zVN1njb1IpJo7W2g9QveEBgQGuSMjreRGVPt7teB%0ATG3KfvYwEIvFbaav8Wc%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1405932721/466e4b48f1b6a64677806197d324/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=611f44627156d572207ae9f696035f4a5c8654c7218b6f09967bea112633ae7c&req=dSQnE8B9n4ZdWPMW1HO4zVN1njb1IpJo7W2g9QveEBgQGuSMjreRGVPt7teB%0ATG3KfvYwEIvFbaav8Wc%3D%0A)

**Getting started**
-------------------

To set up an Alias plugin, first provide the absolute URL of your image.

Make sure the image is Bitmap (bmp3), 800x480 pixels, 1-bit sRGB 2c, and of size 48062B (exact). [See here](https://docs.usetrmnl.com/go/diy/byod-s)
 for a hint on generating this format with ImageMagick.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1405945732/3edb0b165d114e6c119c71ffda20/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=7bdee9b4f0c23c283b2bae263442fd950bc51060a928326c103aa7821b531710&req=dSQnE8B6mIZcW%2FMW1HO4zeq45XeyHJ2V9xzpjwqPMRnLR%2F36isfi7aQqUANN%0A%2B7QM37GAkbZD0MHGS1k%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1405945732/3edb0b165d114e6c119c71ffda20/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=7bdee9b4f0c23c283b2bae263442fd950bc51060a928326c103aa7821b531710&req=dSQnE8B6mIZcW%2FMW1HO4zeq45XeyHJ2V9xzpjwqPMRnLR%2F36isfi7aQqUANN%0A%2B7QM37GAkbZD0MHGS1k%3D%0A)

**Type - Plain Text**

When your TRMNL device requests content from your Alias plugin instance, TRMNL will respond with the data you provided in the TRMNL web application. For example, `https://yourwebserver.com/image1.bmp` as per the screenshot above.

**Type - Encrypted**

For an alias with type Encrypted, encrypt your image\_url using <TBD> algorithm.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1405951354/2af38f5cabaa8b46469f602077e8/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=8e9de05dcef6c323359f25dc21be30a7f503054b655382bd8f11def83d5f936a&req=dSQnE8B7nIJaXfMW1HO4zY%2BaoUt0jnEW0g2SPolM7bZaxeXXNoynAm29KkUn%0AjAhjJwfbjqxgoZ0djIQ%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1405951354/2af38f5cabaa8b46469f602077e8/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=8e9de05dcef6c323359f25dc21be30a7f503054b655382bd8f11def83d5f936a&req=dSQnE8B7nIJaXfMW1HO4zY%2BaoUt0jnEW0g2SPolM7bZaxeXXNoynAm29KkUn%0AjAhjJwfbjqxgoZ0djIQ%3D%0A)

Next, provide a decryption key to your TRMNL device via the captive WiFi portal. You can instantiate WiFi pairing mode by holding the boot button on the back of your TRMNL for 5-6 seconds, then letting go, while the device is turned on.

Your TRMNL device will store this decryption key onboard, and never share it over the internet.

**Putting it all together**
---------------------------

The Alias plugin provides a secure way to generate and consume content without sharing any information with the TRMNL servers, while still leveraging the convenience and power of the TRMNL web application.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

# Nextcloud Calendar | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Nextcloud Calendar

Know what's on your schedule.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated this week

Table of contents

[](#h_afd0056e0c)

[](#h_849963f256)

[](#h_1fd00278c7)

[](#h_cda014d0b9)

Connecting your Nextcloud Calendar to TRMNL takes just a few seconds.

**Step 1 - Visit the Nextcloud Calendar Plugin**
------------------------------------------------

Inside TRMNL, navigate to Plugins > Nextcloud Calendar.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1323893778/861832c7a56c196f0983c2982968/trmnl-nextcloud-calendar-plugin.png?expires=1743477300&signature=353f7142099f6645aa4908e2d14b5f0cdb1a451cf95f1cfd97a65a2f198d2391&req=dSMlFcF3noZYUfMW1HO4zeK1s95TFSJ4j4y51dIVgsHE9c6UwffjyZrI0Inw%0AphBMVe9EkS71XlHyyo4%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1323893778/861832c7a56c196f0983c2982968/trmnl-nextcloud-calendar-plugin.png?expires=1743477300&signature=353f7142099f6645aa4908e2d14b5f0cdb1a451cf95f1cfd97a65a2f198d2391&req=dSMlFcF3noZYUfMW1HO4zeK1s95TFSJ4j4y51dIVgsHE9c6UwffjyZrI0Inw%0AphBMVe9EkS71XlHyyo4%3D%0A)

**Step 2 - Connect Nextcloud Calendar**
---------------------------------------

**Note**: _Enabling this plugin requires publishing your Nextcloud calendar to an anonymized "ICS" style format. This is similar to publishing an unlisted YouTube video or "view with link" permission Google Docs file. If your calendar has sensitive data you may limit the published permissions to only expose timestamps, not event details._

Inside your Nextcloud Calendar, open the share menu and click the "+" next to the "Share link" option ([source](https://docs.nextcloud.com/server/19/user_manual/pim/calendar.html#publishing-a-calendar)
).

Copy this URL to your clipboard.

**Step 3 - Configure Plugin**
-----------------------------

Back inside TRMNL, paste your published calendar link into the ICS input field. Your full URL should begin with "https". You can attempt to visit it in your web browser -- it should download an ".ics" file to your computer which you can safely delete.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1323893212/d1f05602d03f23cbc311811b50e1/outlook-calendar-ics.png?expires=1743477300&signature=5b0b900e07e3e27b161eb2b7c98007ddda60e6bc63e2792c9d8484eafd9a8117&req=dSMlFcF3noNeW%2FMW1HO4zbfr1AZ43eYvXbj%2BeDLoJuaF8CZ%2FFROcw24OfpQk%0A1l9bMmYn0H%2FAwlTFKp8%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1323893212/d1f05602d03f23cbc311811b50e1/outlook-calendar-ics.png?expires=1743477300&signature=5b0b900e07e3e27b161eb2b7c98007ddda60e6bc63e2792c9d8484eafd9a8117&req=dSMlFcF3noNeW%2FMW1HO4zbfr1AZ43eYvXbj%2BeDLoJuaF8CZ%2FFROcw24OfpQk%0A1l9bMmYn0H%2FAwlTFKp8%3D%0A)

Next you may set a few preferences.

**Time Format**

24 hours vs 12 hour (AM/PM) style.

**Include Description**

If "Yes," a truncated preview of the event's description field will be shown beneath the event title. Note that on the "default" Layout (explained below), setting this option to "No" will ~double the number of events shown thanks to saved space.

**First Day of Week**

Applies only to the "month" view. Tis allows you to set which day of the week is represented by the first column, furthest to the left. Defaults to Sunday.

**Ignored Phrases**

Supports a list of words that will be used to ignore events based on title or description content.

**Layout**

*   Default (upcoming events for today, tomorrow, next day)
    
*   Week (5-7 days upcoming)
    
*   Month (this calendar month)
    

Note that only "Week" and "Month" layouts support multi-day events, but every layout supports all-day events.

**Example** - Week layout with multi-day event ("Michael OOO")

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1323893215/73db96468f5457af475ea6f4368b/trmnl-google-calendar-week-mode.png?expires=1743477300&signature=62cc247ae4083b9ec2af908ab76bd3d6e42fe54aa9d643a0d3bbf4afb630cc35&req=dSMlFcF3noNeXPMW1HO4zeYq9Hmt%2BlGMROV%2Fdo46lpFhiMduOMW%2BywqN%2By0s%0ApfJvyxda1aK0Tz0TnRA%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1323893215/73db96468f5457af475ea6f4368b/trmnl-google-calendar-week-mode.png?expires=1743477300&signature=62cc247ae4083b9ec2af908ab76bd3d6e42fe54aa9d643a0d3bbf4afb630cc35&req=dSMlFcF3noNeXPMW1HO4zeYq9Hmt%2BlGMROV%2Fdo46lpFhiMduOMW%2BywqN%2By0s%0ApfJvyxda1aK0Tz0TnRA%3D%0A)

**Example** - Default layout with all-day event ("Michael OOO")

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1323893219/f8624712faa8499e1556fb9707ab/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=425af27998a28618c0764c32914407d1310cf169d7978800e1fe51d266ac850b&req=dSMlFcF3noNeUPMW1HO4zXPPN%2BHuxT60gHQ%2BhGj98qfgIlkhp2rXCm1DCbaF%0Av%2B30141HR4nDvVNpGCU%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1323893219/f8624712faa8499e1556fb9707ab/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=425af27998a28618c0764c32914407d1310cf169d7978800e1fe51d266ac850b&req=dSMlFcF3noNeUPMW1HO4zXPPN%2BHuxT60gHQ%2BhGj98qfgIlkhp2rXCm1DCbaF%0Av%2B30141HR4nDvVNpGCU%3D%0A)

**Example** - Month layout with multi-day event:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1323893218/a8c0f02b2dca36c3fee6b53cecea/trmnl-google-calendar-month-example.png?expires=1743477300&signature=fe8e097f6958314d6667338dc0619ae80870fe1a7a6276971b1dda19b7a113e2&req=dSMlFcF3noNeUfMW1HO4zSpuH6FrQDMKM4i0dF7PtKQ%2FiR7bfR6cfgfKSBio%0AWUgx2w7Ochidf2ew%2FMM%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1323893218/a8c0f02b2dca36c3fee6b53cecea/trmnl-google-calendar-month-example.png?expires=1743477300&signature=fe8e097f6958314d6667338dc0619ae80870fe1a7a6276971b1dda19b7a113e2&req=dSMlFcF3noNeUfMW1HO4zSpuH6FrQDMKM4i0dF7PtKQ%2FiR7bfR6cfgfKSBio%0AWUgx2w7Ochidf2ew%2FMM%3D%0A)

**Step 4 - You're Done!**
-------------------------

Based on your device's refresh settings, you'll begin seeing Nextcloud Calendar events very soon.

Note: while we fetch data according to your refresh interval, TRMNL only generates new screen renders if the data fetched contains changes. Thus setting your layout to "Default" (which shows 2-3 days) but updating an event 4+ days in the future will not trigger a screen refresh.

Stay focused.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

Tempest Weather Station

Dedicated e-ink screen for your local climate.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 2 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_ccb8a030af)

[](#h_76a25856ba)

[](#h_4a17c1a801)

[](#h_5eba78d3af)

Connecting your Tempest WeatherFlow device to TRMNL takes just a few seconds.

Step 1 - Visit the Tempest Weather Station plugin
-------------------------------------------------

Inside TRMNL, navigate to Plugins > Tempest Weather Station.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1360392682/53da199eaf8d988b344858e64ec0/tempest-eink-weather-plugin-trmnl.png?expires=1743477300&signature=b3a606bce4e1fe006927ec4e6010e6413c43d0c2afdc4f639fcb70f6acba012a&req=dSMhFsp3n4dXW%2FMW1HO4zfg2WL%2Fmfsm8pYDHzCjHYcaJkNMyzdk3JJ0FIbfo%0Aw%2FvFjB%2B3qnrp3DVKwn4%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1360392682/53da199eaf8d988b344858e64ec0/tempest-eink-weather-plugin-trmnl.png?expires=1743477300&signature=b3a606bce4e1fe006927ec4e6010e6413c43d0c2afdc4f639fcb70f6acba012a&req=dSMhFsp3n4dXW%2FMW1HO4zfg2WL%2Fmfsm8pYDHzCjHYcaJkNMyzdk3JJ0FIbfo%0Aw%2FvFjB%2B3qnrp3DVKwn4%3D%0A)

Click to "Connect with Tempest Weather Station" on the right side of the screen.

**Step 2 - Connect Tempest**
----------------------------

You'll be redirected to the tempestwx.com website. Log in and then approve TRMNL's data access request.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1347628324/17f54e631f34f4f706f11808aab8/tempest-oauth2-consent-screen.png?expires=1743477300&signature=bf3f4e5f18bd314f41198814d7da04a2abb449d7f17e39978c4af9d73965c3e2&req=dSMjEc98lYJdXfMW1HO4zfH5pV%2BwQlqIzfjHi6IfA9%2BYmxjvLaSN4U3TGklb%0AOYMWJPXs3z32f5Iij80%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1347628324/17f54e631f34f4f706f11808aab8/tempest-oauth2-consent-screen.png?expires=1743477300&signature=bf3f4e5f18bd314f41198814d7da04a2abb449d7f17e39978c4af9d73965c3e2&req=dSMjEc98lYJdXfMW1HO4zfH5pV%2BwQlqIzfjHi6IfA9%2BYmxjvLaSN4U3TGklb%0AOYMWJPXs3z32f5Iij80%3D%0A)

This is "read only" and will not modify any settings or stations on your account.

If for some reason the above screen does not appear, but instead yields "Unknown Application" like below, try switching to a desktop computer (if on a phone) or to Google Chrome (if on Safari).

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1374546645/0c93a1b57c0d7b126ecdc9730230/tempest-unknown-application.png?expires=1743477300&signature=009aa48c39d57a6d35139136f3de11fb14c2bfc79e1761b7c73b5d921186fe2b&req=dSMgEsx6m4dbXPMW1HO4zVXRT3P8247gthySaHXkMYFaNiSHJTqNGbmySd%2Bw%0A%2BDJykjFrccRgbgI9%2FBc%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1374546645/0c93a1b57c0d7b126ecdc9730230/tempest-unknown-application.png?expires=1743477300&signature=009aa48c39d57a6d35139136f3de11fb14c2bfc79e1761b7c73b5d921186fe2b&req=dSMgEsx6m4dbXPMW1HO4zVXRT3P8247gthySaHXkMYFaNiSHJTqNGbmySd%2Bw%0A%2BDJykjFrccRgbgI9%2FBc%3D%0A)

**Step 3 - Configure Plugin**
-----------------------------

Select which Tempest Station's weather data you want to display on your TRMNL device, as well as the measurement format for a few metrics.  
​

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1360392123/efbeb7bb012a9181d3a8f4dc8d1c/trmnl-tempest-weather-settings.png?expires=1743477300&signature=5daa5941378bf62b638f37e53fda36efb84b7f13621225d9839b4d86c5e6661f&req=dSMhFsp3n4BdWvMW1HO4zZIaoUb2P6FVBAS4eBhNpkI7iAKZS4UiTV6Ka8ha%0AAbRTUZz93QnCjpMOn1M%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1360392123/efbeb7bb012a9181d3a8f4dc8d1c/trmnl-tempest-weather-settings.png?expires=1743477300&signature=5daa5941378bf62b638f37e53fda36efb84b7f13621225d9839b4d86c5e6661f&req=dSMhFsp3n4BdWvMW1HO4zZIaoUb2P6FVBAS4eBhNpkI7iAKZS4UiTV6Ka8ha%0AAbRTUZz93QnCjpMOn1M%3D%0A)

If you'd like to capture weather from multiple stations, and perhaps combine it on a single screen, simply create multiple instances of this plugin and then [generate a Mashup](https://intercom.help/trmnl/en/articles/10168132-mashups)
 to see them all together.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1347634322/816c039e60f77a4d21f41004a239/atfdsbbcfhi97iqrzyfzunti4o55?expires=1743477300&signature=08f2b72a99ca0ad7db67ff8e91ecb23460e572a88b8f1dd753c587f01acab832&req=dSMjEc99mYJdW%2FMW1HO4zSEfDDP0ugK1O%2FaycVn%2F2IdeUKzSogQkOo4u902B%0A91mzGCTddO940RJjJ6E%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1347634322/816c039e60f77a4d21f41004a239/atfdsbbcfhi97iqrzyfzunti4o55?expires=1743477300&signature=08f2b72a99ca0ad7db67ff8e91ecb23460e572a88b8f1dd753c587f01acab832&req=dSMjEc99mYJdW%2FMW1HO4zSEfDDP0ugK1O%2FaycVn%2F2IdeUKzSogQkOo4u902B%0A91mzGCTddO940RJjJ6E%3D%0A)

In the example above, 2 stations in nearby locations are shown side by side.

**Step 4 - You're Done!**
-------------------------

Based on your device's refresh settings, you'll begin seeing Tempest Weather Station forecasts very soon.

Stay focused.

Did this answer your question?

# Custom plugin filters | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_bbc4b2f9f5)

[](#h_7946179100)

[](#h_1390794d23)

[](#h_e379e72cb3)

[All Collections](/en/)

[Plugins](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820559-plugins)

Custom plugin filters

Improve content formatting with Liquid and localizations.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 2 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_bbc4b2f9f5)

[](#h_7946179100)

[](#h_1390794d23)

[](#h_e379e72cb3)

Below is a growing list of custom (fancy) mutations available to Private Plugins, whose variable interpolation is powered by the open source [Liquid library](https://github.com/Shopify/liquid)
.

Getting started with Liquid
---------------------------

To get started quickly with `{{ liquid }}` flavor variable notation, create a Private Plugin inside TRMNL, visit the Markup Editor, then follow along our Liquid 101 guide:

[https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/articles/10671186-liquid-101](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/articles/10671186-liquid-101)

To understand how Liquid words under the hood, check out the official docs:

[https://rubydoc.info/gems/liquid](https://rubydoc.info/gems/liquid)

To parse and re-format Liquid-injected data, see the "Filters" section of this cheat sheet:

[https://github.com/shopify/liquid/wiki/liquid-for-designers#standard-filters](https://github.com/shopify/liquid/wiki/liquid-for-designers#standard-filters)

TRMNL custom filters
--------------------

Given our web application is built in Ruby/Rails, we're able to extend the default Liquid library with custom filters using the following strategy:

[https://github.com/shopify/liquid/wiki/liquid-for-programmers#extending-liquid](https://github.com/shopify/liquid/wiki/liquid-for-programmers#extending-liquid)

We currently offer the following extensions:  
​

{{ 1234 | number\_with\_delimiter }}  # => 1,234  
  
\# custom delimiter (default is comma)  
{{ 1234 | number\_with\_delimiter: '.' }} # => 1.234  
{{ 1000000 | number\_with\_delimiter: ' ' }} # => 1 000 000  
  
\# optional 2nd arg separates whole number from fractional value  
{{ 1234.57 | number\_with\_delimiter: ' ', ',' }} # => 1 234,57  
  
\# currency handling  
{{ 10420 | number\_to\_currency }} # => $10,420.00  
{{ 152350.69 | number\_to\_currency: '£' }} # => £152,350.69  
  
\# optional 2nd + 3rd args delimit + separate  
{{ 1234.57 | number\_to\_currency: '£', '.', ',' }} # => £1.234,57  
  
\# pluralize + inflect/humanize  
{{ "book" | pluralize: 1 }} # => 1 book  
{{ "book" | pluralize: 2 }} # => 2 books  
{{ "octopus" | pluralize: 3 }} # => 3 octopi  
{{ "person" | pluralize: 4 }} # => 4 people  
  
\# convert a variable to JSON  
{{ my\_var | json }} => {"foo":"bar"}

Note: named parameters are not supported by the Liquid library, so you must supply all preceding arguments in the case that you want to override a 2nd+ parameter default.

TRMNL also offers **localization filters**.

First, `l_date` localizes a date (object or string) to a friendlier format with [strftime syntax](https://www.foragoodstrftime.com/)
.

{{ '2025-01-11' | l\_date: '%y %b' }} # => 25 Jan  
  
\# with a specific locale, ex: Korean  
{{ '2025-01-11' | l\_date: '%y %b', 'ko' }} # => 25 1월  
  
\# with the user's locale; good for published Plugin Recipes  
{{ '2025-01-11' | l\_date: '%y %b', trmnl.user.locale }} # => 25 1월

Next, `l_word` translates common words to another language. Contribute more [here](https://github.com/usetrmnl/localizations)
.

<p>{{ "today" | l\_word: 'es-ES' }}</p> # => hoy  
  
{% assign day = "tomorrow" %}  
<p>{{ day | l\_word: trmnl.user.locale }}</p> # => 내일

Troubleshooting
---------------

Combining filters with our Framework handlers, for example [Value Formatting](https://usetrmnl.com/framework/format_value)
, may produce unexpected results. For example:

<span class="value value--xlarge value--tnums" data-value-type="number">  
  {{ 10420.00 | number\_to\_currency }}  
</span>

Will yield $10,420 without `.00` trailing decimal places, because `value--tnums` attempts to simplify whole numbers.

Adding more custom filters
--------------------------

Email [\[email protected\]](/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#2450414549645157415056494a480a474b49)
 or hop inside our Developer-only Discord > #Plugins channel to request additional filters or arguments.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

---

# Parcel | TRMNL Help Center

Parcel

Track package deliveries

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 2 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_9e3156ffa6)

[](#h_89c38aefe6)

[](#h_f9f095fd68)

[](#h_15e74e811e)

The [Parcel](https://parcelapp.net/)
 app for iOS and macOS conveniently tracks packages across many different delivery providers.

Connecting the plugin to your Parcel account only takes a few steps.

A premium subscription to Parcel is required.

Step 1 - Visit the Parcel Plugin
--------------------------------

Inside TRMNL, navigate to Plugins > Parcel.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1400194731/546539679885055242b6619b226a/CleanShot+2025-02-27+at+14_30_03%402x.png?expires=1743477300&signature=8979edd10d84049517c409fa84dd2587ec9cf4dd002e151038263280b20772e3&req=dSQnFsh3mYZcWPMW1HO4zWIegNXx17%2BgYK7lkPP41t6lmd05gvsM1acrpngo%0AlyuCPtMOqhwuvO%2BxnGA%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1400194731/546539679885055242b6619b226a/CleanShot+2025-02-27+at+14_30_03%402x.png?expires=1743477300&signature=8979edd10d84049517c409fa84dd2587ec9cf4dd002e151038263280b20772e3&req=dSQnFsh3mYZcWPMW1HO4zWIegNXx17%2BgYK7lkPP41t6lmd05gvsM1acrpngo%0AlyuCPtMOqhwuvO%2BxnGA%3D%0A)

Step 2 - Log in to Parcel Web Access
------------------------------------

In a new tab, visit [https://web.parcelapp.net/](https://web.parcelapp.net/)
 and follow the instructions to sign in.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1400112654/0aa43be30c28b278cf075ca36d10/CleanShot+2025-02-27+at+13_41_58%402x.png?expires=1743477300&signature=e7cb10d106689a1eabd432fe212630e7fb3e7288049db06dcad5139eb422c2a8&req=dSQnFsh%2Fn4daXfMW1HO4zdYagVLbSzZoYYL6Q8HhsfpI75otY5Mw0U9M1zPE%0ArbuhwUXJoieEpgVli78%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1400112654/0aa43be30c28b278cf075ca36d10/CleanShot+2025-02-27+at+13_41_58%402x.png?expires=1743477300&signature=e7cb10d106689a1eabd432fe212630e7fb3e7288049db06dcad5139eb422c2a8&req=dSQnFsh%2Fn4daXfMW1HO4zdYagVLbSzZoYYL6Q8HhsfpI75otY5Mw0U9M1zPE%0ArbuhwUXJoieEpgVli78%3D%0A)

Step 3 - Generate the API Key
-----------------------------

Click on "API" to bring up the dialog box. Then click "Create a Key" to generate a new API key. Copy the API key into the clipboard.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1400125575/59992a502ceb633c3647e2bd5575/CleanShot+2025-02-27+at+13_47_30%402x.png?expires=1743477300&signature=754205ffee172f40b503ddaff98b07f5f4b1555da7f9f30b70c7bf29f21f6123&req=dSQnFsh8mIRYXPMW1HO4zdiYugan2gl7KNRaCQT%2FBF4O1Ol4OqGSWL2RI4w8%0AR2uNHZ1RKGKbIsgwwMo%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1400125575/59992a502ceb633c3647e2bd5575/CleanShot+2025-02-27+at+13_47_30%402x.png?expires=1743477300&signature=754205ffee172f40b503ddaff98b07f5f4b1555da7f9f30b70c7bf29f21f6123&req=dSQnFsh8mIRYXPMW1HO4zdiYugan2gl7KNRaCQT%2FBF4O1Ol4OqGSWL2RI4w8%0AR2uNHZ1RKGKbIsgwwMo%3D%0A)

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1400127330/bac66a7bbab40f184cd046161be6/CleanShot+2025-02-27+at+13_47_58%402x.png?expires=1743477300&signature=72c7f24952880fbaab97e4f3a982757b8628c486676bc0931a9faae90d4c5722&req=dSQnFsh8moJcWfMW1HO4zTqPH2x5gtKUW5U0QnD6hQqFPOxq8tQioVtR1Y%2BM%0AqZ37WGFXN2SIBmgplTw%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1400127330/bac66a7bbab40f184cd046161be6/CleanShot+2025-02-27+at+13_47_58%402x.png?expires=1743477300&signature=72c7f24952880fbaab97e4f3a982757b8628c486676bc0931a9faae90d4c5722&req=dSQnFsh8moJcWfMW1HO4zTqPH2x5gtKUW5U0QnD6hQqFPOxq8tQioVtR1Y%2BM%0AqZ37WGFXN2SIBmgplTw%3D%0A)

Step 4 - Configure Plugin
-------------------------

Back in the TRMNL dashboard, paste in the API key, and select what type of deliveries to display.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1400195353/46c0d2d7dd06cb8e9587c96ae98b/CleanShot+2025-02-27+at+14_30_39%402x.png?expires=1743477300&signature=bdc65ca26f5c32247c5594a487457650ea0454a429f0a1e97114815c1ae5a221&req=dSQnFsh3mIJaWvMW1HO4zYWhBnss6vZ1IV8m%2BmXv4TE9YzB2KGDcPtLXeSNA%0AjUnUllq5VRQncOThN5c%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1400195353/46c0d2d7dd06cb8e9587c96ae98b/CleanShot+2025-02-27+at+14_30_39%402x.png?expires=1743477300&signature=bdc65ca26f5c32247c5594a487457650ea0454a429f0a1e97114815c1ae5a221&req=dSQnFsh3mIJaWvMW1HO4zYWhBnss6vZ1IV8m%2BmXv4TE9YzB2KGDcPtLXeSNA%0AjUnUllq5VRQncOThN5c%3D%0A)

You're done!

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

# Apple Calendar | TRMNL Help Center

Apple Calendar

Know what's on your schedule.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated this week

Table of contents

[](#h_52c09d09bd)

[](#h_6f0d1dbfba)

[](#h_f4f62660ac)

[](#h_8aacec4e45)

Connecting your Apple Calendar to TRMNL takes just a few seconds.

**Step 1 - Visit the Apple Calendar Plugin**
--------------------------------------------

Inside TRMNL, navigate to Plugins > Apple Calendar.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1308298675/eef2da86b4339441e96589d28212/trmnl-apple-calendar-plugin.png?expires=1743477300&signature=11814b341d8a0d8756f370259f815736e1468466a550564d4b7fdc892971598e&req=dSMnHst3lYdYXPMW1HO4zc1bc1M4Qnyam8rDDaVe47zFzqUhMxlNl%2B2xSLaX%0Avmp6vr4KGk5bUjAceV8%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1308298675/eef2da86b4339441e96589d28212/trmnl-apple-calendar-plugin.png?expires=1743477300&signature=11814b341d8a0d8756f370259f815736e1468466a550564d4b7fdc892971598e&req=dSMnHst3lYdYXPMW1HO4zc1bc1M4Qnyam8rDDaVe47zFzqUhMxlNl%2B2xSLaX%0Avmp6vr4KGk5bUjAceV8%3D%0A)

**Step 2 - Connect Apple Calendar**
-----------------------------------

**Note**: _Enabling this plugin requires publishing your Apple calendar to an anonymized "ICS" style format. This is similar to publishing an unlisted YouTube video or "view with link" permission Google Docs file. If your calendar has sensitive data you may limit the published permissions to only expose timestamps, not event details._

First open your Apple Calendar client on your computer.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1308301059/837e44ebd8a14967aad48d8ff5b0/apple-calendar-left-navigation.png?expires=1743477300&signature=568e3365d9ebe464ca63ec5e16917274d339719c00f46aecc70fa7d6090c2cf6&req=dSMnHsp%2BnIFaUPMW1HO4zRE4hi4Ziz6uDCsS%2Fd378B4fEl2mmshx0dBdSE2F%0A2zL2fi5qLZ8w%2FTiXPp4%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1308301059/837e44ebd8a14967aad48d8ff5b0/apple-calendar-left-navigation.png?expires=1743477300&signature=568e3365d9ebe464ca63ec5e16917274d339719c00f46aecc70fa7d6090c2cf6&req=dSMnHsp%2BnIFaUPMW1HO4zRE4hi4Ziz6uDCsS%2Fd378B4fEl2mmshx0dBdSE2F%0A2zL2fi5qLZ8w%2FTiXPp4%3D%0A)

Ctrl-click on the calendar and check the Public Calendar box. After a moment (you may need to navigate away, then re-open this pane) a URL will appear below.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1308301491/843b66f140fae1bf0ff1827e080b/apple-calendar-public-calendar-enabled.png?expires=1743477300&signature=37b4d1827a1cb3be28b44ab09f29089aff8a33aa9db9ed72b1aa509a3b4b86a6&req=dSMnHsp%2BnIVWWPMW1HO4zX8VHuoPy2rilUcT9KD%2BsZHvLua7SB8Jtct8v188%0AW1QdxKrQceBn2Z8HbIc%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1308301491/843b66f140fae1bf0ff1827e080b/apple-calendar-public-calendar-enabled.png?expires=1743477300&signature=37b4d1827a1cb3be28b44ab09f29089aff8a33aa9db9ed72b1aa509a3b4b86a6&req=dSMnHsp%2BnIVWWPMW1HO4zX8VHuoPy2rilUcT9KD%2BsZHvLua7SB8Jtct8v188%0AW1QdxKrQceBn2Z8HbIc%3D%0A)

Copy this long URL value.

**Step 3 - Configure Plugin**
-----------------------------

Back inside TRMNL, paste your published calendar link into the ICS input field. Important: replace the "webcal" text with "https" so your full URL looks like `https://p44-caldav.icloud.com/published....`.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1308298414/7bc2902394d8211a93895570d471/outlook-calendar-ics.png?expires=1743477300&signature=732ff5057f8f54dff7299b6c1df544feb46f1eb60524c0b75e7e26838b39f71d&req=dSMnHst3lYVeXfMW1HO4zThSn729h857d2sJuz8dOGbd0aptsXCBh3hhR6Q%2F%0A9wP1QH7tQbjMXSLhkI8%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1308298414/7bc2902394d8211a93895570d471/outlook-calendar-ics.png?expires=1743477300&signature=732ff5057f8f54dff7299b6c1df544feb46f1eb60524c0b75e7e26838b39f71d&req=dSMnHst3lYVeXfMW1HO4zThSn729h857d2sJuz8dOGbd0aptsXCBh3hhR6Q%2F%0A9wP1QH7tQbjMXSLhkI8%3D%0A)

Next you may set a few preferences.

**Time Format**

24 hours vs 12 hour (AM/PM) style.

**Include Description**

If "Yes," a truncated preview of the event's description field will be shown beneath the event title. Note that on the "default" Layout (explained below), setting this option to "No" will ~double the number of events shown thanks to saved space.

**First Day of Week**

Applies only to the "month" view. Similar to native Outlook Calendar (month view), this allows you to set which day of the week is represented by the first column, furthest to the left. Defaults to Sunday.

**Ignored Phrases**

Supports a list of words that will be used to ignore events based on title or description content.

**Layout**

*   Default (upcoming events for today, tomorrow, next day)
    
*   Week (5-7 days upcoming)
    
*   Month (this calendar month)
    

Note that only "Week" and "Month" layouts support multi-day events, but every layout supports all-day events.

**Example** - Week layout with multi-day event ("Michael OOO")

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1308298417/dbc0841cf5d9669a90984702c9cc/trmnl-google-calendar-week-mode.png?expires=1743477300&signature=c0c56dd89283a7d529d94c2e73ff1243166f228e5ad64f16473eccb058c330ee&req=dSMnHst3lYVeXvMW1HO4zcqRWr4bdpSdwUeeM6sG1uXn66KxywYsf2PhQKAx%0AqfKwKFj8%2F7CRSoM5YAg%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1308298417/dbc0841cf5d9669a90984702c9cc/trmnl-google-calendar-week-mode.png?expires=1743477300&signature=c0c56dd89283a7d529d94c2e73ff1243166f228e5ad64f16473eccb058c330ee&req=dSMnHst3lYVeXvMW1HO4zcqRWr4bdpSdwUeeM6sG1uXn66KxywYsf2PhQKAx%0AqfKwKFj8%2F7CRSoM5YAg%3D%0A)

**Example** - Default layout with all-day event ("Michael OOO")

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1308298415/f6dfe9c4d612b9058780446b133d/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=d774d001ee6353414a99e6f2c4c6df5ca5ec641ad519daeaa40e92487cc54092&req=dSMnHst3lYVeXPMW1HO4zUgDArzL6rZApZBVB%2FVGVWNFXzol%2BWQAEaKgnzXY%0AxCO2AV6%2FbCACF1RdTi4%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1308298415/f6dfe9c4d612b9058780446b133d/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=d774d001ee6353414a99e6f2c4c6df5ca5ec641ad519daeaa40e92487cc54092&req=dSMnHst3lYVeXPMW1HO4zUgDArzL6rZApZBVB%2FVGVWNFXzol%2BWQAEaKgnzXY%0AxCO2AV6%2FbCACF1RdTi4%3D%0A)

**Example** - Month layout with multi-day event:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1308298419/deea0f97fbe778307c6489df51c5/trmnl-google-calendar-month-example.png?expires=1743477300&signature=4c26541edfa7a771a3c7065e694d2a0771ce46a8693033e8695c88ae30419e05&req=dSMnHst3lYVeUPMW1HO4zaC%2B%2FIcM7cYzaEobIRSdybrJKQENg8QWtLmp4n57%0AOQ1ruyvFloNCvG5z%2FDM%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1308298419/deea0f97fbe778307c6489df51c5/trmnl-google-calendar-month-example.png?expires=1743477300&signature=4c26541edfa7a771a3c7065e694d2a0771ce46a8693033e8695c88ae30419e05&req=dSMnHst3lYVeUPMW1HO4zaC%2B%2FIcM7cYzaEobIRSdybrJKQENg8QWtLmp4n57%0AOQ1ruyvFloNCvG5z%2FDM%3D%0A)

**Step 4 - You're Done!**
-------------------------

Based on your device's refresh settings, you'll begin seeing Apple Calendar events very soon.

Note: while we fetch data according to your refresh interval, TRMNL only generates new screen renders if the data fetched contains changes. Thus setting your layout to "Default" (which shows 2-3 days) but updating an event 4+ days in the future will not trigger a screen refresh.

Stay focused.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

# Custom plugin form builder | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_c77ca39ebe)

[](#h_98df974ac6)

[](#h_df4f3fd8e6)

[](#h_77cc4d0b70)

[](#h_db4dc8a5cf)

[All Collections](/en/)

[Plugins](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820559-plugins)

Custom plugin form builder

Create user-facing configuration fields in YAML.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 3 weeks ago

Table of contents

[](#h_c77ca39ebe)

[](#h_98df974ac6)

[](#h_df4f3fd8e6)

[](#h_77cc4d0b70)

[](#h_db4dc8a5cf)

If you're new to building plugins, see [Private Plugins](https://intercom.help/trmnl/en/articles/9510536-private-plugins)
 and [Public Plugins API Docs](https://docs.usetrmnl.com/go/plugin-marketplace/introduction)
.

Below is a guide to adding **user-facing form fields inside a Private Plugin or [Recipe](https://intercom.help/trmnl/en/articles/10122094-plugin-recipes)
.**

**How it works**
----------------

Step 1 - Plugin author (you) creates custom fields

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1367287123/83c1ef9708e957ef648c12dfa136/trmnl-custom-plugin-fields.png?expires=1743477300&signature=30f76eae6d843819c9c85813d555f14ba9a32c6f1edd8c3a9927e2ac2ceacd1d&req=dSMhEct2moBdWvMW1HO4zayKCIC0Ybz%2BwIxf1RkgSB1FQw2IKtRz%2BB%2FBvh2d%0Azkdo%2B73SwJIzSzBf2nE%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1367287123/83c1ef9708e957ef648c12dfa136/trmnl-custom-plugin-fields.png?expires=1743477300&signature=30f76eae6d843819c9c85813d555f14ba9a32c6f1edd8c3a9927e2ac2ceacd1d&req=dSMhEct2moBdWvMW1HO4zayKCIC0Ybz%2BwIxf1RkgSB1FQw2IKtRz%2BB%2FBvh2d%0Azkdo%2B73SwJIzSzBf2nE%3D%0A)

Step 2 - Plugin user (including you) can interact with rendered fields

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1367265600/58802f7035cdfad36d07fc21e609/trmnl-custom-field-example.png?expires=1743477300&signature=da613ae7a9d792b73eb7fd5227f07bf26406b89edce894e6e1082c30d7eacf1c&req=dSMhEct4mIdfWfMW1HO4zYmge8tlaXgJC0TU2WVM%2BgbDrWQlLqRHB2sjKUTV%0AAQOnDo4%2FFvDdwuSy%2Bfs%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1367265600/58802f7035cdfad36d07fc21e609/trmnl-custom-field-example.png?expires=1743477300&signature=da613ae7a9d792b73eb7fd5227f07bf26406b89edce894e6e1082c30d7eacf1c&req=dSMhEct4mIdfWfMW1HO4zYmge8tlaXgJC0TU2WVM%2BgbDrWQlLqRHB2sjKUTV%0AAQOnDo4%2FFvDdwuSy%2Bfs%3D%0A)

Step 3 - Provided values are accessible via author-defined key/value pairs inside the Markup Editor

{{ trmnl.plugin\_settings.custom\_fields\_values }}  
  
\# => { "password": "secret", "lookback\_period": "7" }

Let's begin!

**Supported field types**
-------------------------

Where possible, TRMNL follows [HTML5 input types](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn_web_development/Extensions/Forms/HTML5_input_types)
 to leverage native browser validations and UX features. Our current selection includes:

*   url
    
*   string
    
*   text (textarea)
    
*   code (like textarea, but monospace font)
    
*   number
    
*   password
    
*   date (M Y D)
    
*   time (HH:SS)
    
*   select (single or multi)
    
*   time\_zone
    
*   copyable (produces 'click to copy' button)
    

Coming soon:

*   radio (binary toggle)
    
*   email
    
*   xhrFetch (`select` field that fetches `<option>` values from external URL)
    

**Anatomy of a form field**
---------------------------

The following key/value pairs are available to all field types:

*   `keyname` - parameterized identifier, not user-facing, ex `user_email`
    
*   `field_type` - one of the above "type" values
    
*   `name` - field label
    
*   `description` - secondary field label, HTML-friendly
    
*   `help_text` - tertiary field label, HTML-friendly (optional)
    
*   `optional` - boolean; unless set to true, `required` will be added to HTML input (omit if field should be required)
    
*   `default` - value if input is left blank; must be a lowercase, parameterized version of one of the provided `options` values or will not be pre-chosen on `select` field type. example: "Upcoming Movies" option => `upcoming_movies` as `default`
    

The following key/value pairs are available for _some_ field types:

*   `rows` - number of visible rows on a `text` or `code` field
    
*   `options` - collection of option values for the `select` field
    
*   `placeholder` - example value if input is cleared; supported by `url`, `string`, `text`, `number`, `date`, `code`
    

When building a form field, only the following values are required:

*   keyname, name, field\_type
    

**Building form fields**
------------------------

Below are examples of every supported field type, which you may modify with optional parameters described above.

Note that every field must be indented 2 spaces and be preceded with a `-`, also called a [block sequence](https://www.tutorialspoint.com/yaml/yaml_collections_and_structures.htm)
.

**url**

\- keyname: url  
  field\_type: url  
  name: Web Address  
  description: URL of RSS Feed  
  placeholder: https://www.site.com/rss  
  help\_text: Please include http:// or https://

**string**

\- keyname: api\_key  
  field\_type: string  
  name: API Key  
  description: Account API Key  
  placeholder: sa\_api\_key\_qwerty

**text** (textarea)

\- keyname: prompt  
  field\_type: text  
  name: Prompt  
  description: Enter your prompt for Chat GPT to respond.  
  placeholder: Tell me a Dad Joke under 200 words.

**number**

\- keyname: retirement\_age  
  field\_type: number  
  placeholder: '65'  
  name: Retirement Age  
  description: At what age do you plan to retire?

**password**

\- keyname: password  
  field\_type: password  
  name: Password  
  description: Mobile app login password  
  placeholder: s3cret!

**code**

\- keyname: json\_query  
  field\_type: code  
  rows: 8  
  name: JSON Query  
  description: Provide a raw query  
  placeholder: |  
    { "cannot": "spare a square" }  
  help\_text: Learn how to do this <a href="https://jquery.com/" class="underline">here</a>.

**date**

\- keyname: start\_date  
  field\_type: date  
  placeholder: '2024-11-26'  
  name: Start Date  
  description: Provide your start date

When using the date field, rendered form will have a M/D/Y picker. However the value inside `{{ trmnl.plugin_settings.custom_fields_values }}` will be `YYYY-MM-DD`.

**time**

\- keyname: scroll\_time  
  field\_type: time  
  name: Fixed start time?  
  description: By default, the week's earliest event time will be used.  
  help\_text: Optional. Applies to week view only.

**select** (single, unified label/value option tags)

\- keyname: filter\_by  
  field\_type: select  
  options:  
  - Upcoming # value will be 'upcoming'  
  - Now Playing # value will be 'now\_playing'  
  default: now\_playing  
  name: Filter By  
  description: Select a movie type

  
​**select** (single, with separate label/value option tags)

\- keyname: lookback\_period  
  field\_type: select  
  options:  
  - One Week: 7  
  - Two weeks: 14  
  default: 14 # should be set to the value, not the label  
  name: Lookback Period

**select** (multi)

\- keyname: sales\_pipeline  
  field\_type: select  
  name: Pipeline Statuses  
  description: Select up to 3 statuses  
  options:  
  - 'Discovery'  
  - 'Pending'  
  - 'Closed-lost'  
  - 'Closed-won'  
  multiple: true

Note: if you create a `select` field that has options "Yes" and "No", and you want the default option to be "No," then you must wrap the default in quotes as "no" or it will be considered truthy. Example:

\- keyname: include\_description  
  field\_type: select  
  name: Include Description  
  description: Select up to 3 statuses  
  options:  
  - "Yes"  
  - "No"  
  default: "no" # unless wrapped in quotes, value will be true

**time\_zone**

\- keyname: time\_zone  
  field\_type: time\_zone  
  name: Time Zone  
  description: Where are you located?

**copyable**

\- keyname: webhook\_url  
  field\_type: copyable  
  name: Webhook URL  
  value: "https://vandelayindustries.com/hooks/IMPORTS\_EXPORTS"  
  description: "(Webhook strategy only) Paste this into your integration"

**Troubleshooting**
-------------------

**Form fields don't appear**

If your YAML cannot be parsed for any reason, it will be ignored and no errors will be returned.

Check your YAML syntax with a free online tool to ensure proper formatting before saving it in the Custom Fields code editor:

[https://yaml-online-parser.appspot.com/](https://yaml-online-parser.appspot.com/)

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

---

# How to set up a new device | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_21058be1e7)

[](#h_6e746a80e3)

[](#h_6c73d1c8ad)

[](#h_33338a5a39)

[](#h_281a621591)

[All Collections](/en/)

[General](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820478-general)

How to set up a new device

Unboxing and connecting TRMNL for the first time.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 5 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_21058be1e7)

[](#h_6e746a80e3)

[](#h_6c73d1c8ad)

[](#h_33338a5a39)

[](#h_281a621591)

Congrats on receiving your TRMNL! We're stoked to have you. If your box has a strange clear film accessory, [go here](https://intercom.help/trmnl/en/articles/10217443-applying-the-screen-anti-glare-protector)
.

When you take the device out of the box, it may already have content on the screen. This does not\* mean the device is turned on -- e-ink is cool like that.

**Step 1 - Turn on TRMNL**
--------------------------

Flip the power switch to ON from the back of your TRMNL device. After it wakes up and blinks a few times, your screen might look something like this:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246665300/5656dec928919129bc2e5e8da9a8/trmnl-setup-screen.jpeg?expires=1743477300&signature=6319480d6b65437c69252d4e733da93e066eeaed942f9d2b366054c8c29c6ef4&req=dSIjEM94mIJfWfMW1HO4zVNGUMqw7ECgv1UMN6K%2FhlV58KF4RF1njTePYfMe%0AlRlOprGjieZzsDp7j4Q%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246665300/5656dec928919129bc2e5e8da9a8/trmnl-setup-screen.jpeg?expires=1743477300&signature=6319480d6b65437c69252d4e733da93e066eeaed942f9d2b366054c8c29c6ef4&req=dSIjEM94mIJfWfMW1HO4zVNGUMqw7ECgv1UMN6K%2FhlV58KF4RF1njTePYfMe%0AlRlOprGjieZzsDp7j4Q%3D%0A)

If nothing happens when you turn on the device, the battery may be drained. In this case, plug TRMNL in with the included USB-C cable (if part of your order) and restart your device using the OFF/ON switch on the back.

**Step 2 - Connect to WiFi**
----------------------------

As the device screen says, use your phone or a nearby computer to find and connect to the WiFi network named "TRMNL," which will broadcast from your turned on device.

[![TRMNL device WiFi setup steps](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1131054590/ce4d66889f2a306cb58b32fd/setup_device_wifi.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=646f15f0a24a94657b4bca188d64c19c5f3f6ec5cdc36fcb16d5b2ee9ab44bfb&req=dSEkF8l7mYRWWfMW1HO4zdxLO9ETGZc76%2FsYHBAA3rY1onpbtbAjhlA%2BTDab%0A2tRjURzVKKNIJ32B6SQ%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1131054590/ce4d66889f2a306cb58b32fd/setup_device_wifi.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=646f15f0a24a94657b4bca188d64c19c5f3f6ec5cdc36fcb16d5b2ee9ab44bfb&req=dSEkF8l7mYRWWfMW1HO4zdxLO9ETGZc76%2FsYHBAA3rY1onpbtbAjhlA%2BTDab%0A2tRjURzVKKNIJ32B6SQ%3D%0A)

After connecting, a WiFi portal will appear like the middle screenshot above.

Wait a moment while TRMNL scans for available networks, or provide credentials into the SSID/Password box directly if your home/office network doesn't appear or is hidden. Finally, click Connect to share these credentials with your TRMNL device.

(_Your WiFi credentials are [never](https://docs.usetrmnl.com/go/how-it-works#opinionated-device-less-than-greater-than-server-relationship)
 sent to our servers_)

**Troubleshooting**

For suggestions to fix a few rare issues, see our [troubleshooting guide](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/articles/10193157-device-wifi-troubleshooting)
.

**Step 3 - Register your Device**
---------------------------------

After adding your WiFi credentials, TRMNL will restart and show a setup message.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1249374401/5d7025e935d56c50a964ac23ec43/trmnl-device-id-screen.jpeg?expires=1743477300&signature=4aeea00715bb9745afc2c4ef91a2f3a581ff5517fe0e436114208021fbb4796c&req=dSIjH8p5mYVfWPMW1HO4zaTe%2BGnsilRBG5MmOYA86TfNpZ4WvOE85rm8o1Gd%0Ay74QRHbZvOuO4HJhiVk%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1249374401/5d7025e935d56c50a964ac23ec43/trmnl-device-id-screen.jpeg?expires=1743477300&signature=4aeea00715bb9745afc2c4ef91a2f3a581ff5517fe0e436114208021fbb4796c&req=dSIjH8p5mYVfWPMW1HO4zaTe%2BGnsilRBG5MmOYA86TfNpZ4WvOE85rm8o1Gd%0Ay74QRHbZvOuO4HJhiVk%3D%0A)

If you don't have a TRMNL account yet (different from your online shopping profile), register at [https://usetrmnl.com/signup](https://usetrmnl.com/signup)
. You'll be asked for a Device ID, and in this input box provide the ID from your TRMNL's screen.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1070517969/ffbda6ba7baf74720f2833bf/TRMNL+device+registration.png?expires=1743477300&signature=88cc074b6ea131367feaf860a799643d3084703125c89e96b57d29dc4363c22b&req=dSAgFsx%2FmohZUPMW1HO4zfxnqtDJRyH%2B5vmU%2Fo2dhNE2TmF35D5pv0djUNiJ%0AZE9zSB8wusB951bLGNc%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1070517969/ffbda6ba7baf74720f2833bf/TRMNL+device+registration.png?expires=1743477300&signature=88cc074b6ea131367feaf860a799643d3084703125c89e96b57d29dc4363c22b&req=dSAgFsx%2FmohZUPMW1HO4zfxnqtDJRyH%2B5vmU%2Fo2dhNE2TmF35D5pv0djUNiJ%0AZE9zSB8wusB951bLGNc%3D%0A)

If you already have a TRMNL account, select Add New from the top-right dropdown picker while [logged in](https://usetrmnl.com/login)
.

**Step 4 - Connect Plugins**
----------------------------

From the TRMNL website, visit the Plugins directory and start connecting data you'd like to show on your device. After your first plugin is connected, you're ready to rock.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1070522209/85d1b9e85c33fbab3bf8ad56/TRMNL+plugins+directory.png?expires=1743477300&signature=9c532b215766722ecb4e2109ac8f0cc1cfb2943443ba1d2f2b6cae3d2f14156a&req=dSAgFsx8n4NfUPMW1HO4zd434yolHo71OrElWqMmkSHcwC10hE65%2FBY5YDH2%0AZJksT7p1feeTvxsvFjQ%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1070522209/85d1b9e85c33fbab3bf8ad56/TRMNL+plugins+directory.png?expires=1743477300&signature=9c532b215766722ecb4e2109ac8f0cc1cfb2943443ba1d2f2b6cae3d2f14156a&req=dSAgFsx8n4NfUPMW1HO4zd434yolHo71OrElWqMmkSHcwC10hE65%2FBY5YDH2%0AZJksT7p1feeTvxsvFjQ%3D%0A)

Simply restart your device by toggling it OFF/ON, or click the small button beneath the power switch to force refresh your display. This tells TRMNL to request content from our web application.

You can also set up a [special function](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/articles/9672080-special-functions)
, which is triggered by double clicking the button on the back of your TRMNL device.

**Step 5 - Enjoy!**
-------------------

TRMNL keeps you focused but informed, aware but not distracted, and in sync, async.

Feel free to modify the refresh rate, enable sleep mode, and more from the [Devices > Edit](https://usetrmnl.com/devices)
 page in your TRMNL account.

If you have questions about the setup process, email us at [\[email protected\]](/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#681c0d0905281d1b0d1c1a050604460b0705)
.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

[All Collections](/en/)

[General](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820478-general)

Special Functions

How to set up custom behaviors on your device.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 6 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_287acfcedb)

[](#h_2208ce73ce)

[](#h_2b0dc7e87a)

[](#h_22a3b7627e)

[](#h_5cfc4f2323)

[](#h_e4903e2a1f)

The back of your TRMNL device has an on/off switch, USB-C input, and multi functional "boot" button.

[![](https://trmnl.intercom-attachments-1.com/i/o/1128531399/d588c07f6106d21e95f28f7b/8a43fab09b1391e486f47759fe5cdd89_original.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=b9e7c0f20e3def397929cfad954670386de24507feb00bc10d969de8a2e91785&req=dSElHsx9nIJWUPMW1HO4zY1sq3DlckJLWXpc155ibEZNcOHgV46c%2FtC3oHk7%0ANVt3uYsMcbsylwHs1aQ%3D%0A)](https://trmnl.intercom-attachments-1.com/i/o/1128531399/d588c07f6106d21e95f28f7b/8a43fab09b1391e486f47759fe5cdd89_original.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=b9e7c0f20e3def397929cfad954670386de24507feb00bc10d969de8a2e91785&req=dSElHsx9nIJWUPMW1HO4zY1sq3DlckJLWXpc155ibEZNcOHgV46c%2FtC3oHk7%0ANVt3uYsMcbsylwHs1aQ%3D%0A)

The boot button does 2 things by default:

1.  Skip to the next screen in your playlist (click)
    
2.  Reset WiFi credentials (hold for 5 seconds)
    

But you can program a 3rd function, attached to a "double-click" of this button, with any of the following behaviors.

**Identify**
------------

Triggers a simple identification screen to help you determine which device is which.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1128529296/77c4302dbf3c9543fdee782a/trmnl-identification-screen-example.png?expires=1743477300&signature=2ac34a4bd4bf250bad9c85fe6c4ad8f06b2dfd40e01f1d25bf2d652ece7d5b11&req=dSElHsx8lINWX%2FMW1HO4zXVYaJt31LbaeyExKIAcBGOlq2q9%2Fs7mz%2Fo1851r%0APf7GSRtPjRmQaq%2BQ3mU%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/1128529296/77c4302dbf3c9543fdee782a/trmnl-identification-screen-example.png?expires=1743477300&signature=2ac34a4bd4bf250bad9c85fe6c4ad8f06b2dfd40e01f1d25bf2d652ece7d5b11&req=dSElHsx8lINWX%2FMW1HO4zXVYaJt31LbaeyExKIAcBGOlq2q9%2Fs7mz%2Fo1851r%0APf7GSRtPjRmQaq%2BQ3mU%3D%0A)

This is helpful for customers with multiple devices who may not give them descriptive names, or who have their devices in the same room with a similar case color.

**Sleep**
---------

Puts your device to sleep for 8 hours. In the future you may be able to customize this sleep period length.

**Add WiFi**
------------

Instructs your device's firmware to activate the "TRMNL" WiFi portal so that you can connect to a new network, without resetting your existing credentials.

**Restart Playlist**
--------------------

Begins showing content from your Playlist at the top/first position. Think of this as an enhancement to the single-click "skip" feature, as it skips multiple screens all at once.

**Rewind**
----------

Goes back to the previously viewed screen. Helpful if you noticed something interesting just as your TRMNL device began showing new content.

**Send to me**
--------------

Sends yourself an email with the latest (current) device screen content. Helpful if you want to save/bookmark something for later but don't want to search for it in your Playlist history.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

# Frequently Asked Questions | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

[All Collections](/en/)

[General](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820478-general)

Frequently Asked Questions

Pricing, use cases, and more.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 3 months ago

**How much does TRMNL cost?**

Customers pay a 1-time fee to buy a device, then get lifetime access to software updates and plugins.

**Is there a recurring subscription fee?**

Nope. Buy a TRMNL device once, then use it free forever. Every device enables lifetime access to our web portal, but you can also leverage our open source platforms to point devices at your own servers if desired.

**How big is a TRMNL device?**

The screen is 7.5 inches diagonal and the full device is around 4.5x7 inches. It sits at a 15 degree angle on your desk or counter, or can be hung directly on a wall.

**What can I do with TRMNL?**

We provide dozens of native plugins for personal and professional users. Whether you want to view your calendar, upcoming weather, business KPIs, or just a random Wikipedia article, TRMNL's growing plugin directory has everything you need.

Users with our developer mode enabled may also build plugins, either for themselves or publicly listed in our directory.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

# How refresh rates work | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_64269842e4)

[](#h_6bc016b817)

[](#h_854b46ae51)

[](#h_7094fc0e29)

[](#h_8943c22098)

[](#h_ead6e5ebd0)

[](#h_f97632e351)

[All Collections](/en/)

[General](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820478-general)

How refresh rates work

Understanding when and how your device content is updated.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over a month ago

Table of contents

[](#h_64269842e4)

[](#h_6bc016b817)

[](#h_854b46ae51)

[](#h_7094fc0e29)

[](#h_8943c22098)

[](#h_ead6e5ebd0)

[](#h_f97632e351)

As illustrated in our [architecture docs](https://docs.usetrmnl.com/go/how-it-works)
, TRMNL has 1 paradigm that underscores how content is displayed on your device. To summarize:

**Devices ping the TRMNL server. Not the other way around**.

Practically this means:

*   You cannot click a button on our website and 'force' new content to appear on your device. Your device must ask for it.
    
*   Your device will not "know" when new content has been synced, or new screen images have been generated. The device must ask for it.
    

Of course, it's natural to want to skip ahead to new content, or refresh a generated screen while you build custom plugins. So that is possible, but you'll leverage both the web interface and your device’s skip button to do it.

Here's more about how TRMNL refresh rates work.

1.  [Plugin (default) refresh rates](#h_64269842e4)
    
2.  [Overriding plugin refresh rates](#h_6bc016b817)
    
3.  [Device refresh rates](#h_854b46ae51)
    
4.  [Mashup refresh rates](#h_8943c22098)
    
5.  [Lazy refreshing device content](#h_7094fc0e29)
    
6.  [Determining "when" (hh:ss) a refresh occurs](#h_ead6e5ebd0)
    

Plugin refresh rates
--------------------

Every native plugin has a default refresh rate. For example our "Days left this year" refresh just 1x per day, because it would be pointless to re-generate the same screen more often.

But our GitHub Commit Graph updates every 30 minutes. The random Wikipedia article generator refreshes every 4 hours. And our Product Hunt plugin refreshes hourly.

These are just defaults, however. You are welcome to override them on your own account.

Overriding a plugin refresh rate
--------------------------------

After setting up a plugin in your TRMNL account, you'll notice a refresh rate dropdown on the right side of the settings page:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1248056985/d66d55bdcaaef9235370db6e0394/trmnl-plugin-refresh-rate-dropdown.png?expires=1743476400&signature=fd8817c5f497d74cf232ba1c1489bf8f0d34256408db9ecd40d65285a06bb2ee&req=dSIjHsl7m4hXXPMW1HO4zT99S0fqBvjvAUBm%2FWKn8hxvKHtcwtWcycoBUbBk%0AqvCAxg3bUdMaKT9WJvA%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1248056985/d66d55bdcaaef9235370db6e0394/trmnl-plugin-refresh-rate-dropdown.png?expires=1743476400&signature=fd8817c5f497d74cf232ba1c1489bf8f0d34256408db9ecd40d65285a06bb2ee&req=dSIjHsl7m4hXXPMW1HO4zT99S0fqBvjvAUBm%2FWKn8hxvKHtcwtWcycoBUbBk%0AqvCAxg3bUdMaKT9WJvA%3D%0A)

Depending on which plugin you're editing, this dropdown will have different options.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1248058098/2596a3abb5483fb86c7819f63867/image.png?expires=1743476400&signature=a94f7a94e40bdf921daa57c19587fbc1451bde93b21ac680148ce7d4fe3d38b3&req=dSIjHsl7lYFWUfMW1HO4zdWo%2FZTbSLuF7U7xz7vipZgx5PXDtrypvj5HH2o2%0AANycCADkHTc1cubWaV4%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1248058098/2596a3abb5483fb86c7819f63867/image.png?expires=1743476400&signature=a94f7a94e40bdf921daa57c19587fbc1451bde93b21ac680148ce7d4fe3d38b3&req=dSIjHsl7lYFWUfMW1HO4zdWo%2FZTbSLuF7U7xz7vipZgx5PXDtrypvj5HH2o2%0AANycCADkHTc1cubWaV4%3D%0A)

When it's time to generate new screen content, **TRMNL will follow whichever refresh rate is faster** -- yours, or the system default.

However, **you cannot refresh faster than the system allows**. So for example, since Shopify has a default of every 10 mins, you can refresh every 10, 15, etc minutes. But since our RSS plugin refreshes by default every 60 mins, you cannot refresh faster than 60 minutes.

We are open to decreasing refresh intervals on a case by case basis. These limitations are simply in place to predict our server resource requirements and maintain free, lifetime usage for all of your TRMNL devices.

Device refresh rates
--------------------

Adjacent to your plugin setting refresh rate is your parent device refresh rate.

You might configure a few plugins to refresh every 15 minutes, but if your device refreshes every 30 minutes, then you will typically see content that was generated 30+ minutes ago. Simply multiply the number of items in your Playlist by your device refresh rate (editable from your [Devices tab](https://usetrmnl.com/devices)
), and the result is the delay (in minutes) between content _generation_ and content _display_.

This generation process happens independently of your device pinging the TRMNL server. In other words, **TRMNL does not sync content + generate graphics on-demand when your device pings the server**. This would be too compute intensive, drain your device battery (to stay awake for fresh content), and have unexpected results in the case that new content doesn't exist or the 3rd party plugin is nonresponsive.

Lazy refreshing device content
------------------------------

Above we describe how plugin content may be requested every _N_ minutes, based on your preferences on the plugin settings screen.

However it is possible (and common) that when TRMNL requests new data from a plugin, the content has not changed since our last request.

For example, if your connect Google Calendar and set it to refresh every 15 minutes, TRMNL will sync new calendar events every 15 minutes. But if the events returned to us have the same title, description, start/end date, and so on, TRMNL will not generate a new graphic for your device.

Here's an example of that in action.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1260961312/ccb513bf104185c72c2fd9c163ea/trmnl-sync-vs-refresh.png?expires=1743476400&signature=3e9d880d0c78739fa1cdfeca27aed0f70fa5a53bb7949b7bfea08935b4f918b7&req=dSIhFsB4nIJeW%2FMW1HO4zbBbWX64A33x3DHjad0tw0v9%2BNK%2FoJ8cLu5k4Luw%0ALFce2IAqmtXB74jwA6g%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1260961312/ccb513bf104185c72c2fd9c163ea/trmnl-sync-vs-refresh.png?expires=1743476400&signature=3e9d880d0c78739fa1cdfeca27aed0f70fa5a53bb7949b7bfea08935b4f918b7&req=dSIhFsB4nIJeW%2FMW1HO4zbBbWX64A33x3DHjad0tw0v9%2BNK%2FoJ8cLu5k4Luw%0ALFce2IAqmtXB74jwA6g%3D%0A)

This is due to TRMNL's timer-based content generation strategy. Every minute, TRMNL loops through every plugin that is due to be refreshed and attempts to create new screens.

This screen creation attempt has 2 steps:

1.  **sync** new content
    
2.  **render** new content
    

When TRMNL syncs content, but it matches the previously synced content (from 15+ minutes ago), the system stops and does not re-_render_ (generate a screen) the content.

This saves compute power, without changing your device experience. You will still see the calendar graphic if it's up next on your Playlist, but the image itself may have been generated 15+ minutes ago.

Thus on your plugin settings screen might look like this:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1248114594/548dd1b933c9868512e82042333d/trmnl-plugin-refresh-compute-savings.png?expires=1743476400&signature=64998b04c800eb4695f19405f1aa84014fbc7b5a97dd7e959d54a0f6d1d68d0a&req=dSIjHsh%2FmYRWXfMW1HO4zcY%2FW2AyDQeZHGDSY%2B9r2O6LHD4P8nIcB7MUuq4K%0A9oSXJv7rxdI5a50gW9M%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1248114594/548dd1b933c9868512e82042333d/trmnl-plugin-refresh-compute-savings.png?expires=1743476400&signature=64998b04c800eb4695f19405f1aa84014fbc7b5a97dd7e959d54a0f6d1d68d0a&req=dSIjHsh%2FmYRWXfMW1HO4zcY%2FW2AyDQeZHGDSY%2B9r2O6LHD4P8nIcB7MUuq4K%0A9oSXJv7rxdI5a50gW9M%3D%0A)

Here we have a 1 hour refresh set on our Shopify plugin, but the "Refreshed" timestamp shows 6 hours ago. That implies we have not received a new order in 6 hours. But rest assured, TRMNL looks for new orders every hour based on our preferences.

**Mashup refresh rates**
------------------------

A Mashup is any combination of 2 or more plugins on a single screen, using one of these layouts (excluding the top left option):

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1248121901/ab258cadbdcd96ecbce9c513d33c/trmnl-mashup-layouts.png?expires=1743476400&signature=1572534bf17b01a6a3bb11f4672e685b3b5736cc050d2176c37152b885b9268c&req=dSIjHsh8nIhfWPMW1HO4zXlttbt1okEg8giUb3%2BGdHWwKaK2gY2%2BUZDBezqS%0A3SCFHSb1U7NdEfYFfZk%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1248121901/ab258cadbdcd96ecbce9c513d33c/trmnl-mashup-layouts.png?expires=1743476400&signature=1572534bf17b01a6a3bb11f4672e685b3b5736cc050d2176c37152b885b9268c&req=dSIjHsh8nIhfWPMW1HO4zXlttbt1okEg8giUb3%2BGdHWwKaK2gY2%2BUZDBezqS%0A3SCFHSb1U7NdEfYFfZk%3D%0A)

Since Mashups are composed of several underlying Playlist items (plugin settings), we sync new data for each of your plugin settings when generating new Mashup screens for your device.

Given the details mentioned previously regarding plugins refreshing at their own pace, independent of your device requesting new content, it may be the case that a given Mashup with (for example) 3 pieces of content will have 1 piece with a recent update, and other 2 pieces of content will be 15, 30, or more minutes old.

**Determining "when" a refresh occurs**
---------------------------------------

New screens are generated relative to the moment in time that you establish a refresh rate.

If you enable Google Calendar at 14:00 (2p) local time, for example, and the default refresh rate is 1x per day, then it will refresh daily at 14:00 your local time.

If you later change your Google Calendar plugin to refresh 4x /day, and you make this change at 18:00 (6p) local time, then new screens will be generated at 18:00, 00:00, 06:00, and 12:00 in your local time.

**In summary**
--------------

We're linking this help guide from a few places in-app to clarify how refreshing works, but the main points are:

1.  TRMNL's website does not 'ping' your device, only your device can ping the TRMNL website
    
2.  Your plugin <> device refresh intervals, when combined with our lazy loading generation strategy, may seem to indicate that plugins are not generating on time. But TRMNL does follow your timing preferences, with exceptions mentioned above.
    

If you have additional questions, send us an email or live chat at any time.

  
Stay focused.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

---

# International Customs / Duty Fees | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_55425057a9)

[](#h_ab67d33ef1)

[](#h_b5291235ad)

[](#h_5f6a830358)

[All Collections](/en/)

[General](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820478-general)

International Customs / Duty Fees

Pricing impact when buying TRMNL from abroad.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 2 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_55425057a9)

[](#h_ab67d33ef1)

[](#h_b5291235ad)

[](#h_5f6a830358)

TRMNL holds several EC licenses and is permitted to sell in many countries around the world.

As of this writing, all items are assembled + shipped from our office near Atlanta, Georgia, USA.

**Estimated duty fees**
-----------------------

For some customers abroad, our shipping origin has no effect beyond delivery times. For example, there are no import duty fees for customers in:

*   Australia
    
*   Hong Kong
    
*   New Zealand
    
*   Philippines
    
*   (+ several others)
    

But residents in _some_ countries are not so lucky. In our experience, here are estimated fees (USD) in a handful of popular TRMNL customer locations:

*   Canada, $13.50
    
*   Germany, $19
    
*   Netherlands, $22
    
*   Switzerland, $8
    
*   United Kingdom, $18.50
    

The exact amount paid at arrival time may be lower or higher pending the quantity of devices you ordered, and if you included add-ons.

For reference, TRMNL devices ship with description "\[Case Color\] E-ink display," category "Accessory - with battery," and HS Code 85171400.

Finally, when you receive a notice from your local courier with a commercial invoice and "Declared value," note that this declared value is the total of the goods -- not the Duty fee. That would be no fun indeed.

**Optimizing duty fees**
------------------------

Where allowed, we set our declared value to our lowest advertised price, for example when valid coupons are applied. This reduces fees for many customers.

We also offer occasional discounts to customers abroad, specifically to help cover international postage or duty fees.

**Paying duty fees**
--------------------

Some customers may prefer to pre-pay their Duty fee to avoid the hassle of making a separate payment in-person at a local post office.

But this is not always an optimal decision, as some couriers charge a large "courier handling fee" of $7-28 for this pre-pay privilege.

Other customers prefer to pre-pay due to their in-office job or travel schedule. In our experience, post offices typically hold packages for days or weeks before returning them to TRMNL. Additionally, some local couriers allow Duty fees to be paid online, or they include a payment slip during delivery and allow the recipient to pay fees later.

**Avoiding duty fees**
----------------------

It's not possible to completely avoid Duty fees, even if TRMNL devices are shipped from Europe. There would simply be one larger fee paid up front, when we send products to a regional center.

That said, we are looking for an EU-based distributor to help alleviate shipping times and potentially shipping fees. If you have a suggestion, email [\[email protected\]](/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#d9adbcb8b499acaabcadabb4b7b5f7bab6b4)
.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

TRMNL mobile app

How to use TRMNL on your iPhone or Android. Sort of.

We built TRMNL with a mobile-friendly navigation and responsive design for iPhones, Androids, tablets, and everything in between.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1228105071/3a675b4c158e28965707155c9d50/trmnl-mobile-dashboard.png?expires=1743477300&signature=36e9f2222cb4cec0c8cc916c588d9cd9474b314eb1f0bb7b8dc9095bed63bc86&req=dSIlHsh%2BmIFYWPMW1HO4zZuQwtVzT9PMxoBgw8sFIITuqTl%2FNhQuKsQlpWfB%0A1jtpY5cJdfMZ5uEEy1E%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1228105071/3a675b4c158e28965707155c9d50/trmnl-mobile-dashboard.png?expires=1743477300&signature=36e9f2222cb4cec0c8cc916c588d9cd9474b314eb1f0bb7b8dc9095bed63bc86&req=dSIlHsh%2BmIFYWPMW1HO4zZuQwtVzT9PMxoBgw8sFIITuqTl%2FNhQuKsQlpWfB%0A1jtpY5cJdfMZ5uEEy1E%3D%0A)

But how can you get to this experience in 1 tap?

Save TRMNL to your device's home screen.

Step 1 - Visit TRMNL
--------------------

On your phone or table, visit [usetrmnl.com](https://usetrmnl.com)
 with the Safari or Firefox mobile browser application.

We suggest logging in and visiting your dashboard, which looks like the screen above.

Step 2 - Add TRMNL to your device
---------------------------------

In the browser application navigation you should see a "share" icon, which is usually a square with an up-arrow inside.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1228111227/5593093c5dde95049fa8b95907ee/TRMNL+mobile+browser+share+button.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=b80bf9ab440cba23631038453f84fb26f8bc02c3227c497ceb9a0d8614436c22&req=dSIlHsh%2FnINdXvMW1HO4zYszCh0s4b%2BBisg%2B89cnnwxOvjKlN5lfVwfufqxe%0AOMEQkzoQu4YbQNNDbLQ%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1228111227/5593093c5dde95049fa8b95907ee/TRMNL+mobile+browser+share+button.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=b80bf9ab440cba23631038453f84fb26f8bc02c3227c497ceb9a0d8614436c22&req=dSIlHsh%2FnINdXvMW1HO4zYszCh0s4b%2BBisg%2B89cnnwxOvjKlN5lfVwfufqxe%0AOMEQkzoQu4YbQNNDbLQ%3D%0A)

Tap this icon, then find and select the "Add to Home Screen" option.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1228113729/c16dc16ac414ada943910eb9284b/trmnl-add-to-home-screen.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=49339b4757fb988bdcba01650ae0935183c5d55f807361b9183f21ba6950e323&req=dSIlHsh%2FnoZdUPMW1HO4zc%2B3rTVUkDdXBDtaera1zo1nFb5VQ8f6BnhhKyzf%0AjPi1Y5Z0zewybB0K0Ek%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1228113729/c16dc16ac414ada943910eb9284b/trmnl-add-to-home-screen.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=49339b4757fb988bdcba01650ae0935183c5d55f807361b9183f21ba6950e323&req=dSIlHsh%2FnoZdUPMW1HO4zc%2B3rTVUkDdXBDtaera1zo1nFb5VQ8f6BnhhKyzf%0AjPi1Y5Z0zewybB0K0Ek%3D%0A)

Provide a new name, we suggest simply "TRMNL."

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1228114755/958a9345c93c1380458eac220bef/trmnl-mobile-app-naming.png?expires=1743477300&signature=b288ab38354365f0da9e0db8c68577d8d5e0b8db7ab63236d9f590e45be37c78&req=dSIlHsh%2FmYZaXPMW1HO4zXEp51%2BKqIVIlQWlEsLM0Uq%2BAmnJZgqjZQiVq5D2%0A2Y23crDjGg4kDNeugtU%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1228114755/958a9345c93c1380458eac220bef/trmnl-mobile-app-naming.png?expires=1743477300&signature=b288ab38354365f0da9e0db8c68577d8d5e0b8db7ab63236d9f590e45be37c78&req=dSIlHsh%2FmYZaXPMW1HO4zXEp51%2BKqIVIlQWlEsLM0Uq%2BAmnJZgqjZQiVq5D2%0A2Y23crDjGg4kDNeugtU%3D%0A)

Select "Add" to finish.

Step 3 - You're Done!
---------------------

TRMNL is just a tap away while you're on the go.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1228115816/098a78d365cceca66c422a19fe37/trmnl-iphone-android-app.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=d98e64ea5d1f99b0013227e30bf276631953a863e01ef78429a689726a04effd&req=dSIlHsh%2FmIleX%2FMW1HO4zUTe6S9gfcLADMJLfpsSx5RjpEUEkelInqsr6xJO%0Ayd50CMpuSmiVbYL5hRQ%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1228115816/098a78d365cceca66c422a19fe37/trmnl-iphone-android-app.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=d98e64ea5d1f99b0013227e30bf276631953a863e01ef78429a689726a04effd&req=dSIlHsh%2FmIleX%2FMW1HO4zUTe6S9gfcLADMJLfpsSx5RjpEUEkelInqsr6xJO%0Ayd50CMpuSmiVbYL5hRQ%3D%0A)

Stay focused.

# Applying the screen (anti glare) protector | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

[All Collections](/en/)

[General](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820478-general)

Applying the screen (anti glare) protector

What is this screen film thing in my box?

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 5 months ago

Your TRMNL shipment may include a pre-cut screen protector. This is included in all crowdfunded pre-orders, as well as all orders with the "Clarity Kit" add-on.

This small bonus is an **anti-glare film**, designed to reduce light refraction on devices placed in direct sunlight. Applying this accessory is totally optional, and we suggest testing your device in its desired location to determine if you need it at all.

To apply the anti-glare film you have a couple options:

1.  Carefully place it on your device screen as-is, using the alcohol wipe and micrifiber cloth to remove dust and improve adherence.
    
2.  [Dissassemble your device](https://intercom.help/trmnl/en/articles/10003228-how-to-disassemble-your-trmnl)
    , remove the screen, and apply it with slightly better accuracy
    

The benefit of Option 2 is in removing air bubbles following application. Just like adding a screen protector to your phone, you'll want to apply some (gentle) pressure with a sturdy but dull-eged tool to squeeze out the air. Otherwise you may wish you hadn't applied the protector in the first place. ;)

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃
