# Refer & Earn | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_c33ed1d696)

[](#h_64957cc5f8)

[](#h_ca3aec556e)

[](#h_89ae8fb9d4)

[All Collections](/en/)

[General](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820478-general)

Refer & Earn

Benefits and ideas for sharing TRMNL with your network.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 2 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_c33ed1d696)

[](#h_64957cc5f8)

[](#h_ca3aec556e)

[](#h_89ae8fb9d4)

The TRMNL team spent years building B2B subscription software before diving into consumer tech hardware with $0 /month recurring revenue.

It's been an exciting ride, but we rely on customers to help spread the word. We don't advertise on Facebook or Google, and we don't have any billboards. (We did [design one](https://x.com/useTRMNL/status/1868827604322861386)
, though.)

So instead of giving money to marketers whose job is to make people click buttons and get distracted, why not reward our community?

Introducing Refer & Earn
------------------------

With TRMNL you can create incentives for yourself and others including:

*   Give $10, get $10
    
*   Give $15, get $5
    
*   Give $5, get $15
    

Or even:

*   Give away our Developer edition perk ($20 value)
    
*   Give away free shipping to Canada, UK, etc regions with <= $20 postage
    

Once created, this coupon will be available inside your account alongside a real-time redemption tracker so you know if your efforts are working:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1319544695/61627b1433994834bfd8d0fc29cc/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=77ce8de821378334794317fde747c40b325ee4d2cd7e9b178e291f750b069a06&req=dSMmH8x6mYdWXPMW1HO4zTjfHrcTQtLnp0bTVpO%2Bd8NCxV7pJPjI00mizgiw%0A2qP5V8MvF6dy1H3Ftq8%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1319544695/61627b1433994834bfd8d0fc29cc/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=77ce8de821378334794317fde747c40b325ee4d2cd7e9b178e291f750b069a06&req=dSMmH8x6mYdWXPMW1HO4zTjfHrcTQtLnp0bTVpO%2Bd8NCxV7pJPjI00mizgiw%0A2qP5V8MvF6dy1H3Ftq8%3D%0A)

**If you prefer store credit instead of cash, that's fine too**. We'll top up your online store customer profile 1x per month with recent redemptions.

Apply for a referral code
-------------------------

Refer & Earn affiliates are manually approved after confirming a few details:

*   You're an active TRMNL user (no affiliate marketers please)
    
*   You'll represent our brand with integrity (no spam posting on random websites)
    
*   You're comfortable answering questions about how the product works
    

If this is you, click "Request a Code" inside [your TRMNL account](https://usetrmnl.com/account)
. If you already did that, just reply to the email we sent you and we'll set up a code.

Using your referral code
------------------------

Nobody enjoys hard-to-apply coupon codes. Once you have yours, point people to our home page with a "ref" param like so:

https://usetrmnl.com?ref=<your-code>

For example, if your coupon code is "billy10" it would be:

https://usetrmnl.com?ref=billy10

When your referral lands at checkout the code will be automatically applied:  
​

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1328047155/6d10da4c9891caa75b5c2e185b8e/trmnl-discount-generator-billy-10-example.png?expires=1743477300&signature=d459842e1b9ccfa77b23a3abf916cccce29f31fca276d77c796e14c34586f2b9&req=dSMlHsl6moBaXPMW1HO4zfeF4qIny8VWqNcHf9iG5RMS9Vjo2Gm8yEgto3Re%0AsnPUb%2F9kaTD9PcoYVzI%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1328047155/6d10da4c9891caa75b5c2e185b8e/trmnl-discount-generator-billy-10-example.png?expires=1743477300&signature=d459842e1b9ccfa77b23a3abf916cccce29f31fca276d77c796e14c34586f2b9&req=dSMlHsl6moBaXPMW1HO4zfeF4qIny8VWqNcHf9iG5RMS9Vjo2Gm8yEgto3Re%0AsnPUb%2F9kaTD9PcoYVzI%3D%0A)

Alternatively, point folks to `https://usetrmnl.com` (no params) and tell them to "input coupon code `my-code` at Checkout," as depicted above.

Tips to share TRMNL
-------------------

We don't need expect anything fancy. Sharing TRMNL in your own words is ideal. But we will provide a few examples (via email) that have worked well for others.

From sharing a picture of your device, to posting on X about a custom plugin you're building, or even replying to a comment on Hacker News, we've witnessed dozens of tiny shoutouts drive significant interest to our mission.

If you're not a marketer (congrats!), no sweat. We'll help find opportunities to share your referral code so that everyone wins. We'll also share the 1-pager mentioned above with approved affiliates, so go ahead and [apply](https://usetrmnl.com/account)
.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

# Device / WiFi troubleshooting | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_1cf5393650)

[](#h_6adb37c99c)

[All Collections](/en/)

[General](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820478-general)

Device / WiFi troubleshooting

Understanding error screens and connection issues.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 3 weeks ago

Table of contents

[](#h_1cf5393650)

[](#h_6adb37c99c)

Below is a work-in-progress collection of potential issues + fixes to ensure your TRMNL device remains connected.

**Initial Setup Issues**
------------------------

If you've just unboxed your TRMNL, see the following tips.

#### WiFi portal closing unexpectedly

On your phone or computer, click "forget network" (or similar feature), then restart your device and re-connect to TRMNL WiFi.

#### WiFi network not listed

Like many IoT devices, TRMNL requires a 2.4ghz network. If you only have 5ghz enabled on your router, you can usually enable dual band with no changes required for your existing devices.

It's ideal to have a separate, dedicated 2.4ghz network versus a "dual band" network, because routers with dual-band enabled will often instruct devices to use the 5ghz band, which is incompatible with most IoT devices.

#### My network has a captive portal

If you're setting up TRMNL in a building with "hotel style" WiFi, whereby you must input credentials inside a captive portal popup following network connection, TRMNL must be accompanied by a middleware device.

One user reported buying this [$35 Opal Router](https://www.amazon.com/GL-iNet-GL-SFT1200-Secure-Travel-Router/dp/B09N72FMH5)
 (Amazon) and using it to quickly bypass their network's captive portal configuration. Then you can connect TRMNL to this router's access point with no issues.

#### Wifi network not connecting

If you're inputting your home or office network's WiFi credentials into the [TRMNL WiFi portal](https://intercom.help/trmnl/en/articles/9416306-how-to-set-up-a-new-device)
, but the device is not connecting or showing an error screen, check out the security settings on your router. While TRMNL should work with WPA, WPA2, and WPA3, some users have reported that only WPA3 connections were successful for their device.

Another thing to check is whether `https://trmnl.app` loads on your local network, incognito. Just use your phone (on WiFi) or computer and visit the URL. If it doesn't load, your router or ISP is blocking the endpoint that our Firmware pings for screen content. **Note: do not use [https://trmnl.app](https://trmnl.app)
** to operate your device. It will not work.

In this case, you can simply modify the firmware to ping our actual URL, `https://usetrmnl.com` , by choosing "Custom Server" from the WiFi setup step and inputting "[https://usetrmnl.com](https://usetrmnl.com)
".

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1384336478/234babc450453e13317ac5ee2054/trmnl-custom-server.png?expires=1743477300&signature=ad57e9a22e4b32fc7d90c34f1eae33895cf19d1a7535a43e02b74a8cf71dbb39&req=dSMvEsp9m4VYUfMW1HO4zYLrj%2BdrsrhIMeLP4Xk1zzQcRpGWTApU1sQVzdOF%0AaNoU55wZ8ak6KTmlQzs%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1384336478/234babc450453e13317ac5ee2054/trmnl-custom-server.png?expires=1743477300&signature=ad57e9a22e4b32fc7d90c34f1eae33895cf19d1a7535a43e02b74a8cf71dbb39&req=dSMvEsp9m4VYUfMW1HO4zYLrj%2BdrsrhIMeLP4Xk1zzQcRpGWTApU1sQVzdOF%0AaNoU55wZ8ak6KTmlQzs%3D%0A)

To reproduce this setup step, hold the circular button on the back of your TRMNL for 5-6 seconds, then let get. You may also need to turn the device off, wait 5 seconds, then turn it back on (after performing a hold-reset).

**Ongoing Issues**
------------------

If you've already set up your TRMNL but are experiencing new issues, see the following tips. We will update this as often as we detect a new pattern.

For live help, open the chat widget in the bottom right corner and ping us in real time. Be ready to share your router brand / model or other home networking settings to help us help you.

#### Firmware update looping / slow

Our firmware packages are only around 1.4mb, however it may take a few minutes for the package to be installed on your device following a download. We do not recommend clicking the boot button to 'skip' this update, or turning your device off/on.

If you prefer to disable firmware updates, simply visit [Devices > Edit](https://usetrmnl.com/devices)
 > scroll down and uncheck the "OTA Updates" feture. Note that this requires the Developer edition perk, but if you don't have that enabled then you can send us a live chat and we'll do it on your behalf.

#### Intermittment content vs error screen

If your TRMNL sometimes displays content as expected, but at other times shows an error screen, it's possible the buffer needs to be reset.

Simply turn off your device for 5-7 seconds (this length of time is necessary), then turn it back on.

#### Error screen: "wifi not connected" or "content malformed"

Suggestion: If you have ad blockers installed at the router-level, try whitelisting the domain "[https://trmnl.app](https://trmnl.app)
". This is the endpoint where the device firmware fetches new content.

Suggestion: Set your Device's refresh rate (visit [Devices > Edit](https://usetrmnl.com/devices)
 > scroll down) to 5 minutes, then click the button on the back of your device 1x. This should sync your new refresh rate. Then, wait 5 minutes for the device to perform a full refresh cycle (sleep, wake, request content).

Suggestion: To help us confirm if this is a local network issue (vs device / firmware related), try connecting your TRMNL to your phone's hotspot. If you're using an iPhone > Personal HotSpot, make sure to toggle on "Maximize Compatibility" (beneath your editable WiFi Password field).

**Orbi mesh customer?**

Your standard setup may include a dual-band 2.4 / 5ghz network. However some users have reported that they needed to enable a 2.4ghz-only band for their TRMNL connection to remain stable.

#### Ubiquiti / Unifi customer?

Our friends at HostiFi wrote [this article](https://support.hostifi.com/en/articles/7019454-unifi-recommend-settings-for-iot-devices)
 with tips to ensure iOT devices like TRMNL play nicely with your network.

Without a proper setup, your router's default feature "Band Steering" will direct TRMNL devices to leverage the 5ghz band which will not work, even if you connected to 2.4ghz during setup.

Below are some router settings from another user that fixed their connectivity issues. They have a 2.4ghz-only SSID with multiple IoT devices:  
​

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1276590467/12af8da0a2e7a6a9ca6b89bbacd8/unifi-settings-2.png?expires=1743477300&signature=4cfbc9528f9de6366927a007e9d90ed64a6cbeed637fcffbf6ed2d00da92ec18&req=dSIgEMx3nYVZXvMW1HO4zcW5Dm8M5JnpzyB%2FmuRlr43%2BGlJANlM5LVmtYrMC%0ArikyqOU9v%2B4JSpdK%2B%2BU%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1276590467/12af8da0a2e7a6a9ca6b89bbacd8/unifi-settings-2.png?expires=1743477300&signature=4cfbc9528f9de6366927a007e9d90ed64a6cbeed637fcffbf6ed2d00da92ec18&req=dSIgEMx3nYVZXvMW1HO4zcW5Dm8M5JnpzyB%2FmuRlr43%2BGlJANlM5LVmtYrMC%0ArikyqOU9v%2B4JSpdK%2B%2BU%3D%0A)

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1276590465/569c6b2c40832edbea75b1c6a84f/unifi-settings-1.png?expires=1743477300&signature=0374e938d526e1e6c21b4409a93ef7d41eb04fa58ff837c8e774cbfe2cb1a676&req=dSIgEMx3nYVZXPMW1HO4zd9%2FGhXpVWv%2F9CUbaJbQYG17qU2LYLhSJkhx22Gm%0AaH1soAAfSdTCb1fCtlk%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1276590465/569c6b2c40832edbea75b1c6a84f/unifi-settings-1.png?expires=1743477300&signature=0374e938d526e1e6c21b4409a93ef7d41eb04fa58ff837c8e774cbfe2cb1a676&req=dSIgEMx3nYVZXPMW1HO4zd9%2FGhXpVWv%2F9CUbaJbQYG17qU2LYLhSJkhx22Gm%0AaH1soAAfSdTCb1fCtlk%3D%0A)

If some of the above parameters don't work, try setting just your router's "Minimum Data Rate Control" setting to a minimum of 12mbps on the 2.4ghz network.

#### What else?

In general, device connectivity issues are a mix of local networking / router quirks and some ongoing compatibility improvements being made to our open source firmware:

[https://github.com/usetrmnl/firmware](https://github.com/usetrmnl/firmware)

So if your device is having issues, rest assured that we can probably fix it with a little bit of back and forth debugging, and your hardware is in good condition otherwise.

(_As of this writing in November 2024 we've shipped 1,500 devices. Only 1x had a broken WiFi receiver on the board, which we immediately replaced at no cost to the customer._)

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

# Device battery FAQ | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_7ffd1ecb8b)

[](#h_ab43496116)

[](#h_9e51593f7b)

[All Collections](/en/)

[General](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820478-general)

Device battery FAQ

On charging and predicting your TRMNL's energy.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 2 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_7ffd1ecb8b)

[](#h_ab43496116)

[](#h_9e51593f7b)

While logged into TRMNL you can see WiFi + battery strength from your device picker or [all devices](https://usetrmnl.com/devices)
 view:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1379761850/5cc06090f21792701dc9abeb95e7/trmnl-devices-view.png?expires=1743477300&signature=0b293f38f439165c831d5a05880038aa54e53f526455b58c350f0dbf2db397fe&req=dSMgH854nIlaWfMW1HO4zfbHOoC35CpuZFPYCrXyd8EdYhPIt96%2F%2BDa4L8LM%0ABexJENDjv%2B8umQANw%2Fg%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1379761850/5cc06090f21792701dc9abeb95e7/trmnl-devices-view.png?expires=1743477300&signature=0b293f38f439165c831d5a05880038aa54e53f526455b58c350f0dbf2db397fe&req=dSMgH854nIlaWfMW1HO4zfbHOoC35CpuZFPYCrXyd8EdYhPIt96%2F%2BDa4L8LM%0ABexJENDjv%2B8umQANw%2Fg%3D%0A)

Calculating remaining battery power is a simple equation, but it becomes less reliable as energy is drained and playlist refresh rates change.

**Low battery notification**
----------------------------

When your TRMNL device has < 10% energy remaining, you'll be notified by the following screen on your display:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1379767577/5c688f45cd7b0980f4c130a9145c/trmnl-low-battery-screen.png?expires=1743477300&signature=a765eaccf6410df60167a899dc0b922ca67df5254a5f7117feaca3271c4043a7&req=dSMgH854moRYXvMW1HO4zcc6OYTXm8TKMhPPnWE7gBMgNQbCjWjY8tX%2B4rWS%0A%2BvWUrieyQcza8OqPn%2FA%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1379767577/5c688f45cd7b0980f4c130a9145c/trmnl-low-battery-screen.png?expires=1743477300&signature=a765eaccf6410df60167a899dc0b922ca67df5254a5f7117feaca3271c4043a7&req=dSMgH854moRYXvMW1HO4zcc6OYTXm8TKMhPPnWE7gBMgNQbCjWjY8tX%2B4rWS%0A%2BvWUrieyQcza8OqPn%2FA%3D%0A)

In the future you may be able to customize this screen. ;)

**Charging your TRMNL**
-----------------------

There are 2 battery options, 1800mAh (default) and 2500mAh (upgraded).

Assuming 0% energy:

*   1800mAh - 3.5 hours to full charge
    
*   2500mAh - 5 hours to full charge
    

When a TRMNL is plugged in to charge, you may notice its reported battery power seems to fully restore within minutes:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1379766479/a145362272ca1fdf5dfbbfab7ad8/trmnl-battery-charge-state.png?expires=1743477300&signature=65dc7c5405a1d623d8b4347518ddff4064d936dbd94fcc3b42bdbe6b7c3a889f&req=dSMgH854m4VYUPMW1HO4zSDdQk3a7HPM%2BkxYuiq9hBr%2B1CVR1nMxNk4xCjlo%0AAIJYLTvzLpYGZreV9ss%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1379766479/a145362272ca1fdf5dfbbfab7ad8/trmnl-battery-charge-state.png?expires=1743477300&signature=65dc7c5405a1d623d8b4347518ddff4064d936dbd94fcc3b42bdbe6b7c3a889f&req=dSMgH854m4VYUPMW1HO4zSDdQk3a7HPM%2BkxYuiq9hBr%2B1CVR1nMxNk4xCjlo%0AAIJYLTvzLpYGZreV9ss%3D%0A)

However this is not necessarily true. As of this writing, TRMNL's web interface does not differentiate between "now charging" versus "fully charged."

Therefore, whenever you see the low battery screen, we suggest plugging in your TRMNL for at least a couple hours.

**Understanding power consumption**
-----------------------------------

One refresh cycle takes 32.8mA over a period of 24s. In this time the device will ping the TRMNL server, download an image, and refresh the display.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1379770401/dbb99758317f655be8712226c03f/trmnl-display-power-refresh-cycle.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=7f18d0cf48ef64771667a23378502ba3d13ddd87592096873a973821e7a31856&req=dSMgH855nYVfWPMW1HO4zWWlAotyC650L5jvc6hM%2BAVNCJs21HViDpJTqcoB%0AvhXI4L6EjwUignF8Zmg%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1379770401/dbb99758317f655be8712226c03f/trmnl-display-power-refresh-cycle.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=7f18d0cf48ef64771667a23378502ba3d13ddd87592096873a973821e7a31856&req=dSMgH855nYVfWPMW1HO4zWWlAotyC650L5jvc6hM%2BAVNCJs21HViDpJTqcoB%0AvhXI4L6EjwUignF8Zmg%3D%0A)

If there is no need to download and refresh the display with new image content -- for example if an image is not returned, or the returned image matches what is currently displayed -- power consumption will be around 20% of the above calculation.

For more comprehensive details on TRMNL device power consumption, see here:

[https://github.com/usetrmnl/firmware?tab=readme-ov-file#power-consumption](https://github.com/usetrmnl/firmware?tab=readme-ov-file#power-consumption)

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

# Mirroring a Device | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_1fa7e1627c)

[](#h_390e75497b)

[](#h_8c412b352e)

[All Collections](/en/)

[General](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820478-general)

Mirroring a Device

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 2 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_1fa7e1627c)

[](#h_390e75497b)

[](#h_8c412b352e)

How to Enable Mirroring
=======================

Enable the device to be Sharable in the Master Device settings

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1372998248/63aa80b7bb08ad06547c712c97d0/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=1e5c7daef2c8d5698f7d59968896c75ee29c708299a49f9509f007dfb1126a95&req=dSMgFMB3lYNbUfMW1HO4zYCbtFtCqHHUfEEx4YxPenBN9LnRXvGsD406cna2%0AuLxKQ%2BNOYFO10jCsz%2BM%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1372998248/63aa80b7bb08ad06547c712c97d0/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=1e5c7daef2c8d5698f7d59968896c75ee29c708299a49f9509f007dfb1126a95&req=dSMgFMB3lYNbUfMW1HO4zYCbtFtCqHHUfEEx4YxPenBN9LnRXvGsD406cna2%0AuLxKQ%2BNOYFO10jCsz%2BM%3D%0A)

In the child device, enter the `friendly_id` of the device to mirror  
​

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1372999008/3ab72b5a768fa3fbf2dfecbf4515/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=6201b06a50e94a16e263995d62da625a210229e3b24bc7f2a9f5d3686682686a&req=dSMgFMB3lIFfUfMW1HO4zRTsF0MEve9UgwzPXNsWclI81U3ohkaVdCy3chR6%0A9LOytjnT6poms3lRVoQ%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1372999008/3ab72b5a768fa3fbf2dfecbf4515/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=6201b06a50e94a16e263995d62da625a210229e3b24bc7f2a9f5d3686682686a&req=dSMgFMB3lIFfUfMW1HO4zRTsF0MEve9UgwzPXNsWclI81U3ohkaVdCy3chR6%0A9LOytjnT6poms3lRVoQ%3D%0A)

How does Mirroring Work?
========================

1.  Once a device is set up to be Sharable instead of Standalone, anyone can mirror the device if they know the `friendly_id`.
    
2.  Mirroring a device copies the plugins in the master device's playlist at the start. If the master device adds more plugins later, the mirrored device will not automatically receive them.
    
3.  If the master device changes the visibility setting to "Standalone" from "Sharable", TRMNL will delete all the mirrored plugins from child devices that have the master device's plugins. This ensures the master device can always modify the mirrorable settings. However, independently installed plugins in child device would remain unaffected.
    
4.  A child device can install its own plugins independently, and nothing will be shared with the master device.
    
5.  If the master device has shared 5 plugins, the child device can delete 2 and retain only 3. However, deleting plugins from the child device will not affect the plugins on the master device.
    

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1373007072/84773da94c1828fd736d8e808820/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=518372ece7085330369c23847e3bbb2ecf42a1898931f0e7f7fccdc52fa90e9f&req=dSMgFcl%2BmoFYW%2FMW1HO4zQNF4fRTJ%2FP5Br4ZtrPq547UqtRFZn15VOUSgkvG%0AHeLD6Mhv2upY2cG%2BE2U%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1373007072/84773da94c1828fd736d8e808820/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=518372ece7085330369c23847e3bbb2ecf42a1898931f0e7f7fccdc52fa90e9f&req=dSMgFcl%2BmoFYW%2FMW1HO4zQNF4fRTJ%2FP5Br4ZtrPq547UqtRFZn15VOUSgkvG%0AHeLD6Mhv2upY2cG%2BE2U%3D%0A)

Mirroring use case
==================

*   Mirroring is useful when doing a Team purchase, where one Team Member acts as a master device and oauth's the B2B dashboard eg (Shopify, Google Analytics, Mailchimp, etc) without necessarily having to share the credentials with the rest of the team. The Child device will get the B2B dashboard while still being able to install their own plugins
    
*   Sharing a plugin with your grandparents / parents who are not technically sound. You can install a shared family calendar / note board / birthday remainder on master device and the child device will just get them.
    

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

# Finding your TRMNL Mac Address | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_09768e159e)

[](#h_78ed0b70b4)

[All Collections](/en/)

[General](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820478-general)

Finding your TRMNL Mac Address

For debugging and customer support.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 2 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_09768e159e)

[](#h_78ed0b70b4)

Every TRMNL has 2 immutable characteristics -- a Mac Address, and a Serial.

Mac Addresses are generated by our manufacturer, and Serial values are printed directly on the PCB (circuit board).

In some cases, TRMNL may need to know one of these values to help debug a connection issue. But instead of [disassembling your device](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/articles/10003228-how-to-disassemble-your-trmnl)
, we suggest looking up your Mac Address instead.

**Option A - WiFi Router settings**
-----------------------------------

Pending your local network setup, you may have access to a wireless router settings interface. If you're using TRMNL at home, this would show al ist of devices such as your phone, television, computers, and so on.

If you have access to this, look for a device whose name starts with "ESP\_", followed by a few random characters. Select that device and you should see a "MAC" value such as "AB:4D:CA:FF:Q1".

**Option B - WiFi Portal Footer**
---------------------------------

Put your TRMNL in "pairing mode" by turning it on, waiting for it to boot, then holding the button on the back (next to the on/off switch) for 5-6 seconds.

Let go of the button, then wait for TRMNL to show a WiFi setup screen like this:  
​

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1389951722/c0cef3da83da00ac3311a6399884/trmnl-setup-screen.jpeg?expires=1743477300&signature=936299dc8990f43a47d7e21f33b2c2e0d5a7c27eb3182035d0e5d53bee177223&req=dSMvH8B7nIZdW%2FMW1HO4zd8k9lKtxue6Yfr%2FTpewoF2N0JkLGEotMHwvy%2FBd%0A4XcszqMDn71wjy%2FUZ1Y%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1389951722/c0cef3da83da00ac3311a6399884/trmnl-setup-screen.jpeg?expires=1743477300&signature=936299dc8990f43a47d7e21f33b2c2e0d5a7c27eb3182035d0e5d53bee177223&req=dSMvH8B7nIZdW%2FMW1HO4zd8k9lKtxue6Yfr%2FTpewoF2N0JkLGEotMHwvy%2FBd%0A4XcszqMDn71wjy%2FUZ1Y%3D%0A)

Connect to the WiFi network named "TRMNL," and you should see a screen like this:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1389952187/ea4e4ecfd2cd36c4d7d96543d518/trmnl-wifi-captive-portal-mac.png?expires=1743477300&signature=6df7ef52f0ed1f0ee158de3cb62cb20530c01a15175791f2a784370e6cbf5c3d&req=dSMvH8B7n4BXXvMW1HO4zWxO4WUWns0IsT0pXraO%2Fpz9EBglkf0AnvZ%2FG%2F8K%0Ahoavuj69YqCXeQC7SKE%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1389952187/ea4e4ecfd2cd36c4d7d96543d518/trmnl-wifi-captive-portal-mac.png?expires=1743477300&signature=6df7ef52f0ed1f0ee158de3cb62cb20530c01a15175791f2a784370e6cbf5c3d&req=dSMvH8B7n4BXXvMW1HO4zWxO4WUWns0IsT0pXraO%2Fpz9EBglkf0AnvZ%2FG%2F8K%0Ahoavuj69YqCXeQC7SKE%3D%0A)

Select your local network, input a password, then coick "Connect." Within 1-2 seconds you should see a grey footer, "Connecting to SSID, MAC address:"

This screen usually disappears after 2-3 seconds, so it's easiest if you take a screenshot when you see the grey bar. The MAC address will be at the bottom of the footer area.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

# Mashups | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_c30326dc4d)

[](#h_c82fb3c6b1)

[](#h_d27cf9c697)

[](#h_d8837b6acf)

[All Collections](/en/)

[General](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820478-general)

Mashups

How to build split-screen plugins.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated this week

Table of contents

[](#h_c30326dc4d)

[](#h_c82fb3c6b1)

[](#h_d27cf9c697)

[](#h_d8837b6acf)

TRMNL offers several layout combinations for your plugins. The default layout is full screen, illustrated by the top left icon in the graphic below.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1259881326/fcbe7ef849aa82a501c88976f17d/trmnl-mashup-layout-options.png?expires=1743477300&signature=b7daab37e4b47597c9dc50a658bc6f78715ae926e9acceaf972deb3b3e8557d0&req=dSIiH8F2nIJdX%2FMW1HO4zbabQ2M5FJE1njHe9sRHlx3TUDrOEFxUkeuh4oAD%0ADTWX7m7P4fKjzS92Kis%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1259881326/fcbe7ef849aa82a501c88976f17d/trmnl-mashup-layout-options.png?expires=1743477300&signature=b7daab37e4b47597c9dc50a658bc6f78715ae926e9acceaf972deb3b3e8557d0&req=dSIiH8F2nIJdX%2FMW1HO4zbabQ2M5FJE1njHe9sRHlx3TUDrOEFxUkeuh4oAD%0ADTWX7m7P4fKjzS92Kis%3D%0A)

**Create a Mashup**
-------------------

When you connect a new plugin, or create a new plugin "instance" (for an existing plugin), TRMNL adds a full screen layout to your Playlist automatically.

To instead leverage a Mashups layout, simply visit your [Playlists tab](https://usetrmnl.com/playlists)
 and hover your mouse over the "Add a Plugin" dropdown.

Here you can select a layout, then begin building it out with a few clicks.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1259884042/e1c1747e53f42784d8ed3db74273/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=e49f93b96855aa58cd15e69908aad617cfe649c11d48cc875716b3a66616c9e5&req=dSIiH8F2mYFbW%2FMW1HO4zbkxDnE%2B768y%2BmWqu2bQud5PE7cjvDCj7jeUwH3b%0AIIt10iefC%2FCdH4d0ZaY%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1259884042/e1c1747e53f42784d8ed3db74273/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=e49f93b96855aa58cd15e69908aad617cfe649c11d48cc875716b3a66616c9e5&req=dSIiH8F2mYFbW%2FMW1HO4zbkxDnE%2B768y%2BmWqu2bQud5PE7cjvDCj7jeUwH3b%0AIIt10iefC%2FCdH4d0ZaY%3D%0A)

In this example above we chose the 50/50 split screen layout, which is the top-right icon in the graphic at the top of this guide.

Next, we can choose any\* of our connected plugins from the "Section A" and "Section B" dropdowns.

As you can see, whatever plugin we provide in the Section A plugin will be mapped to the left pane layout, denoted by the 'A' inside the template.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1259885759/7120fb78852f3893fde34ab6029f/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=95cb35f61def98ddee370d9d5600348257d8feffdb625113b63b500a85e9e35f&req=dSIiH8F2mIZaUPMW1HO4zX4TiA%2FX4Gz%2BAIMd88p2pW8zeOQN1kJOkPCLeI6n%0A8MHuUV1VqPqlH2PcnSc%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1259885759/7120fb78852f3893fde34ab6029f/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=95cb35f61def98ddee370d9d5600348257d8feffdb625113b63b500a85e9e35f&req=dSIiH8F2mIZaUPMW1HO4zX4TiA%2FX4Gz%2BAIMd88p2pW8zeOQN1kJOkPCLeI6n%0A8MHuUV1VqPqlH2PcnSc%3D%0A)

Once you've chosen a plugin for each section, your Playlist will refresh.

**See your Mashup**
-------------------

After creating a mashup, it should then take just a few seconds for the Mashup content to be generated. So instead of waiting for your device to fetch this particular content, you can actually refresh your Playlists tab to see the preview image.

If you'd like to inspect your Mashup more closely before it appears on your device, simply right click on the image and choose "Open Image in New Tab."

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1259887484/5875c7c1594abd2a2ebcf5ea7e55/trmnl-mashup-inspect-image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=a1fb0b9d81da40ddf9a1b5096d49bee36cee1b65bbab8df893cd698d4fca86f4&req=dSIiH8F2moVXXfMW1HO4zaoTQWqVxCBskQIvSnb5jGR2DSwNuttWUN6Uxl9M%0AdGFGJM4wi22WPlLdRSo%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1259887484/5875c7c1594abd2a2ebcf5ea7e55/trmnl-mashup-inspect-image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=a1fb0b9d81da40ddf9a1b5096d49bee36cee1b65bbab8df893cd698d4fca86f4&req=dSIiH8F2moVXXfMW1HO4zaoTQWqVxCBskQIvSnb5jGR2DSwNuttWUN6Uxl9M%0AdGFGJM4wi22WPlLdRSo%3D%0A)

**Edit a Mashup**
-----------------

To update the contents of an individual item / section within a Mashup, hover the gear cog and click Edit.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1447128318/b3059b9dee9e5acb51ded9abcba6/trmnl-edit-mashup.png?expires=1743477300&signature=86db302e0fc3bb4bad0d484a769c41fd625d9f50b4c2c5f0f512e3cded525c9d&req=dSQjEch8lYJeUfMW1HO4zcSm46l0UUwhc%2FJCVx%2BRcrh0X%2BvjtikrsJCSGZjb%0AD3aqL4WY4wfOvWkF7hQ%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1447128318/b3059b9dee9e5acb51ded9abcba6/trmnl-edit-mashup.png?expires=1743477300&signature=86db302e0fc3bb4bad0d484a769c41fd625d9f50b4c2c5f0f512e3cded525c9d&req=dSQjEch8lYJeUfMW1HO4zcSm46l0UUwhc%2FJCVx%2BRcrh0X%2BvjtikrsJCSGZjb%0AD3aqL4WY4wfOvWkF7hQ%3D%0A)

**Troubleshooting Mashups**
---------------------------

If you've created a Mashup but still see orange boxes, try waiting a few more seconds for our queue to pick up your inner contents and generate a graphic.

If your Mashup contains Private Plugin or Recipes, and the content is duplicated between unique instances, check that the markup (HTML, CSS, JS) is containerized to be unique across instances. For example, if you have a chart that binds to "#my-chart," then one of your Mashup sections will work, and the other will not.

If your Mashup has some working sections, and some blank sections, consider it's possible our system "timed out" while loading all the content and taking a snapshot for your device. If you have access to the markup and logic of the blank section, try making it smaller and faster. If the blank section is a native plugin, let us know.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

---

# How to change my time zone | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

[All Collections](/en/)

[General](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820478-general)

How to change my time zone

Set a time zone from your user profile.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 2 months ago

Many TRMNL plugins work best when we're aware of your local time zone.

During registration at usetrmnl.com/signup we attempt to "guess" this, but it's not always perfect.

To update your time zone, visit your Account page by clicking the bottom-right icon in the nav bar or going directly to [https://usetrmnl.com/account](https://usetrmnl.com/account)
.

From here you can set both your time zone, as well as your preferred language.

[![TRMNL time zone and local setting](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1384793711/ffbfe3f5ef20dae46462e5df692a/trmnl-time-zone-locale-setting.png?expires=1743477300&signature=927850015c079e431c44bdf38519e99c346cdbb2bd137d599688faed4eb1c0ce&req=dSMvEs53noZeWPMW1HO4zWv6ULfTLL1o1RlFNoeYUa1fBpWteR08V7RAz%2FYY%0AFHwCE0P%2FiUrCmDZbR5g%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1384793711/ffbfe3f5ef20dae46462e5df692a/trmnl-time-zone-locale-setting.png?expires=1743477300&signature=927850015c079e431c44bdf38519e99c346cdbb2bd137d599688faed4eb1c0ce&req=dSMvEs53noZeWPMW1HO4zWv6ULfTLL1o1RlFNoeYUa1fBpWteR08V7RAz%2FYY%0AFHwCE0P%2FiUrCmDZbR5g%3D%0A)

The language setting will improve your TRMNL experience in a few places:

1.  the web app interface (labels, description text, buttons, etc)
    
2.  plugin renders (localized dates, keywords)
    
3.  custom plugins (via a growing "word dictionary")
    

To contribute to our localization efforts, go here:

[https://github.com/usetrmnl/trmnl-i18n/](https://github.com/usetrmnl/trmnl-i18n/)

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

# Manually flash firmware | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_22ba9668e6)

[](#h_c0839e8155)

[](#h_af8cc1b22e)

[](#h_151df2e9b5)

[All Collections](/en/)

[General](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820478-general)

Manually flash firmware

How to set your device to a specific firmware version

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 4 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_22ba9668e6)

[](#h_c0839e8155)

[](#h_af8cc1b22e)

[](#h_151df2e9b5)

**_Note_**_: this guide assumes your device has Developer edition enabled. If it doesn't, visit [https://usetrmnl.com/upgrade](https://usetrmnl.com/upgrade)
 while logged in._

There are a couple reasons you may want to dictate your device's firmware:

1.  Your local network performs better on a specific release
    
2.  You've modified the [native firmware](https://github.com/usetrmnl/firmware)
     or prefer to use your own
    

If you simply need to update your device's firmware to the latest stable version, you may skip the entire guide below and use [this tool](https://usetrmnl.com/flash)
 to flash via a web browser in < 2 minutes.

**Step 1 - Disable OTA Updates**
--------------------------------

Inside TRMNL, navigate to your device in the top-right dropdown. On the settings page, scroll down to Developer Perks and disable OTA Updates.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1293924250/4a466c270a9358c55555d93cfab0/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=4e49a3ed198cef13ee67716bea5e1876930aa001c4fe8acda6429ebc36019614&req=dSIuFcB8mYNaWfMW1HO4zapVYZVi2QtHt8lvKIsaY28IWEce25856rV5JJMy%0A2W6U6FUqyTVRjvD6LkY%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1293924250/4a466c270a9358c55555d93cfab0/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=4e49a3ed198cef13ee67716bea5e1876930aa001c4fe8acda6429ebc36019614&req=dSIuFcB8mYNaWfMW1HO4zapVYZVi2QtHt8lvKIsaY28IWEce25856rV5JJMy%0A2W6U6FUqyTVRjvD6LkY%3D%0A)

Without this turned off, each time your device pings the TRMNL web server it will be instructed to download the latest firmware release.

**Step 2 - Download the TRMNL Firmware (optional)**
---------------------------------------------------

If you intend to use or modify TRMNL's firmware, you can download it here:

[https://github.com/usetrmnl/firmware](https://github.com/usetrmnl/firmware)

We recommend using the GitHub CLI (`gh repo clone usetrmnl/firmware`) but you may also download it as a zip folder from the Code dropdown in the top-right corner.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1293926392/1940e222f94146de28dea63481d6/trmnl-firmware-repo-download-zip.png?expires=1743477300&signature=b5c0fc7d1b3815dc402f03473b37bdad6fdf4b67eb016daaa46dfac439274c66&req=dSIuFcB8m4JWW%2FMW1HO4zSYWMRsbZ%2BoPTuHDsLUqSK54Ad%2Bcak6DD2GJNbHQ%0AbCQ25FFGLgiteUzEu%2Bw%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1293926392/1940e222f94146de28dea63481d6/trmnl-firmware-repo-download-zip.png?expires=1743477300&signature=b5c0fc7d1b3815dc402f03473b37bdad6fdf4b67eb016daaa46dfac439274c66&req=dSIuFcB8m4JWW%2FMW1HO4zSYWMRsbZ%2BoPTuHDsLUqSK54Ad%2Bcak6DD2GJNbHQ%0AbCQ25FFGLgiteUzEu%2Bw%3D%0A)

**Step 3 - Build + Flash Your Device**
--------------------------------------

Follow the steps on our Firmware README to compile the downloaded source code (Step 2) and upload ("flash") it to your device. No coding knowledge is required.

[https://github.com/usetrmnl/firmware?tab=readme-ov-file#compilation-guide](https://github.com/usetrmnl/firmware?tab=readme-ov-file#compilation-guide)

If you don't need the latest firmware version, and instead prefer to flash a different one, simply copy your preferred FW from the `builds` directory:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1293932273/3794b17c00eb93a74e30bf19bc40/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=a9d0f122fa4edfcd478d562e4575cdd998903e2f343adcf9aa1c13b7f7371581&req=dSIuFcB9n4NYWvMW1HO4zbR7HdwuDNsqjTyYF9ciCeg5kg98uW6wTJXS0kB8%0ArCvCetdV9ez2C2cgBsc%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1293932273/3794b17c00eb93a74e30bf19bc40/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=a9d0f122fa4edfcd478d562e4575cdd998903e2f343adcf9aa1c13b7f7371581&req=dSIuFcB9n4NYWvMW1HO4zbR7HdwuDNsqjTyYF9ciCeg5kg98uW6wTJXS0kB8%0ArCvCetdV9ez2C2cgBsc%3D%0A)

Then paste it into the hidden `.pio` directory. The full path should be `.pio/build/esp32-c3-devkitc-02/firmware.bin`, thus you should rename the copied "FWX.X.X.bin" to be named `firmware.bin`.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1293949297/c82503bffa6cd9ae6e7ddc285caf/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=c6c36af0270f77323506c4642dd1e2ca5843f7ea5a5f6edafa7f2585fcbec9b3&req=dSIuFcB6lINWXvMW1HO4zR67E9HrX4ppUnqK6I342Wht2%2FnvhLDOb5iH2mM0%0AdiXO4rexCPBro2BnejA%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1293949297/c82503bffa6cd9ae6e7ddc285caf/image.png?expires=1743477300&signature=c6c36af0270f77323506c4642dd1e2ca5843f7ea5a5f6edafa7f2585fcbec9b3&req=dSIuFcB6lINWXvMW1HO4zR67E9HrX4ppUnqK6I342Wht2%2FnvhLDOb5iH2mM0%0AdiXO4rexCPBro2BnejA%3D%0A)

When you have the preferred FW version (binary file) inside the `.pio/build/esp32-c3-devkitc-02` directory -- either because you copy/pasted from the root `build` directory or chose to "Build" it via the Platform IO extension -- you are ready to upload.

The README file continues these instructions:

[https://github.com/usetrmnl/firmware?tab=readme-ov-file#uploading-guide-platformio](https://github.com/usetrmnl/firmware?tab=readme-ov-file#uploading-guide-platformio)

_Note the importance of putting your TRMNL in "boot mode" for the contents to be written to the device._

**Step 4 - Set up your Device**
-------------------------------

You may have already set up your TRMNL device on the web application, which you don't need to do again. Instead, you'll just need to re-pair your local WiFi credentials.

Turn off the device (following Step 3 above), wait 5 seconds, then turn the device back on. It should go into the default setup mode, prompting you to connect to TRMNL WiFi as described [here](https://intercom.help/trmnl/en/articles/9416306-how-to-set-up-a-new-device)
.

After pairing your local WiFi network, TRMNL will run your customized firmware for as long as you allow it. To reverse all of the above at any time, just re-enable "OTA Updates" from your device settings inside the TRMNL web application.

Did this answer your question?

😞😐😃

---

# Custom plugins with Apple Shortcuts | TRMNL Help Center

[Skip to main content](#main-content)

Table of contents

[](#h_363c359765)

[](#h_f2159007c9)

[](#h_41b88c09d5)

[](#h_4cf21c45a2)

[](#h_7824fd3cec)

[](#h_70c31d4772)

[All Collections](/en/)

[General](https://help.usetrmnl.com/en/collections/7820478-general)

Custom plugins with Apple Shortcuts

Build TRMNL plugins directly from your Apple device.

![Ryan avatar](https://static.intercomassets.com/avatars/7041257/square_128/icon--brand_1024px-1717452963.png)

Written by Ryan

Updated over 5 months ago

Table of contents

[](#h_363c359765)

[](#h_f2159007c9)

[](#h_41b88c09d5)

[](#h_4cf21c45a2)

[](#h_7824fd3cec)

[](#h_70c31d4772)

Behind the scenes at TRMNL it takes a little bit of magic to turn useful information into a beautiful graphic on your device.

But TRMNL users don't need to worry about any of that. You can build custom plugins with just a little bit of HTML and an HTTP request.

Since HTML and HTTP basically run the entire internet, this makes Apple Shortcuts a viable and free candidate for creating todo lists, weather tickers, and more, directly from an Apple Device.

Without setting up a web server you can generate new plugins with dynamic data, automatically from your iPhone, iPad, or Mac computer.

Step 1 - Create a Private Plugin
--------------------------------

Inside TRMNL, navigate to Plugins and search for Private Plugin. This requires our Developer edition upgrade, which is just a 1 time fee of $20 from [usetrmnl.com/upgrade](https://usetrmnl.com/upgrade)
.

Provide a name for your plugin, then select the Webhook strategy, then hit Save.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246672462/ed1f51adb5d331a810a2496f3c18/trmnl-private-plugin-apple-shortcut-demo.png?expires=1743477300&signature=4b630ccb736e59413878f2ff7edbabad5115f1d433f9ff36bff86743a79110fa&req=dSIjEM95n4VZW%2FMW1HO4ze24OphjI5YiWYrzFgxDSJYdVt9%2BAetx7ftAS%2BEh%0AhjbZY%2BLMGHk8rVpPuCM%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246672462/ed1f51adb5d331a810a2496f3c18/trmnl-private-plugin-apple-shortcut-demo.png?expires=1743477300&signature=4b630ccb736e59413878f2ff7edbabad5115f1d433f9ff36bff86743a79110fa&req=dSIjEM95n4VZW%2FMW1HO4ze24OphjI5YiWYrzFgxDSJYdVt9%2BAetx7ftAS%2BEh%0AhjbZY%2BLMGHk8rVpPuCM%3D%0A)

Step 2 - Get the Template
-------------------------

A TRMNL community member created this public template to help you get started:  
​[https://www.icloud.com/shortcuts/69e47acc278140379e7da8c32a147210](https://www.icloud.com/shortcuts/69e47acc278140379e7da8c32a147210)

If you click the link above from an iOS device, you'll see a setup screen like this:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246676273/786a0e4a041ee6f3dd39ee03039a/trmnl-set-up-shortcut.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=90f110afd442fa9be96df60aa10a6ae36eca0f9636b171d413e1b467491885ee&req=dSIjEM95m4NYWvMW1HO4zQDpoXTJuPI9Dqivdj0BdNAuNceh8k2oJI%2FYZF7m%0A0imCJE09%2FiWFMFTv2aM%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246676273/786a0e4a041ee6f3dd39ee03039a/trmnl-set-up-shortcut.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=90f110afd442fa9be96df60aa10a6ae36eca0f9636b171d413e1b467491885ee&req=dSIjEM95m4NYWvMW1HO4zQDpoXTJuPI9Dqivdj0BdNAuNceh8k2oJI%2FYZF7m%0A0imCJE09%2FiWFMFTv2aM%3D%0A)

Click "Set Up Shortcut," then you'll land on a screen like this:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246676517/456796f0fa34b42e7190bb63601f/trmnl-add-shortcut.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=8af5948d62b2a59476e5dcf19fc8a94843230d02c38ec3559115d91e6a61b749&req=dSIjEM95m4ReXvMW1HO4zYPSLAyuVWTZ1bemsHLR6AwPoUlquJTj7IRoav6i%0AvHRNhApwqRc2cS63TSE%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246676517/456796f0fa34b42e7190bb63601f/trmnl-add-shortcut.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=8af5948d62b2a59476e5dcf19fc8a94843230d02c38ec3559115d91e6a61b749&req=dSIjEM95m4ReXvMW1HO4zYPSLAyuVWTZ1bemsHLR6AwPoUlquJTj7IRoav6i%0AvHRNhApwqRc2cS63TSE%3D%0A)

In this blank text box, copy / paste your Private Plugin's UUID from inside your TRMNL account. This will not appear until you click Save (the end of Step 1 above).

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246677125/3f3aa4c130bfb3d174e2de518dd8/trmnl-plugin-uuid.png?expires=1743477300&signature=c8e25e3d555c9810333327c5547dba9579c0a0a15c9eca005cd6bfc4823e9333&req=dSIjEM95moBdXPMW1HO4zYwIqWYfsPD9L6855Ia7RfMAQsWCE2ysafFURIsP%0Al3JQWCJyUuJcuZMwQDI%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246677125/3f3aa4c130bfb3d174e2de518dd8/trmnl-plugin-uuid.png?expires=1743477300&signature=c8e25e3d555c9810333327c5547dba9579c0a0a15c9eca005cd6bfc4823e9333&req=dSIjEM95moBdXPMW1HO4zYwIqWYfsPD9L6855Ia7RfMAQsWCE2ysafFURIsP%0Al3JQWCJyUuJcuZMwQDI%3D%0A)

(**Tip**: if you're using an Apple computer to create the plugin, and your iPhone or iPad to create the Shortcut, then you can likely "copy" on your computer, then "paste" on your device, to avoid manually inputting this long string of characters)

Click "Add Shortcut" to finish adding the Shortcut template to your Apple device.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246679965/7d3b7fd890aaaba2e155cb54eb3f/view-trmnl-apple-shortcuts.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=2bce9129e10dad5d1548d5bd72622116a2db23ee9777cf7abc4cfdd9414728b7&req=dSIjEM95lIhZXPMW1HO4zR0oohsoWrqs8XIs%2BbOXFuypzQzJEjBpF%2FCNcwDt%0AaXVhQNwhDJ7IxcEXf68%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246679965/7d3b7fd890aaaba2e155cb54eb3f/view-trmnl-apple-shortcuts.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=2bce9129e10dad5d1548d5bd72622116a2db23ee9777cf7abc4cfdd9414728b7&req=dSIjEM95lIhZXPMW1HO4zR0oohsoWrqs8XIs%2BbOXFuypzQzJEjBpF%2FCNcwDt%0AaXVhQNwhDJ7IxcEXf68%3D%0A)

You may now view it from your Shortcuts dashboard and begin building custom logic.

Step 3 - Add functionality
--------------------------

Open your "TRMNL Starter Template" Shortcut on your Apple device by clicking the 3 dots in the top right corner of the widget. Optionally rename it by clicking the down arrow along the top of your screen.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246680456/01996f958739574113277803ce06/rename-trmnl-apple-shortcut.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=3fa988c0ac27406cc3553bdbd29b32f6169138ac34d7ae7f7a0920f46009ba82&req=dSIjEM92nYVaX%2FMW1HO4zeT53WVyMJjWOG%2Fn8qdcsK1jk%2FxiGAn7tQzpU0SL%0AFkbxuTqAhmep3pxZ%2BFg%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246680456/01996f958739574113277803ce06/rename-trmnl-apple-shortcut.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=3fa988c0ac27406cc3553bdbd29b32f6169138ac34d7ae7f7a0920f46009ba82&req=dSIjEM92nYVaX%2FMW1HO4zeT53WVyMJjWOG%2Fn8qdcsK1jk%2FxiGAn7tQzpU0SL%0AFkbxuTqAhmep3pxZ%2BFg%3D%0A)

In this tutorial we'll build a plugin that showcases random facts about dogs. The final result will look something like this:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1247409716/3024dbf3c499708a56c808e5ce3d/trmnl-dog-fact-plugin.jpeg?expires=1743477300&signature=5f98d4b4eb7bcae6fdb8e77a61702a9c199b4c04d7f70f84742f1e74dd3bd72b&req=dSIjEc1%2BlIZeX%2FMW1HO4zberskHIa%2B%2F6mmuD%2FvzceM8d9WeKUAT7Bm3Gteo0%0AkOjSXoixol19W6Pv8Hs%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1247409716/3024dbf3c499708a56c808e5ce3d/trmnl-dog-fact-plugin.jpeg?expires=1743477300&signature=5f98d4b4eb7bcae6fdb8e77a61702a9c199b4c04d7f70f84742f1e74dd3bd72b&req=dSIjEc1%2BlIZeX%2FMW1HO4zberskHIa%2B%2F6mmuD%2FvzceM8d9WeKUAT7Bm3Gteo0%0AkOjSXoixol19W6Pv8Hs%3D%0A)

  
In the bottom search bar, type "Get contents of" and select the "Get contents of URL" option.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246691764/da0484d6cd07e8531ba9e4e73dac/apple-shortcut-get-contents-of-url.png?expires=1743477300&signature=0e7f117683e0702dfe6745b3b29966752265b2286919519fc8b30ee6a83b3d43&req=dSIjEM93nIZZXfMW1HO4zRng6eBgKC%2FMy6NQF1ZWZqY8PeTRrHtq9powf0xo%0AEdQxSTxb%2B0W5Vacyo94%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246691764/da0484d6cd07e8531ba9e4e73dac/apple-shortcut-get-contents-of-url.png?expires=1743477300&signature=0e7f117683e0702dfe6745b3b29966752265b2286919519fc8b30ee6a83b3d43&req=dSIjEM93nIZZXfMW1HO4zRng6eBgKC%2FMy6NQF1ZWZqY8PeTRrHtq9powf0xo%0AEdQxSTxb%2B0W5Vacyo94%3D%0A)

This Shortcut step will be added to the bottom of your template. Hold it down with your finger or mouse and drag it up above the empty Dictionary step.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246700293/519e1db956668d67da5e01fa834c/trmnl-shortcut-get-contents-step.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=7d5da00475e245a937a8d0978621ffdfe46ba754ebed4b94243bbadb2d224a99&req=dSIjEM5%2BnYNWWvMW1HO4zVkwNBFp%2BBKLhqeG2q4aCYb3p8rhJenYrVU6O6e5%0ARMrnKpKsBR%2Bxj2k3gZI%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246700293/519e1db956668d67da5e01fa834c/trmnl-shortcut-get-contents-step.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=7d5da00475e245a937a8d0978621ffdfe46ba754ebed4b94243bbadb2d224a99&req=dSIjEM5%2BnYNWWvMW1HO4zVkwNBFp%2BBKLhqeG2q4aCYb3p8rhJenYrVU6O6e5%0ARMrnKpKsBR%2Bxj2k3gZI%3D%0A)

Click the placeholder "Url" icon, then "Clear variable," then input the following:

`https://dog-api.kinduff.com/api/facts`

Your Shortcut should now look like this:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246700475/2f906112c535c372145e8fdddd3a/trmnl-get-content-of-url.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=9c675c6e3f4094cb97ab75662e655e90532e6d876488ab3d7e966c7a9f6e7b55&req=dSIjEM5%2BnYVYXPMW1HO4zR4QZ7sZWTpjfGGxlNy1HZ9gsPANogR7VfoiP5Ik%0ARIziA8GMZ3SPz0EUHEQ%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246700475/2f906112c535c372145e8fdddd3a/trmnl-get-content-of-url.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=9c675c6e3f4094cb97ab75662e655e90532e6d876488ab3d7e966c7a9f6e7b55&req=dSIjEM5%2BnYVYXPMW1HO4zR4QZ7sZWTpjfGGxlNy1HZ9gsPANogR7VfoiP5Ik%0ARIziA8GMZ3SPz0EUHEQ%3D%0A)

If you click the play button on the bottom of your screen, Apple may ask you to approve access to open Chrome or another web browser. Select Yes.

You might see a new area populate with data, which in our case will be a random dog fact.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246701965/1255c1306c5820031f576439cd51/trmnl-apple-shortcut-get-dog-fact-api.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=1ddc71286df0dd7cb2fa33875e66732e8817047dacef31e66a888f96289a6ba0&req=dSIjEM5%2BnIhZXPMW1HO4zcA7VHbItSkkCH7y5bWFllCz6h04GApETIHnsLSq%0Au5cPq7Fc6aqi3gYr4sA%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246701965/1255c1306c5820031f576439cd51/trmnl-apple-shortcut-get-dog-fact-api.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=1ddc71286df0dd7cb2fa33875e66732e8817047dacef31e66a888f96289a6ba0&req=dSIjEM5%2BnIhZXPMW1HO4zcA7VHbItSkkCH7y5bWFllCz6h04GApETIHnsLSq%0Au5cPq7Fc6aqi3gYr4sA%3D%0A)

In our example above, Apple Shortcuts recommends a "next action" called Get Dictionary Value. Select this, or search for it in the bottom search bar if it does not automatically appear.

After adding a "Get Dictionary Value" step and dragging it below your "Get contents of" step added previously, change the step description to "Get Value for facts in Contents of URL."

Click the play icon again, and your screen should look like this:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246702443/2d47b7a85fb04cfee1a83c73338b/trmnl-apple-shortcut-get-single-dog-fact-value.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=19b28bc4c4a9262e87b14ff82c102c5d0cc644ab427349059f508d1bd069470b&req=dSIjEM5%2Bn4VbWvMW1HO4zcMn9l1%2FSKAbyGx%2B5yG2KRTGiWgPv%2FVrn36UYAgT%0A%2BYz5J%2FBrwqDL%2BpUZe1Q%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246702443/2d47b7a85fb04cfee1a83c73338b/trmnl-apple-shortcut-get-single-dog-fact-value.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=19b28bc4c4a9262e87b14ff82c102c5d0cc644ab427349059f508d1bd069470b&req=dSIjEM5%2Bn4VbWvMW1HO4zcMn9l1%2FSKAbyGx%2B5yG2KRTGiWgPv%2FVrn36UYAgT%0A%2BYz5J%2FBrwqDL%2BpUZe1Q%3D%0A)

Here we simply eliminated all the extra API data from the free Dog Facts tool, making a simple string of text that TRMNL can merge into a plugin design.

As a final step, input "dog\_fact" in the 'key' field of our previously empty Dictionary step. Then in the 'value' field on the right, select Dictionary Value from the list of available variables.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246711016/c270b920639ba3fc77a69ab087a4/trmnl-dictionary-key-value-setting.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=dbce7c3a0568e0a3a12f5e7281e630a3e4c03321970a72c8f6092270675021aa&req=dSIjEM5%2FnIFeX%2FMW1HO4zScTDwukrKVWLUi4%2BmDPezkYVfTYwTpD83BiDgey%0Ad3cJS9tfUjj0TbwN4eo%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246711016/c270b920639ba3fc77a69ab087a4/trmnl-dictionary-key-value-setting.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=dbce7c3a0568e0a3a12f5e7281e630a3e4c03321970a72c8f6092270675021aa&req=dSIjEM5%2FnIFeX%2FMW1HO4zScTDwukrKVWLUi4%2BmDPezkYVfTYwTpD83BiDgey%0Ad3cJS9tfUjj0TbwN4eo%3D%0A)

And that's it! Clicking the play button should now:

1.  fetch a random dog fact
    
2.  assign it to a variable called `dog_fact`
    
3.  nest the `dog_fact` value inside `merge_variables` (generated by the starter template)
    
4.  send the `merge_variables` content to your TRMNL private plugin
    

Here are the results of clicking the play button after following all the steps above:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246712488/1f6bd88b3f250c60f5c2f0ec14d0/trmnl-shortcut-success-response.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=b5db5ac6ee659fc17ced4a5f1b954bf6941f537ab7f0f64888cb1cbdf9c4fe36&req=dSIjEM5%2Fn4VXUfMW1HO4zT17LzujvDXG5Osao8TTjEPwv3wAz6WHlJORy744%0AMLUIxFEAKDgbYoMs%2BlA%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246712488/1f6bd88b3f250c60f5c2f0ec14d0/trmnl-shortcut-success-response.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=b5db5ac6ee659fc17ced4a5f1b954bf6941f537ab7f0f64888cb1cbdf9c4fe36&req=dSIjEM5%2Fn4VXUfMW1HO4zT17LzujvDXG5Osao8TTjEPwv3wAz6WHlJORy744%0AMLUIxFEAKDgbYoMs%2BlA%3D%0A)

If your Shortcut isn't working as expected, here is another Shortcut template with all of the steps above completed. You will just need to provide your Plugin UUID to connect it to your account, which is explained above in Step 2.

[https://www.icloud.com/shortcuts/e71f4f49f5764a328a6f8e104cc1a234](https://www.icloud.com/shortcuts/e71f4f49f5764a328a6f8e104cc1a234)

Step 4 - Design your plugin
---------------------------

Back inside your TRMNL account, click the "Edit Markup" button at the top of your private plugin's settings screen.

Copy/paste the content below into the "Full" tab code editor, which should be pre-selected:

<div class="layout layout--center">  
  <div class="layout layout--col">  
    <div class="b-h-gray-1">Did you know?</div>  
    {% if dog\_fact.size < 300 %}  
      <p class="value">{{dog\_fact}}</p>  
      {% else %}  
      <p class="value--small">{{dog\_fact}}</p>  
      {% endif %}  
  </div>  
</div>  
  
<div class="title\_bar">  
  <img class="image" src="https://img.icons8.com/dog" />  
  <span class="title">Dog Facts</span>  
</div>

Notice the use of `{{ dog_fact }}`, this is how we merge in our data from the Dog Facts API.

Next, return to the Shortcut you created on your Apple device. Click the play button. A dog fact will be fetched + sent to TRMNL.

  
Finally, inside TRMNL go back to your plugin settings screen from the link near the top:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246715134/150d734b8e2acf40242aa3cf288d/trmnl-back-to-plugin-settings.png?expires=1743477300&signature=bbdc3968aa5c7e0747ab4a072261648b8957d932087c902c3ad6e744a1da5cab&req=dSIjEM5%2FmIBcXfMW1HO4zVShJJysc7pqm2H8HXzc15ISqtiKvr2HXB9dpO0s%0Afh9ktyG4oQVnmMkxvSE%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246715134/150d734b8e2acf40242aa3cf288d/trmnl-back-to-plugin-settings.png?expires=1743477300&signature=bbdc3968aa5c7e0747ab4a072261648b8957d932087c902c3ad6e744a1da5cab&req=dSIjEM5%2FmIBcXfMW1HO4zVShJJysc7pqm2H8HXzc15ISqtiKvr2HXB9dpO0s%0Afh9ktyG4oQVnmMkxvSE%3D%0A)

Click Force Refresh, then wait a few seconds.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246715230/261f69a49a02922032128c61a2e5/trmnl-force-refresh-button.png?expires=1743477300&signature=a283e2df71fbf55825632f16eb03345d534e6102d59a375ed746c9c834940633&req=dSIjEM5%2FmINcWfMW1HO4zQOf%2F2Er5c79FbRKReHu8RB5o97FKPWz6a4XS7BV%0AGAnOvL0LMQ5vSXjQRS4%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246715230/261f69a49a02922032128c61a2e5/trmnl-force-refresh-button.png?expires=1743477300&signature=a283e2df71fbf55825632f16eb03345d534e6102d59a375ed746c9c834940633&req=dSIjEM5%2FmINcWfMW1HO4zQOf%2F2Er5c79FbRKReHu8RB5o97FKPWz6a4XS7BV%0AGAnOvL0LMQ5vSXjQRS4%3D%0A)

Refresh the web page in your browser and you should see a random dog fact:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246715335/7f4ed6757a9420f2986f3e33a9d8/trmnl-random-dog-fact-generated-screen.png?expires=1743477300&signature=d7136a32b768026b07e27431aeaf2294ee77167f6c787c48bb878079992c73dd&req=dSIjEM5%2FmIJcXPMW1HO4zZ1jEqBiLe7%2Fq8fTdA96QCsE1cdgikkETGR4WjW9%0AriYKyMK28tTV7O1pRGw%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246715335/7f4ed6757a9420f2986f3e33a9d8/trmnl-random-dog-fact-generated-screen.png?expires=1743477300&signature=d7136a32b768026b07e27431aeaf2294ee77167f6c787c48bb878079992c73dd&req=dSIjEM5%2FmIJcXPMW1HO4zZ1jEqBiLe7%2Fq8fTdA96QCsE1cdgikkETGR4WjW9%0AriYKyMK28tTV7O1pRGw%3D%0A)

Step 5 - Automate new plugin content
------------------------------------

Once you're happy with your Shortcut, head over to the Automation tab on your Shortcuts app.  
​

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246722102/f7d50782ab63b16e0814283e194b/trmnl-shortcut-automations-create.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=04dbcfbf6f3d69d5dd17ed398eac2e987534a1372a37b36e94a98a8586f3b3ff&req=dSIjEM58n4BfW%2FMW1HO4zVe%2B3KzIz3wu8Ash3awxzcQJU%2Bu7YZxP1qWJnmaG%0A%2B6WJRhSL%2FD4cqFSKKS8%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246722102/f7d50782ab63b16e0814283e194b/trmnl-shortcut-automations-create.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=04dbcfbf6f3d69d5dd17ed398eac2e987534a1372a37b36e94a98a8586f3b3ff&req=dSIjEM58n4BfW%2FMW1HO4zVe%2B3KzIz3wu8Ash3awxzcQJU%2Bu7YZxP1qWJnmaG%0A%2B6WJRhSL%2FD4cqFSKKS8%3D%0A)

Select "New Automation", then choose some logic for how often the automation should be executed. For example, youcould choose "Time of Day" and select "Daily", "10a."

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246722188/eeed571100a565e403ae3f46ca8c/trmnl-dog-fact-automation-10-am.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=8485a386d1637277142782ad308223c5e15b5866c97ebdb9497043b347cd721d&req=dSIjEM58n4BXUfMW1HO4zdgup7AjJRkByySKiFiykep5oUrrUWDURqu9fmrq%0A6OdZJ0EHCnxoDSNyPN4%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246722188/eeed571100a565e403ae3f46ca8c/trmnl-dog-fact-automation-10-am.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=8485a386d1637277142782ad308223c5e15b5866c97ebdb9497043b347cd721d&req=dSIjEM58n4BXUfMW1HO4zdgup7AjJRkByySKiFiykep5oUrrUWDURqu9fmrq%0A6OdZJ0EHCnxoDSNyPN4%3D%0A)

Select your "Dog Facts" Shortcut from the My Shortcuts section:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246722253/887b3bf1c45fcf7198d9bf4528f4/trmnl-dog-fact-automation-complete.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=19d0a42db5bf7c100996ddc828d08622180259af1bdc731555d2d41f013d9de6&req=dSIjEM58n4NaWvMW1HO4zeM71tZ7Mo5MfDoWnis60ESR%2FwlKtnKJEkgT8Dsn%0AI5DO1zYDb%2B6Nze%2BH%2Bf0%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246722253/887b3bf1c45fcf7198d9bf4528f4/trmnl-dog-fact-automation-complete.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=19d0a42db5bf7c100996ddc828d08622180259af1bdc731555d2d41f013d9de6&req=dSIjEM58n4NaWvMW1HO4zeM71tZ7Mo5MfDoWnis60ESR%2FwlKtnKJEkgT8Dsn%0AI5DO1zYDb%2B6Nze%2BH%2Bf0%3D%0A)

And you're done! A new dog fact will be generated on your TRMNL device every day at 10a. If you want more dog facts, just duplicate the automation at different times throughout the day.

Step 5 - Build more plugins
---------------------------

Phew! That was quite the process. Apple Shortcuts can be tricky at first, but once you get the hang of it, ~anything is possible.

For example, here is a custom Todo List plugin created by another TRMNL user:

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246716379/7577eef44a4fa70000b2d976fef3/trmnl-apple-shortcut-todo-list.png?expires=1743477300&signature=0f783707ac4efbf8643df9a0edcc92a7a0e091605cc2ac0c6c0c977576a31c18&req=dSIjEM5%2Fm4JYUPMW1HO4zaAzJPCysRV8bNVigxlRC4xEMRHHl4AGB6DO3d9z%0Ax2cr7rYrAx3xKTJgFvA%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246716379/7577eef44a4fa70000b2d976fef3/trmnl-apple-shortcut-todo-list.png?expires=1743477300&signature=0f783707ac4efbf8643df9a0edcc92a7a0e091605cc2ac0c6c0c977576a31c18&req=dSIjEM5%2Fm4JYUPMW1HO4zaAzJPCysRV8bNVigxlRC4xEMRHHl4AGB6DO3d9z%0Ax2cr7rYrAx3xKTJgFvA%3D%0A)

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246722430/7d8b5e2508a02e62033a182aab67/trmnl-todo-list-shortcut-plugin-render.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=18c34b45a3dd0658335c51ed4e8e2e7870e48146c482eb2fb94879f99c5f908b&req=dSIjEM58n4VcWfMW1HO4zZ7SqcIUd3X%2BQQn%2BOJKm2LYeVzMXXIIM9WlAaGg1%0A4nDFXbyU%2FkKcm91xlAE%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/v9ws3u2x/1246722430/7d8b5e2508a02e62033a182aab67/trmnl-todo-list-shortcut-plugin-render.jpg?expires=1743477300&signature=18c34b45a3dd0658335c51ed4e8e2e7870e48146c482eb2fb94879f99c5f908b&req=dSIjEM58n4VcWfMW1HO4zZ7SqcIUd3X%2BQQn%2BOJKm2LYeVzMXXIIM9WlAaGg1%0A4nDFXbyU%2FkKcm91xlAE%3D%0A)

How it works:

1.  open plugin from the iPhone's home page
    
2.  input a todo item
    
3.  send it to TRMNL
    
4.  display on device
    

Pretty cool, huh? We can't wait to see what you build.

Stay focused.

Did this answer your question?
